
-----title
永康 (出生地)
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年9月7日</a>　九月七日生于龙窟本宅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年</a>　在永康家居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1145&endYear=1145')">1145年</a>　在永康家居，弟充出生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1146&endYear=1146')">1146年</a>　在永康家居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1147&endYear=1147')">1147年</a>　在永康家居，一弟生，殇。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1148&endYear=1148')">1148年</a>　在永康家居，妹生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1149&endYear=1151')">1149-1151年</a>　在永康家居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1152&endYear=1152')">1152年</a>　闻行都有太学,读书山中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1153&endYear=1155')">1153-1155年</a>　家居，多读书山中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1156&endYear=1156')">1156年</a>　不自爱重，猖狂妄行，为乡里所不齿。数年间，祖父母教以读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1157&endYear=1157')">1157年</a>　永康家居读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1158&endYear=1158')">1158年</a>　从义乌何子刚读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1159&endYear=1159')">1159年</a>　学为语言，求以自见于世，凡世人之文章，无细巨必求观之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1160&endYear=1160')">1160年</a>　有经略四方之志。弟昭甫生，百日后归养张氏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1161&endYear=1161')">1161年</a>　考古人用兵成败之迹，著《酌古论》。郡守周葵得之，请为上客。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='82548801249f4874a97f1402fd62847b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("82548801249f4874a97f1402fd62847b");'><span id='82548801249f4874a97f1402fd62847b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1164')">1163-1164年</a>，21-22岁</div><div id='82548801249f4874a97f1402fd62847b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　由临安归永康。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1164&endYear=1164')">1164年</a>　居永康。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6b8f6e647d8a43a9b1f8835292031ba2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6b8f6e647d8a43a9b1f8835292031ba2");'><span id='6b8f6e647d8a43a9b1f8835292031ba2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1168')">1165-1168年</a>，23-26岁</div><div id='6b8f6e647d8a43a9b1f8835292031ba2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1165&endYear=1165')">1165年8月</a>　八月，母卒，居忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　纂《英豪录》，自序寄慨。作品：英豪录序。<div id='poem_1283496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>英豪录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283496")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283496_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283496'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283496'>今天子即位之初，虏再犯边，君忧臣劳，兵民死之，而财用匮焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283496_comment'></div>距靖康之祸于是四十载矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283496_comment'></div>虽其中间尝息于和，而养安之患滋大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283496_comment'></div>踵而为之，患犹昔也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283496_comment'></div>起而决之，则又惮乎力之不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283496_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283496_comment'></div>事势之极，其难处非一日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283496_comment'></div>蔡谟有言：「创业之事，苟非上圣，必由英豪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283496_comment'></div>今上既圣矣，而英豪之士阙乎未有闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283496_comment'></div>余甚惑焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283496_comment'></div>夫天下有大变，功名之机也，抚其机而不有人以制之，岂大变终已不得平乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283496_comment'></div>此非天意也，顾天实生之，而人不知所用耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283496_comment'></div>彼英豪者，非即人以求用者也，宁不用死耳，而少贬焉不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283496_comment'></div>故饥寒迫于身，视天下犹吾事也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283496_comment'></div>见易于庸人，谓强敌可剿也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283496_comment'></div>信口而言，惟意之为，礼法之不可羁也，死生祸福之不能惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283496_comment'></div>一有事焉，君子小人，一见而得其情；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283496_comment'></div>是非利害之间，一言而决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283496_comment'></div>理繁剧则庖丁之解牛也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283496_comment'></div>处危疑则匠石之斲鼻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283496_comment'></div>盖其才智过人者远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283496_comment'></div>然而旅出旅处，而混于不可知之间，媢之者谓狂，而实狂者又偶似之，将特自标树，则夫虚张以求贾者又得而误之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283496_comment'></div>此英豪之所以困而不达，而谓无人焉者非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283496_comment'></div>嗟夫，承平之时，展才无所不用，职也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283496_comment'></div>而困于艰难之际者，独何欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283496_comment'></div>且上之人亦过矣，独不可策之以言而试之以事乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283496_comment'></div>虽商、周之于伊、吕，不废也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283496_comment'></div>废之而不务，而忧无人焉者，亦非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283496_comment'></div>抑余闻之：昔人有以千金求千里马者，不得，则以五百金买其骨焉，不踰期而千里马至者三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283496_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283496_comment'></div>趋其所好，人之情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283496_comment'></div>不得于生者，见其骨犹贵之，可谓诚好之矣，生者之思奋，固也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283496_comment'></div>故余备录古之英豪之行事，以当千里马之骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283496_comment'></div>诚想其遗风以求之，今未必不有得也，顾其诚好不耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283496_comment'></div>盖晋武帝称「安得诸葛亮者而与之共治」，正使九原可作，盍亦思所以用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283496_comment'></div>凡余所以区区于此录者，夫岂徒哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283496_comment'></div>夫岂徒哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1283496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　《中兴遗传》纂成，有序。作品：中兴遗传序。<div id='poem_1283497' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283497' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283497?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中兴遗传序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283497")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283497_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283497'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283497'>初，龙可伯康游京师，辈饮市肆，方叫呼大噱，赵九龄次张旁行过之，雅与伯康不相识，俄追止次张，牵其臂，迫与共饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283497_comment'></div>次张之父时守官河东，方以疾闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283497_comment'></div>次张以实告，伯康曰：「毋苦！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283497_comment'></div>乃翁疾行瘳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283497_comment'></div>子可人意者，为我姑少留」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283497_comment'></div>次张不得已从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283497_comment'></div>箕踞笑歌，恢谐纵谑，旁若无人，次张固已心异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283497_comment'></div>一日行城外，过麻村，观大阅之所，伯康勃然曰：「子亦喜射乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283497_comment'></div>次张曰：「颇亦好之，而不能精也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283497_comment'></div>伯康曰：「姑试之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283497_comment'></div>次张从旁取弓挟矢以兴，十发而贴中者六七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283497_comment'></div>次张心颇自喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283497_comment'></div>伯康拾矢而射，一发中的，矢矢相属，十发亡一差者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283497_comment'></div>次张惊曰：「子射至此乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283497_comment'></div>伯康曰：「此亦何足道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283497_comment'></div>千军万马，头目转动不常，意之所指，犹望必中，况此定的，又何怪乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283497_comment'></div>次张吐其舌不能收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283497_comment'></div>俄指其地而谓次张曰：「后三年，此间皆胡人，子姑识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283497_comment'></div>火龙骑日，飞雪满天，此京城破日之兆」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283497_comment'></div>因嘻吁长叹，不能自禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283497_comment'></div>后三年，京城失守，其言皆验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283497_comment'></div>中原流离，伯康自是不复见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283497_comment'></div>岂丧乱之际，或死于兵，抑有所奋而不能成也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283497_comment'></div>次张每念其人，言则叹惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283497_comment'></div>绍兴初，韩世忠拒虏于淮西，力颇不敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283497_comment'></div>次张献言：「乞决淮西之水以灌虏营」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283497_comment'></div>朝廷易其言而不之信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283497_comment'></div>已而虏师俄退，世忠力请留战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283497_comment'></div>虏酋使谓曰：「闻南朝欲决水以灌我营，我岂能落人计中」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283497_comment'></div>次张言虽不用，犹足以攻敌人之心者类如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283497_comment'></div>次张尝为李丞相所辟，得承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283497_comment'></div>督府罢，次张亦径归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283497_comment'></div>大驾南渡，次张侨居阳羡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283497_comment'></div>故将岳飞尝隶丞相军中，次张识其人于行伍，言之丞相，给帖补军校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283497_comment'></div>后为统制，遇大驾巡永嘉，与诸将彷徨江上，莫知攸适；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283497_comment'></div>又乏粮，将谋抄掠，次张闻而竟往，说飞移军阳羡，州给之食，飞得无他，而州境赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283497_comment'></div>人有言次张生平于赵丞相者，丞相喜，欲用之，复有谮者曰：「此人心志不可保，使其得志，必为曹操」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283497_comment'></div>丞相疑沮而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283497_comment'></div>次张度时不用，屏居不出，竟死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283497_comment'></div>昔参政周公葵屡为余言其人，且曰：「我尝荐之朝廷，诸公皆诘我：『子端人正士，胡为喜言此等狂生』？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283497_comment'></div>我因告之曰：『吾侪平居谭王道，说《诗》《书》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283497_comment'></div>一日得用，从容庙朝，执持纪纲可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283497_comment'></div>至于排难解纷，仓卒万变，此等殆不可少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283497_comment'></div>吾侪既不能办，而恶他人之能办，是诬天下以无士，而期国事之必不成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283497_comment'></div>是乌可哉』」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283497_comment'></div>余尝大周公之言，异二生之为人而惜其屈，尝欲传其事而不能详，因叹曰：「世之豪伟倜傥之士，沈没于困穷，不能自奋以为世用，欲用而卒沮于疑忌，如二生者宁有限哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283497_comment'></div>然自古乱离战争之际，往往奇才辈出，崭然自赴功名之会，如建炎、绍兴之间，诚亦不少，虽或屈而不用，用不大，大或不终，未四十年，已有不能道其姓字者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283497_comment'></div>记事之文，可少乎哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283497_comment'></div>自是始欲纂集异闻，为《中兴遗传》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283497_comment'></div>然犹恨闻见单寡，欲从先生故老详求其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283497_comment'></div>故先为之纂例，而以渐足之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283497_comment'></div>其一曰大臣，若李纲、宗泽、吕颐浩、赵鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283497_comment'></div>其二曰大将，若种师道、岳飞、韩世忠、吴玠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1283497_comment'></div>其三曰死节，若李若水、刘韐、孙傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1283497_comment'></div>其四曰死事，若种师中、王禀、徐徽言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1283497_comment'></div>其五曰能臣，若陈则、程昌禹、郑刚中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1283497_comment'></div>其六曰能将，若曲端、姚端、王胜、刘锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1283497_comment'></div>其七曰直士，若陈东、欧阳澈、吴若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1283497_comment'></div>其八曰侠士，若王友、张所、刘位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1283497_comment'></div>其九曰辩士，若邵公序、祝子权、汪若海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1283497_comment'></div>其十曰义勇，若孙韩、葛进、石竧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1283497_comment'></div>其十一曰群盗，若李胜、杨进、丁进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1283497_comment'></div>其十二曰贼臣，若徐秉哲、王时雍、范琼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1283497_comment'></div>合十二门而分传之，总目曰《中兴遗传》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1283497_comment'></div>聊以发其行事，而致吾之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1283497_comment'></div>然其端则起于惜二生之失其传，故序首及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1283497_comment'></div>昔司马子长周游四方，纂集旧闻，为《史记》一百三十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1283497_comment'></div>其文驰骋万变，使观者壮心骇目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1283497_comment'></div>顾余何人，岂能使人喜观吾文如子长哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1283497_comment'></div>方将旁求广集，以备史氏之阙遗云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_69_1283497_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　父因事入狱，祖父母忧思成疾，奔走营救。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1166&endYear=1166')">1166年</a>　作史传序。作品：谋臣传序。忠臣传序。高士传序。辩士传序。义士传序。<div id='poem_1283494' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283494' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283494?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谋臣传序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283494")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283494_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283494'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283494'>昔尧舜之际专尚德化，三代之王以仁政，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283494", 1283494, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>伯国</span>以谋，战国以力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283494_comment'></div>始乱之不同，所从来异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283494_comment'></div>由汉迄今，有国家者始兼而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283494_comment'></div>然德化之与仁义，皆人主之躬行者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283494_comment'></div>至于排难解纷，则岂可不以谋，而力乌用哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283494_comment'></div>此权智之士所以为可贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283494_comment'></div>虽然，权智可贵矣，行之以谲，则事以办，亦或以否，否必不可继也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283494_comment'></div>故君子行权于正，用智以理，若庖丁之解牛，是以智不劳而事迎解，功已成而无后患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283494_comment'></div>盖五常之用，智为难，仁、义、礼、信，过则近厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283494_comment'></div>过于智，贼矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283494_comment'></div>故凡列国之策士，皆行穿窬，而衣人之衣以自齿于编民者也，此不足论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283494_comment'></div>论汉以来智而不贼者，然亦无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283494_comment'></div>故身名俱全惟张子房，他皆不逮已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283494_comment'></div>要以排难解纷，故不得而举少之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283494_comment'></div>虽然，事固有幸不幸，遇左马之笔，则片谋寸长，声迹焜灼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283494_comment'></div>史笔中绝，虽有奇谋至计，类郁而弗耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283494_comment'></div>余甚慨焉，故将章列其行事，以备谋国者之览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283494_comment'></div>乃取太史迁之所尝载者，若张陈之徒，标于卷首；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283494_comment'></div>其他删次论列，惟意之从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283494_comment'></div>合而曰《谋臣传》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283494_comment'></div>其奇可资以集事，其贼可以戒，不为无取云耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1283494_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283492' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283492' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283492?labeling=true' target='_blank'>忠臣传序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283492")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283492_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283492'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283492'>余读书至武庚之事，何尝不为之流涕哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283492_comment'></div>嗟夫，忠孝者，立身之大节，为臣而洗君之耻，父雠而子复之，人之至情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283492_comment'></div>度不可为，不顾而为之者，抑吾之情不可不伸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283492_comment'></div>逆计而不为，人乌知吾心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283492_comment'></div>生犹愧耳，况卒不免于死，则将藉口谓何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283492_comment'></div>夫武王之伐纣也，以至仁顺天命，以大义拯斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283492_comment'></div>然君父不以无道贬尊，则武庚视<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1283492", 1283492, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>太白</span>之旗，必有大不忍于此者，然而未即死者，犹有待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283492_comment'></div>及武王既立而没，嗣子幼，君臣兄弟之间疑间方兴，故将挟管蔡之隙以义起，成败之不问，姑明吾心，奋而为之，是以殒首而不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283492_comment'></div>余以为武庚者，古之忠臣孝子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283492_comment'></div>世立是非于成败，故无褒，而孔氏又讳而不道，然则武庚之死越二千载，目之瞑未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283492_comment'></div>虽然，武庚受之嫡嗣，处义之必不可已，而非有深计于后世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283492_comment'></div>若翟义、王淩、毌丘俭、诸葛诞之徒，非清议之所必责，俛首相随属，未过也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283492_comment'></div>而数子者，忠胆愤发，视其国之倾、身之危，不啻不暇熟权其力，趣起扶之，意虽不就，此其心可诬也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283492_comment'></div>作史者谓宜大书以示劝，乃惟旅次之，然且不免不量之讥，甚遂传之《叛臣》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283492_comment'></div>语曰：「盖棺论乃定」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283492_comment'></div>是果可信乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283492_comment'></div>昔者贯高有言：「人情岂不各爱其父母妻子乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283492_comment'></div>今吾三族皆已论死，顾岂以王易吾亲哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283492_comment'></div>然则数子之心壮矣，乃其冤有甚于武庚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283492_comment'></div>余悲之，故列为《忠臣传》，信千古以兴颓俗，此圣人惩劝之法也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1283492_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高士传序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283491")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283491'>三代尚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283491_comment'></div>士之生乎其时者，习有常业，仕有定时，利不能更其所守，而不以名汩其真，养性以安命，修道以成德，教化之渐使然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283491_comment'></div>即不类不齿，《诗序》曰：「人人有士君子之行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283491_comment'></div>当此之时，士亦乌知其为高哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283491_comment'></div>周泽既衰，异端并起，所以贼其良心者厥端非一，士之能固其所守，艰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283491_comment'></div>然颜闵之徒终身陋巷，朝不及夕，蔬食以自如，鼓琴以自娱，视天下之乐举无以易此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283491_comment'></div>或曰：「贫则无用，无用则无累，无累则乐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283491_comment'></div>余以为二子者岂诚有乐于贫贱哉，由其道虽富贵可也，彼其所乐者在此而不在彼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283491_comment'></div>贫贱者人之所恶，二子何好焉，而富贵又何累？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283491_comment'></div>故曰：「穷亦乐，通亦乐」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283491_comment'></div>又曰：「无入而不自得」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283491_comment'></div>由此言之，彼其心岂有徇于外，亦岂必后世之知我哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283491_comment'></div>惟其屹然立于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1283491", 1283491, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>颓波</span>靡俗之中，可以为高矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283491_comment'></div>故世之言二子者，往往尊于王公，而王公亦荣于见齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283491_comment'></div>则夫苟一时者，是果何得哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283491_comment'></div>故自颜闵以来，若四皓、严光、黄宪、徐稚之流，皆其信道之至者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283491_comment'></div>平时不言而人化之，虽不遇，犹玉之在山，其光辉已不可掩，迫之而小应，已与夫汲汲然愿为之者异矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283491_comment'></div>令其遇时行道以正风俗，岂不犹反手哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283491_comment'></div>余历观诸史，见若此者，窃有慕焉，而恨当时之自閟于山林者，史不得而尽载也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283491_comment'></div>幸其犹或载也，总而为《高士传》，以备日览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283491_comment'></div>谚曰：「非尔之高，我之下也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283491_comment'></div>将与学者尽心焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1283491_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辩士传序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283495")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283495'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283495'>古者兵兴，使在其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283495_comment'></div>夫使也者，所以通两国之情，释仇而约，易憾而欢者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283495_comment'></div>彼古人之用兵，非以为得已也，使而不失辞，两国之民实赖之，顾亦何恶哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283495_comment'></div>孔子曰：「诵《诗》三百，使于四方，不能专对，虽多亦奚以为」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283495_comment'></div>盖曲尽人情者莫如《诗》，达乎《诗》而使，则道之以义，开之以理，广譬而约喻，用能曲尽人情，事无有不集者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283495_comment'></div>然则古者之使，本乎曲尽人情，纷挐之辩不贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283495_comment'></div>及至列国之际，强弱之相形，众寡之相倾，一时鲜廉寡耻之徒往来乎其间，摇吻鼓舌，劫之以势，诱之以利，怒之以其所甚辱，趋之以其所甚欲，捭阖而钳制之，以苟一时之成事者，此无异于白昼而攫者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283495_comment'></div>盖其原起于鬼谷子，而成于仪秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283495_comment'></div>当是时也，相师成风，其习已胶而不可解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283495_comment'></div>世之所谓有道之士，若孟、荀、庄周，其立言论事，犹时有辩士之风，要其归以正，是以无讥焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283495_comment'></div>汉兴，郦、陆、侯、随辈皆有辩闻，然嗜利无耻，不问理道之习，亦少衰矣，以比古之贤使，诚为有间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283495_comment'></div>至其辨析利害，切见事情，彼乌可废哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283495_comment'></div>由数子以降，士之肆伟辩以济人之事者，不可胜数，厥迹之著，阙然有愧，史氏之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283495_comment'></div>故余录其可采者，为《辩士传》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283495_comment'></div>又为叙古今使者之所以异而首之，俾奉命行者有考焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1283495_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283493' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283493' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283493?labeling=true' target='_blank'>义士传序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1166年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283493")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283493_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283493'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283493'>昔三代之王也，贤圣之君商为多：敷政出令，不拂民欲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283493_comment'></div>惇德行化，以固民心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283493_comment'></div>虽纣之暴，而民未厌商也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283493_comment'></div>故文王抑畏以全至德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283493_comment'></div>孔子曰：「三分天下有其二，以服事殷」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283493_comment'></div>岂不大哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283493_comment'></div>至武王，不忍天下之乱而卒废之，虽违商而周者十室而八，然商之馀民，眷念先王之旧泽，执义以自守，虽谆复喻之，嚣乎其不肯顺从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283493_comment'></div>而周家卒不敢以刑罚驱之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283493_comment'></div>不惟不敢，亦其心有所愧而不忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283493_comment'></div>故惟遵商之旧政以渐服其心，历三世而后帖然从周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283493_comment'></div>推此之时，稚者已壮，壮者已老，老者已死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283493_comment'></div>耆旧强壮之民卒不肯从，而从之者皆生长于周之民也，可不谓义乎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283493_comment'></div>然犹见称「顽民」，则周人之言也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283493_comment'></div>于商义矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283493_comment'></div>夫伯夷、叔齐，孔子以为义而许之，而商民之事，亦详见于《书》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283493_comment'></div>夷齐是，则商民不非矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283493_comment'></div>夫夷、齐非以一死为足以存商，明君臣之义，虽有圣者不可易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283493_comment'></div>商民非以不肯顺从为足以拒周，顾先王之德泽有以使之，而弗克自已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283493_comment'></div>夫义者，立人之大节；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283493_comment'></div>而爱生惮死，人之情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283493_comment'></div>其不以此而易彼者，诚知所处矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283493_comment'></div>由商而降，惟东汉之治，惇节义，尚廉退，有商之遗风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283493_comment'></div>故其亡也，义士亦略如之，然亦可以为流涕也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283493_comment'></div>若夫王蠋、申包胥之伦，皆非有所激而兴，故特行其志，而从之者不众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283493_comment'></div>然使夫人气沮而胆褫，则其功效岂少哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283493_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283493_comment'></div>商远矣，其民之姓氏不得详也，故序存之，而传夷、齐以为义士首，于东汉之士加详焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283493_comment'></div>其他特起者附之，庶乎有闻风而兴者，岂徒补观览而已哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1283493_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年7月</a>　七月，祖母卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1167&endYear=1167')">1167年12月27日</a>　十二月二十七日，祖父卒。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年4月12日</a>　经叶衡援助，其父于四月十二日出狱，父子团乐，喜甚至泣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1168&endYear=1168')">1168年9月</a>　易名为亮。首贡于乡，录为太学生员。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4bf0ca9db7284a8096c62c82b6afa8f8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4bf0ca9db7284a8096c62c82b6afa8f8");'><span id='4bf0ca9db7284a8096c62c82b6afa8f8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>，27岁</div><div id='4bf0ca9db7284a8096c62c82b6afa8f8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　归休于家，杜门读书，学者多归之。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8e11773cc547497c8bc64d87d2f2e89a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8e11773cc547497c8bc64d87d2f2e89a");'><span id='8e11773cc547497c8bc64d87d2f2e89a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1172')">1170-1172年</a>，28-30岁</div><div id='8e11773cc547497c8bc64d87d2f2e89a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　秋，去临安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1171&endYear=1171')">1171年</a>　嫁妹。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　是岁，始下帷授业，作经书发题以教学者。作品：周礼发题。<div id='poem_1283557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>六经发题<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>周礼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283557")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283557'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283557'>《周礼》一书，先王之遗制具在，吾夫子盖叹其郁郁之文，而知天地之功莫备于此，后有圣人，不能加毫末于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283557_comment'></div>世儒之论以为：治至于周公而术已穷，穷则不可以复，继周之后必为秦，吾夫子盖逆知之而不言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283557_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283557_comment'></div>果其穷也，则周公之志荒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283557_comment'></div>自伏羲、神农、黄帝以来，顺风气之宜而因时制法，凡所以为人道立极，而非有私天下之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283557_comment'></div>盖至于周公，集百圣之大成，文理密察，累累乎如贯珠，井井乎如画棋局，曲而当，尽而不污，无复一毫之间，而人道备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283557_comment'></div>人道备，则足以周天下之理，而通天下之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283557_comment'></div>变通之理具在，周公之道盖至此而与天地同流，而忧其穷哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283557_comment'></div>夫周家之制既定，而上下维持至于八百馀年，诸侯既已擅立，周之王徒拥其虚器，蕞然立于诸侯之上，诸侯皆相顾而莫之或废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283557_comment'></div>彼独何畏而未忍哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283557_comment'></div>岂非周公之制有以维持其不忍之心，虽颠倒错乱而犹未亡也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283557_comment'></div>当是之时，周虽自绝于天，有能变通周公之制而行之，天下不必周，而周公之术盖未始穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283557_comment'></div>秦徒见其得天下之难，以为周公之制盖非其所便，并与夫仅存者而尽弃之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283557_comment'></div>而不知周家之制既尽，而秦亦亡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283557_comment'></div>人道废，则其君岂能独存哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283557_comment'></div>始夫子之言曰：「其或继周者，虽百世可知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283557_comment'></div>盖以为后之王者必因周而损益焉，自是变通，至于百世而不穷，而岂知其至此极也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283557_comment'></div>汉高帝崛起草莽而得天下，知天下厌秦之苛，思有息肩之所，故其君臣相与因陋就简，存宽大之意，而为汉家之制，民亦以是安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283557_comment'></div>而汉祚灵长，绝而复续者，几与夏、商等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283557_comment'></div>自是功利苟且之政习以为常，先王不易之制弃而不讲，人极之不亡者几希矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283557_comment'></div>此有志之士所以抱遗书而兴百世之叹，反覆推究，而冀其复见天地之大全也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283557_comment'></div>然自秦火之馀，此书已非其全，而驳乱不经之言，盖如黑白之不相入，尚可考而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283557_comment'></div>虽然，文武之政布在方册，其人存则其政举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283557_comment'></div>自周之衰以迄于今，盖千五百馀年矣，天独未厌于斯乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283557_comment'></div>故将与诸君参考同异以有待焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1283557_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　下帷授业，作经书发题以教学者。作品：春秋发题。书经发题。诗经发题。论语发题。孟子发题。<div id='poem_1283559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>六经发题<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>春秋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283559")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283559'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283559'>圣人之于天下也，未尝作也，而有述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283559_comment'></div>近世儒者有言：「述之者，天也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283559_comment'></div>作之者，人也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283559_comment'></div>《诗》、《书》、《礼》、《乐》，吾夫子之所以述也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283559_comment'></div>至于《春秋》，其文则鲁史之旧，其详则天子诸侯之行事，其义则天子之所以奉若天道者，而孔子何作焉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283559_comment'></div>孟子之所谓作者，犹曰「整齐其文」云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283559_comment'></div>世儒遂以为《春秋》孔子所自作，笔则笔，削则削，虽游夏不能赞一辞于其间，言其义圣人之所独得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283559_comment'></div>信斯言也，则《春秋》其孔氏之书乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283559_comment'></div>夫《春秋》，天子之事也，圣人以匹夫而与天子之事，此王法之所当正也，不能自逃于王法而能正人乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283559_comment'></div>乱臣贼子其有辞矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283559_comment'></div>夫赏，天命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283559_comment'></div>罚，天讨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283559_comment'></div>天子，奉天而行者也，赏罚而一毫不得其当，是慢天也，慢而至于颠倒错乱，则天道灭矣，灭天道，则为自绝于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283559_comment'></div>夫子，周之民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283559_comment'></div>伤周之自绝于天，而不忍文武之业遂坠于地也，取鲁史之旧文，因天子诸侯之行事而一正之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283559_comment'></div>赏不违乎天命，罚不违乎天讨，犹曰：此周天子之所以奉乎天者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283559_comment'></div>或去天称王，或宰以名见，犹曰：此周天子之所以自赎乎天者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283559_comment'></div>天之道不亡，则周不为自绝于天；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283559_comment'></div>周不为自绝于天，则天下犹有王也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283559_comment'></div>天下有王，而乱臣贼子安得不惧乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283559_comment'></div>然则《春秋》者，周天子之书也，而夫子何与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283559_comment'></div>或曰：「《春秋》而系之以鲁，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283559_comment'></div>曰：「天下有王，凡诸侯之国之所记载，独非天子之事乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283559_comment'></div>而况鲁，周之宗国，其事可得而详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283559_comment'></div>夫子曰：「如有用我者，吾其为东周乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283559_comment'></div>此夫子之志，《春秋》之所由作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283559_comment'></div>是以尽事物之情，达时措之宜，正以等之，恕以通之，直而行之，曲而畅之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283559_comment'></div>其名是也，其实非也，则文与而实不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283559_comment'></div>其心然也，其事异也，则诛其事而达其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283559_comment'></div>微显阐幽，谨严宽裕，如天之称物平施，如阴阳之并行不悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283559_comment'></div>文、武、周公之政所以曲当乎人心者也，而谓《春秋》孔子之所自作，宜非亮之所敢知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283559_comment'></div>《春秋》所书，无往而非天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283559_comment'></div>学者以人而视《春秋》，而谓有得于圣人之意者，非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283559_comment'></div>故将与诸君以天下之公而观之，毋以一人之私而观之，辞达而义畅，庶乎可以窥天道之全也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1283559_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283555' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283555?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283555'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283555'>昔者圣人以道揆古今之变，取其概于道者百篇，而垂万世之训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283555_comment'></div>其文理密察，本末具举，盖有待于后之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283555_comment'></div>而经生分篇析句之学，其何足以知此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283555_comment'></div>亮也何人，而敢议此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283555_comment'></div>盖将与诸君共学焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283555_comment'></div>夫盈宇宙者无非物，日用之间无非事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283555_comment'></div>古之帝王独明于事物之故，发言立政，顺民之心，因时之宜，处其常而不惰，遇其变而天下安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283555_comment'></div>今载之《书》者皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283555_comment'></div>要之，文理密察之功用，至于尧而后无慊诸圣人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283555_comment'></div>是以断诸《尧典》而无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283555_comment'></div>由是言之，删《书》者非圣人之意也，天下之公也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1283555_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283556' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283556' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283556?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283556_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283556'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283556'>道之在天下，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283556", 1283556, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>平施</span>于日用之间，得其性情之正者，彼固有以知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283556_comment'></div>当先王时，天下之人，其发乎情，止乎礼义，盖有不知其然而然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283556_comment'></div>先王既远，民情之流也久矣，而其所谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283556", 1283556, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>平施</span>于日用之间者，与生俱生，固不可得而离也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283556_comment'></div>是以既流之情，易发之言，而天下亦不自知其何若，而圣人于其间有取焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283556_comment'></div>抑不独先王之泽也，圣人之于《诗》，固将使天下复性情之正，而得其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1283556", 1283556, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>平施</span>于日用之间者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283556_comment'></div>乃区区于章句、训诂之末，岂圣人之心也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283556_comment'></div>孔子曰：「兴于《诗」》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283556_comment'></div>章句、训诂亦足以兴乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283556_comment'></div>愿比诸君求其所以兴者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1283556_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>语孟发题<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>论语</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283560")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283560'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283560'>《论语》一书，无非下学之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283560_comment'></div>学者求其上达之说而不得，则取其言之若微妙者玩而索之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283560_comment'></div>意生见长，又从而为之辞曰：「此精也，彼特其粗耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283560_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283560_comment'></div>此其所以终身读之而堕于榛莽之中，而犹自谓其有得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283560_comment'></div>夫道之在天下，无本末，无内外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283560_comment'></div>圣人之言，乌有举其一而遗其一者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283560_comment'></div>举其一而遗其一，则是圣人犹与道为二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283560_comment'></div>然则《论语》之书，若之何而读之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283560_comment'></div>曰：用明于内，汲汲于下学，而求其心之所同然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283560_comment'></div>功深力到，则他日之上达，无非今日之下学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283560_comment'></div>于是而读《论语》之书，必知通体而好之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283560_comment'></div>亮于此书，固终身之所愿学者，方将与诸君商榷其所向而戒涂焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1283560_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283561' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283561?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>孟子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283561'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283561'>昔先儒有言：「公则一，私则万殊」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283561_comment'></div>人心不同，如其面焉，此私心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283561_comment'></div>呜呼，私心一萌，而吾不知其所终穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283561_comment'></div>先王之时，礼达分定，而心有所止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283561_comment'></div>故天下之人各识其本心，亲其亲而亲人之亲，子其子而子人之子，其本心未尝不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283561_comment'></div>周道衰而王泽竭，利害兴而人心动，计较作于中，思虑营于外，其始将计其便安，而其终至于争夺诛杀，毒流四海而未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283561_comment'></div>孟子生于是时，悯天下之至此极，谓其流不可胜救，惟人心一正，则各循其本，而天下定矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283561_comment'></div>况其势已穷而将变，变而通之，何啻反掌之易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283561_comment'></div>孟子知其理之甚速，而时君方以为迂，吾是以知非斯道之难行，而人心之难正也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283561_comment'></div>故善观孟子之书者，当知其主于正人心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283561_comment'></div>而求正人心之说者，当知其严义利之辨于毫釐之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283561_comment'></div>尝试与诸君共之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1283561_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a77e7995f4a84c14b941914331ba2d3c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a77e7995f4a84c14b941914331ba2d3c");'><span id='a77e7995f4a84c14b941914331ba2d3c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1176')">1172-1176年</a>，30-34岁</div><div id='a77e7995f4a84c14b941914331ba2d3c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　立保社，以资研究。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　与应仲实书辟佛说。<div id='poem_1283429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与应仲实<span class='inlineComment2'>（孟明）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283429")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283429_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283429'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283429'>与仲实别，于今八年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283429_comment'></div>祸患奔走，自分死生不相闻知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283429_comment'></div>既而适有天幸，遂得比数于人，然犹于故旧之书阙然不讲，几若自外于门下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283429_comment'></div>重惟少之时，猖狂妄行，乡闾所不齿，仲实以儒先生抚摩煦饫，若昆弟朋友；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283429_comment'></div>虽识者亦有不择交之疑，而仲实不顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283429_comment'></div>困苦之馀，百念灰冷，视前事已若隔世，洗心涤虑，谓可以承君子之教矣，而八年之间，话言不接，吉凶不相问吊，反有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1283429", 1283429, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>白头如新</span>之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283429_comment'></div>退而求之，敢逃其责！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283429_comment'></div>去年秋，群试监中，有司以为不肖，始决意为息肩弛担之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283429_comment'></div>所居僻左，有疑孰问？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283429_comment'></div>恃仲实辈人在尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283429_comment'></div>方图缓步造谒，遇仲实有行都之役，逡巡数月，遂闻新除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283429_comment'></div>官况绝佳，职事简少，儒先生雅宜处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283429_comment'></div>斯道之伸，此其权舆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283429_comment'></div>喜甚至于不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283429_comment'></div>前月末，始闻来归，暑溽如许，不敢辄诣斋阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283429_comment'></div>又思此别相见定何时，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1283429", 1283429, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>进退首鼠</span>，卒以其所欲求正于仲实者而寓之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283429_comment'></div>亮两年来，方悟孟子所谓「人之所以异于禽兽者几希」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283429_comment'></div>仁于我何常之有，朝可夷而暮可蹠也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283429_comment'></div>不仁于我亦何常之有，朝可蹠而暮可夷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283429_comment'></div>「惟圣罔念作狂，惟狂克念作圣」，非圣人姑为是训；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283429_comment'></div>「无若丹朱傲，无若受之酗于酒」，亦非独忧治世而危明主；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283429_comment'></div>人心无常，果如是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283429_comment'></div>曾子曰：「战战兢兢，如临深渊，如履薄冰，今而后吾知免夫，小子」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283429_comment'></div>子张曰：「君子曰终，小人曰死，吾今日其庶几乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283429_comment'></div>古之贤者，其自危盖如此，此所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1283429", 1283429, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>不愧屋漏</span>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1283429", 1283429, "Clauses/76/Comments/1")'>心广体胖</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283429_comment'></div>世之学者，玩心于无形之表，以为卓然而有见，事物虽众，此其得之浅者，不过如枯木死灰而止耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283429_comment'></div>得之深者，纵横妙用，肆而不约，安知所谓文理密察之道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283429_comment'></div>泛乎中流，无所底止，犹自谓其有得，岂不可哀也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283429_comment'></div>故格物致知之学，圣人所以惓惓于天下后世，言之而无隐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283429_comment'></div>夫道之在天下，何物非道，千涂万辙，因事作则，苟能潜心玩省，于所已发处体认，则知「夫子之道，忠恕而已」非设辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283429_comment'></div>亮少不自力，放其心而不知求；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283429_comment'></div>行年三十，始知此事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283429_comment'></div>日用之间，颠倒错紊，如理乱丝，更无着手处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283429_comment'></div>日复一日，终不免于自弃，不识仲实其何以救之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283429_comment'></div>近作十篇，往求檃括，置其言语而索其理之非是，批于左方，使得于是省焉，仲实于亮可以无慊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283429_comment'></div>切毋以故意待之，曰「是」曰「好」而已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283429_comment'></div>儒释之道，判然两涂，此是而彼非，此非而彼是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283429_comment'></div>而溺于佛者，直曰「其道有吾儒所未及者」，否亦曰「其精微处吻合无间」，而高明之士犹曰「儒释深处，所差秒忽尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283429_comment'></div>此举世所以溺焉而不自知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283429_comment'></div>虽知其非者，亦如猩猩知酒之将杀己，且骂而且饮之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283429_comment'></div>近世张给事学佛有见，晚从杨龟山学，自谓能悟其非，驾其说以鼓天下之学者，靡然从之，家置其书，人习其法，几缠缚胶固，虽世之所谓高明之士，往往溺于其中而不能以自出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283429_comment'></div>其为人心之害，何止于战国之杨墨也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283429_comment'></div>亮不自顾，尝痛心焉，而力薄能鲜，无德自将，有言不信，徒慨然而止耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283429_comment'></div>然使贼假募士之名，得入帐下，一旦起而缚之，此李元平所以孺弄于李希烈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283429_comment'></div>茍无儒先生驾说以辟之，则中崩外溃之势遂成，吾道之不绝如缕耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283429_comment'></div>仲实力可以有为者，其将何辞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283429_comment'></div>胸中所怀千万，念遂为仲实言之，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1283429", 1283429, "Clauses/163/Comments/0")'>笔困纸穷</span>，不能以究。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283429_comment'></div>暑伏恐未可迎侍，上道果未有日？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283429_comment'></div>尚当握手一吐其肺腑，不敢以相扰动自外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283429_comment'></div>万一便上道，恐宅眷既众，必不免从诸应取道龙窟，过我为一夕之款否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283429_comment'></div>是所望也，不敢必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283429_comment'></div>若从铜坑口趋界牌，所省不能一二里，而纡曲亦不少矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283429_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1283429", 1283429, "Clauses/178/Comments/0")'>临纸</span>无任惓惓。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1283429_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　妻叔何茂恭卒，有祭文。作品：祭何茂恭文。<div id='poem_1283731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283731?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭何茂恭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283731")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283731'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283731'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283731_comment'></div>公之行义文章，自朝之贤士大夫以及于乡党朋友，翕然推之，莫敢为伍，曾未能出其毫末而遽赍之以入土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283731_comment'></div>使知夫吉凶非必善恶，死生何啻旦暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283731_comment'></div>世道消长，容曰有时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283731_comment'></div>而人理逆顺，莫求其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283731_comment'></div>世有所谓推人支干而察人相貌者，至是而手足俱露矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283731_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283731_comment'></div>昔公于某，面未觌而神已交，语言未通而肺肝相与，誉之诸公之间，妻以其兄之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283731_comment'></div>君子或以为难，世俗谓之过举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283731_comment'></div>属憸谗之相间，而至情之疑阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283731_comment'></div>要不能无遗憾于死生，安得取而投之豺虎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283731_comment'></div>虽此心之昭然，顾有口而莫吐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283731_comment'></div>是用略䌽缯纸钱于末俗，具脯果酒殽于罍俎，酹公之神而侑之以韵语，曰：天之生公，意盖有主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283731_comment'></div>俄而夺之，一息千古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283731_comment'></div>匪伤其私，我心独苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283731_comment'></div>尚想音容，有泪如雨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1283731_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年5月</a>　五月，友人陆九渊、陈傅良举进士，陈亮致书陈傅良祝贺，勉其为国珍重。作品：与陈君举又书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参看童振福《陈亮年谱》第15页。）</span><div id='poem_1283469' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283469' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283469?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与陈君举<span class='inlineComment2'>（傅良）</span>书<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283469")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283469_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283469'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283469'>江头之约，参差一月，何意一别遂如许久！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283469_comment'></div>卧病宿留妻家，又失伺候之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283469_comment'></div>继得所留字及括苍书，甚怅然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283469_comment'></div>家君甚以不能少具礼为歉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283469_comment'></div>象先递来去年十月书，宽夫附到正月书，书辞款密周致，愈重相念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283469_comment'></div>但其间每以得失相开警，爱我则至矣，可得谓之相知耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283469_comment'></div>如我与兄及天民之相知，自以为庶几莫逆矣，凡所谓未能免俗之事，宜皆可以略去，独惓惓于柂楼之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283469_comment'></div>亮于兄言固隐然在心，因书又得猛省，此乃正合所望耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283469_comment'></div>妥斋之教良是，今不复用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283469_comment'></div>甚欲得数语相警策，许之而未，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283469_comment'></div>大抵朋友书，寒温外要当有善相示，有过相告，使相去千里常若面对讲习，庶不为无谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283469_comment'></div>监省中魁，本不足多，但世道如此，足为吾党之庆，幸甚至于不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283469_comment'></div>盛名在人久矣，自此遂出其为己者以为人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283469_comment'></div>人之望我者厚，而伺其手蹉足跌者亦不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283469_comment'></div>盛名之兴，古人所戒，兄于此念之熟矣，其善处之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283469_comment'></div>亮忧患之馀，百念灰冷，环顾其中，自为且不足，天重抑之，使之少思其自为之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283469_comment'></div>兄出我处，要归一是，人生岂必其同耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283469_comment'></div>犹记未试前，从子充侍郎处共饮，促膝对语，几于达旦，平生之怀亦略尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283469_comment'></div>今日之事，惟当闭门读书，追往念旧以求其新；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283469_comment'></div>但三丧未举，朝暮在目，使人肝胆摧裂，如不欲生，手未把卷，心已夺去，奈何，奈何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283469_comment'></div>今岁不问有无，断当随力襄奉云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283469_comment'></div>状头无以易兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283469_comment'></div>兄荣归决当取道下里，无更以绍兴故人为辞，甚欲得一见面叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283469_comment'></div>此榜得人之盛，前此以来所未有：兄横骛于江浙，李深卿独步于七闽，一榜而收二虎，斯已奇矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283469_comment'></div>而况象先、元宾、子宜、益之、德脩诸君子交发而并至耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283469_comment'></div>盛事！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283469_comment'></div>盛事！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283469_comment'></div>象先家事如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283469_comment'></div>此去能免作馆否？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283469_comment'></div>东阳郭君力欲屈致，此君抗志极可喜，往住其家，甚有礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283469_comment'></div>象先不作馆则已，若犹未免，宜无以易此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283469_comment'></div>渠亦不敢相迫，虽五月间来，无害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283469_comment'></div>百里使人来求书，其意勤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283469_comment'></div>因与象先议之，勉为此来，幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283469_comment'></div>亮方欲专遣人，忽有此便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283469_comment'></div>廷对在即，天下事大略可睹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283469_comment'></div>顺理而言，主于爱君忧国可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283469_comment'></div>仲舒三策，要皆其胸中事，缓而切，巽而正，可为廷对法，此亦对君父之道。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1283469_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年</a>　同邑孙贯前来受业，陈亮爱其颖悟，用力琢磨之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　春，以近作寄吕祖谦求教。作品：邓耿赞。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参看童振福《陈亮年谱》第15页。）</span>武侯赞。陈思王赞。广惠祈雨文。祭章德文侍郎文。跋喻季直文编。<div id='poem_1283797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283797?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广惠王祈雨文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283797")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283797'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283797'>昔之为农月也，用其力甚勤，而干于神者有时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283797_comment'></div>陂池湖泺，宿有储水，雨不时至，民无预忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283797_comment'></div>神于斯时，享民之报，为甚逸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283797_comment'></div>今农之惰亦甚矣，方春无事，宜可以用其力，而陂池不塞，湖泺不治，委天之泽，若不足急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283797_comment'></div>四月之间，田有青草，浅耕而易种之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283797_comment'></div>耘耔不虔，嘉种不达，幸其与青草俱活也，指为有秋之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283797_comment'></div>十日无雨，则皇皇奔走告于神，神怜其愚而降之泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283797_comment'></div>以为岁可常也，不改其惰，而恳请之数，顽不自省，神岂能终惠于如此之惰民乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283797_comment'></div>亮等今思厥愆，惭恨<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283797", 1283797, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>入地</span>，欲预为之储，则既已无及；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283797_comment'></div>坐而视之，将无所得食以死，永永无事神之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283797_comment'></div>强颜又哀告焉，而云雨满天，若将许其告者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283797_comment'></div>神更宽其诛，卒赐一岁之泽，而农之惰犹习其故，可以弃之沟壑无疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283797_comment'></div>矢心陈辞，伏地待赐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1283797_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283717' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283717' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283717?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭章德文侍郎文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283717")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283717_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283717'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283717'>呜呼公乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283717_comment'></div>穷之与达，判焉西东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283717_comment'></div>于其中间，又或不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283717_comment'></div>一官自效，随事著功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283717_comment'></div>贵为公卿，有志不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283717_comment'></div>庸讵知夫达之非穷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283717_comment'></div>呜呼公乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283717_comment'></div>是非安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283717_comment'></div>祗系其逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283717_comment'></div>危疑之间，一发不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283717_comment'></div>顺而止之，以图厥终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283717_comment'></div>此心未白，去国匆匆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283717_comment'></div>自古尚多，无愧于中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283717_comment'></div>呜呼公乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283717_comment'></div>学博而粹，气毅以洪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283717_comment'></div>百未试一，论何时公！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283717_comment'></div>为公叹者，是非穷通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283717_comment'></div>岁晚登门，遇知最隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283717_comment'></div>老成已矣，泪搅心胸！</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1283717_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题喻季直文编</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283518")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283518'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283518'>乌伤固多士，而称雄于其间者，余熟其四人焉，盖非特乌伤之雄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283518_comment'></div>喻叔奇于人煦煦有恩意，能使人别去三日念之辄不释；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283518_comment'></div>其为文精深简雅，读之愈久而意若新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283518_comment'></div>何茂恭目空四海，独能降意于一世豪杰，而士亦乐亲之，其文奇壮精致，反覆开阖，而卒能自阐其意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283518_comment'></div>陈德先举一世不足以当其意，而人亦不愿从之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283518_comment'></div>然其文清新劲丽，要不可少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283518_comment'></div>喻季直遇人无亲疏贵贱皆与之尽，而于余尤好；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283518_comment'></div>其文蔚茂驰骋，盖将<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283518", 1283518, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>包罗</span>众体，而一字不苟，读之亹亹而无厌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283518_comment'></div>而四君子者尤工于诗，余病未能学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283518_comment'></div>然皆喜为余出，余亦能为之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1283518", 1283518, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>击节</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283518_comment'></div>余穷滋日甚，索居无赖，时一作念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283518_comment'></div>顾茂恭之骨已冷，而三山相去踰千里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283518_comment'></div>德先季直虽宿春可从其游，而出门辄若有絷其足者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283518_comment'></div>喻行之牧之出季直旧文一编示余，耸然观之，如得所未尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283518_comment'></div>茂恭死，其文益可贵重，而子弟亦珍惜之，欲求一字不可得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283518_comment'></div>得吾季直之文，便如茂恭在日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283518_comment'></div>昔余尝读茂恭之文而面叹曰：「九原不可作，欧苏姑置勿论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283518_comment'></div>如世所谓六君子者，公将何愧」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283518_comment'></div>茂恭油然而笑，盖以为「能知我者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283518_comment'></div>幽明异道，每念此，意为之索然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283518_comment'></div>今将求厌足于季直耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1283518_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年7月</a>　七月，薛季宣卒，有祭文。作品：祭薛士龙知府文。<div id='poem_1283720' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283720' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283720?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭薛士隆知府文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283720")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283720_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283720'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283720'>余行天下，窃有志于当世：其道德纯明可为师表者，执贽进见，获听微言于下风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283720_comment'></div>退而从<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283720", 1283720, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>磊瑰不羁</span>之士接杯酒之欢，笑歌起舞，往往自以为一世之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283720_comment'></div>至于山巅水涯，与夫穷阎委巷之间，抱负所有，分与世绝，足所可及，则必一见，纵力不能自致，而声音姓字之与通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283720_comment'></div>晚将归休，始获见公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283720_comment'></div>握手一笑，话言从容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283720_comment'></div>心满意惬，俯首来东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283720_comment'></div>三年之间，竟安此穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283720_comment'></div>人谁不死，宁公是逢！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283720_comment'></div>又杀吾父，昊天鞠凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283720_comment'></div>生乃如此，实死与同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283720_comment'></div>俯仰惶惶，未知所终。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1283720_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年9月</a>　秋九月，《书欧阳文粹后》成，请吕祖谦评。<div id='poem_1283498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书欧阳文粹后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283498")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283498'>右《欧阳文忠公文粹》一百三十篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283498_comment'></div>公之文根乎仁义而达之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283498", 1283498, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>政理</span>，盖所以翼《六经》而载之万世者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283498_comment'></div>虽片言半简，犹宜存而弗削。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283498_comment'></div>顾犹有所去取于其间，毋乃诵公之文而不知其旨，敢于犯是不韪而不疑也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283498_comment'></div>初，天圣、明道之间，太祖、太宗、真宗以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1283498", 1283498, "Clauses/10/Comments/2")'>深仁厚泽</span>涵养天下盖七十年，百姓能自衣食以乐生送死，而戴白之老安坐以嬉，童儿幼稚什伯为群，相与鼓舞于里巷之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283498_comment'></div>仁宗恭己无为于其上，太母制政房闼，而执政大臣实得以参可否，晏然无以异于汉文、景之平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283498_comment'></div>民生及识五代之乱离者，盖于是与世相忘久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283498_comment'></div>而学士大夫其文犹袭五代之卑陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283498_comment'></div>中经一二大儒起而麾之，而学者未知所向，是以斯文独有愧于古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283498_comment'></div>天子慨然下诏书，以古道饬天下之学者，而公之文遂为一代师法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283498_comment'></div>未几而科举禄利之文非两汉不道，于是本朝之盛极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283498_comment'></div>公于是时，独以先王之法度未尽施于今，以为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1283498", 1283498, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>大阙</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283498_comment'></div>其策学者之辞，慇勤切至，问以古今繁简浅深之宜，与夫周礼之可行与不可行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283498_comment'></div>而一时习见百年之治，若无所事乎此者，使公之志弗克遂伸，而荆国王文公得乘其间而执之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283498_comment'></div>神宗皇帝方锐意于三代之治，荆公以霸者功利之说，饰以三代之文，正百官，定职业，修民兵，制国用，兴学校以养天下之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283498_comment'></div>是皆神宗皇帝圣虑之所及者，尝试行之，寻察其有管晏之所不道，改作之意盖见于末命，而天下已纷然趋于功利而不可禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283498_comment'></div>学者又习于当时之所谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283498", 1283498, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>经义</span>者，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283498", 1283498, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>剥裂</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283498", 1283498, "Clauses/55/Comments/1")'>牵缀</span>，气日以卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283498_comment'></div>公之文虽在，而天下不复道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283498_comment'></div>此子瞻之所为深悲而屡叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283498_comment'></div>元祐间，始以末命从事，学者复知诵公之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283498_comment'></div>未及十年，浸复荆公之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283498_comment'></div>迄于宣、政之末，而五季之文靡然遂行于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283498_comment'></div>然其间可胜道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283498_comment'></div>二圣相承又四十馀年，天下之治大略举矣，而科举之文犹未还嘉祐之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283498_comment'></div>盖非独学者不能上承圣意，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1283498", 1283498, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>科制</span>已非祖宗之旧，而况上论三代！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283498_comment'></div>始以公之文，学者虽私诵习之，而未以为急也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283498_comment'></div>故予姑掇其通于时文者，以与朋友共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283498_comment'></div>由是而不止，则不独尽究公之文，而三代两汉之书盖将自求之而不可御矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283498_comment'></div>先王之法度犹将望之，而况于文乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283498_comment'></div>则其犯是不韪，得罪于世之君子而不辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283498_comment'></div>虽然，公之文<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1283498", 1283498, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>雍容典雅</span>，纡馀宽平，反覆以达其意，无复毫发之遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283498_comment'></div>而其味常深长于言意之外，使人读之，蔼然足以得祖宗致治之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283498_comment'></div>其关世教，岂不大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283498_comment'></div>初，吕文靖公、范文正公以议论不合，党与遂分，而公实与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283498_comment'></div>其后西师既兴，吕公首荐范、富、韩三公，以靖天下之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283498_comment'></div>文正以书自咎，欢然与吕公戮力，而富公独念之不置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283498_comment'></div>夫左右相仇，非国家之福；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283498_comment'></div>而内外相关而下相沮，盖治道之基也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283498_comment'></div>公与范公之意盖如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283498_comment'></div>当是时，虽范忠宣犹有疑于其间，则其用心于圣贤之学而成祖宗致治之美者，所从来远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283498_comment'></div>退之有言：「仁义之人，其言蔼如也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283498_comment'></div>故予论其文，推其心存至公而学本乎先王，庶乎读是编者其知所趋矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283498_comment'></div>乾道癸巳九月朔，陈亮书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1283498_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　吕祖谦之《邓仲华赞》请陈亮评议。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　《伊洛正源书》成，有序。作品：伊洛正源书序。<div id='poem_1283502' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283502' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283502?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伊洛正源书序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283502")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283502_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283502'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283502'>濂溪周先生奋乎百世之下，穷太极之蕴以见圣人之心，盖天民之先觉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283502_comment'></div>手为《太极图》以授二程先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283502_comment'></div>前辈以为二程之学，后更光大，而所从来不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283502_comment'></div>横渠张先生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1283502", 1283502, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>崛起</span>关西，究心于龙德正中之地，深思力行而自得之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283502_comment'></div>视二程为外兄弟之子，而相与讲切，无所不尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283502_comment'></div>世以孟子比横渠，而谓二程为颜子，其学问之渊源，顾岂苟然者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283502_comment'></div>《西铭》之书，明道以为「某得此意，要非子厚笔力不能成也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283502_comment'></div>伊川之叙《易》《春秋》，盖其晚岁之立言以垂后者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283502_comment'></div>间常谓其学者张绎曰：「我昔状明道之行，我之道盖与明道同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283502_comment'></div>异时欲知我者，求之于此文可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283502_comment'></div>其源流之可考者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283502_comment'></div>集为之书，以备日览，目曰《伊洛正源书》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1283502_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　《伊洛礼书补亡》成，有序。作品：伊洛礼书补亡序。<div id='poem_1283507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>伊洛礼书补亡序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283507")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283507'>吾友陈傅良君举为余言：「薛季宣士隆尝从湖襄间所谓袁道洁者游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283507_comment'></div>道洁盖及事伊川，自言得《伊洛礼书》，欲至蜀以授士隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283507_comment'></div>士隆往候于蜀，而道洁不果来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283507_comment'></div>道洁死，无子，不知其书今在何许」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283507_comment'></div>伊川尝言：「旧脩六礼，已及七分，及被召乃止，今更一二年可成」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283507_comment'></div>则信有其书矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283507_comment'></div>道洁之所藏近是，惜其书之散亡而不可见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283507_comment'></div>因集其遗言中凡参考礼仪而是正其可行与不可行者，以为《伊洛礼书补亡》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283507_comment'></div>庶几遗意之未泯，而或者其书之尚可访也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1283507_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　《三先生论事录》成，有序。作品：三先生论事录序。<div id='poem_1283503' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283503' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283503?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三先生论事录序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283503")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283503_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283503'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283503'>昔顾子敦尝为人言：「欲就山间与程正叔读《通典》十年」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283503_comment'></div>世之以是病先生之学者，盖不独今日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283503_comment'></div>夫法度不正则人极不立，人极不立则仁义礼乐无所措，仁义礼乐无所措则圣人之用息矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283503_comment'></div>先生之学，固非求子敦之知者，而为先生之徒者，吾惧子敦之言遂得行乎其间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283503_comment'></div>因取先生兄弟与横渠相与讲明法度者录之篇首，而集其平居议论附之，目曰《三先生论事录》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283503_comment'></div>夫岂以为有补于先生之学，顾其自警者不得不然耳。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1283503_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　该年，刊《程氏易传》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　刊《杨氏中庸解》，有序。作品：杨氏中庸解序。<div id='poem_1283508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283508?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨龟山中庸解序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283508")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283508'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283508'>世所传有伊川先生《易传》，杨龟山《中庸义》，谢上蔡《论语解》，尹和靖《孟子说》，胡文定《春秋传》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283508_comment'></div>谢氏之书，学者知诵习之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283508_comment'></div>尹氏之书，简淡不足以入世好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283508_comment'></div>至于是三书，则非习见是经以志乎举选者，盖未之读也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283508_comment'></div>世之儒者，揭《易传》以与学者共之，于是靡然始知所向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283508_comment'></div>然予以谓不由《大学》《论语》及《孟子》《中庸》以达乎《春秋》之用，宜于《易》未有用心之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283508_comment'></div>今《语孟精义》既出，而谢氏、尹氏之书具在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283508_comment'></div>杨氏《中庸》及胡氏《春秋》，世尚多有之，而终病其未广，别刊为小本，以与《易传》并行，观者宜有取焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1283508_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　刊《胡氏春秋传》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月2日</a>　十二月二日，合葬祖父、祖母、母于龙窟卧龙山，为先祖撰墓志铭。作品：先祖府君墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参看颜虚心《宋陈龙川先生亮年谱》第38页。）</span><div id='poem_1283674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先祖府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283674")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283674'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283674'>东汉之衰，太丘长陈公名实，是为有道君子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283674_comment'></div>纪、群又克世其家，位至三公九卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283674_comment'></div>司马氏南渡，而逵从以迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283674_comment'></div>其后家于吴兴，霸先遂据全吴，四世乃亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283674_comment'></div>其葬于婺之永康号厚陵者，或曰后陵，陵今虽在，锢之以铜，不可发，莫能考其为谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283674_comment'></div>故永康之陈最号繁多，而谱牒未尝相通也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283674_comment'></div>往尝有于百年屋壁间得数纸书，言谱系甚详，有曰王，曰公，曰御史大夫，曰龙虎大将军者，疑其为陈、隋间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283674_comment'></div>至本朝咸平以后，始从世俗称号曰公，则陈氏之散落为民久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283674_comment'></div>亮之八世祖讳通，及其子讳隆，始自奋田闾间，居陵旁七八里，曰前黄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283674_comment'></div>至孙讳援，遂大其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283674_comment'></div>有子四人，其三则于亮为高祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283674_comment'></div>高祖讳贺，早夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283674_comment'></div>一子，曾祖也，讳知元，宣和间以隶籍武弁，例赴京城守御，从大将刘延庆死于固子门外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283674_comment'></div>是生我祖，讳益，字进之，为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283674", 1283674, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>冢子</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283674_comment'></div>先祖少以志气自豪，盖尝入舍选，从事于科举，皆垂得而失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283674_comment'></div>既又欲以武事自奋，亦弗克如其志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283674_comment'></div>晚乃浮沈里闬，自放于杯酒间，酒酣歌呼，遇客，不问其谁氏，必尽醉乃止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283674_comment'></div>然其孝友慈爱，明敏有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1283674", 1283674, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>胆决</span>，盖天资固如此也，故亮尝窃言之，昔韩信谓郦生曰：「魏得毋用周叔为大将乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283674_comment'></div>叔亦信之等夷也而湮坠无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283674_comment'></div>士之困穷偃蹇，百未偿一，卒坐牢落以死者，非尽智失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283674_comment'></div>先祖生于崇宁二年正月五日，殁于乾道三年十有二月二十有七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283674_comment'></div>先祖妣黄氏，敦武郎讳琫之女，其生也先先祖一百九十有三日，其殁也亦先六阅月而闰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283674_comment'></div>后六年十有二月有二日，始克合葬于龙窟卧龙山之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283674_comment'></div>将葬，家君实命亮曰：「我高祖坟墓具在，而我曾祖为季子，我不敢祖也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283674_comment'></div>我曾祖、我先祖坟墓不存，又不得而祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283674_comment'></div>我将葬我先人于其中，俾汝母祔于我先夫人之侧，他日次第以昭穆葬，汝居其隅以供洒扫，使自是谱系一二可数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283674_comment'></div>子孙之贤不肖不可知，而吾之志不可不明也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283674_comment'></div>又命亮实书其事于石，以纳诸先祖之圹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283674_comment'></div>亮拜手稽首而泣书曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1283674'>生有遗才，殁有遗义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283674_comment'></div>地有遗形，墓有遗位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283674_comment'></div>尔子尔孙其勿弃。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1283674_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月2日</a>　十二月二日，合葬祖父、祖母、母于龙窟卧龙山，有墓志铭。作品：先妣黄氏夫人墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283700?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先妣黄氏夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283700")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283700_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283700'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283700'>乾道九年十有二月二日，永康陈亮与其弟充，始克合葬其母夫人于龙窟卧龙山之下，盖家君之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283700_comment'></div>于是亮泣血磨石而书曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1283700'>还山而葬，祔于其姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283700_comment'></div>是为十有四岁而生子，生之二十三年而没，没九年乃葬，其子曰亮、充，而其出则黄氏武经郎讳大圭之女乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283700_comment'></div>不能从死，乃从以居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283700_comment'></div>旦暮率妻孥以洒扫，丝竹终身不至其庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283700_comment'></div>天地无穷，不孝安赎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283700_comment'></div>死则葬我墓之隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283700_comment'></div>后千百年，犹不废其为陈氏之墓，则必遇君子长者之人夫！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1283700_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年12月25日</a>　十二月二十五日，父次尹卒。即葬，移灵于道旁之居，撰移灵文。作品：先考移灵文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（一说父次尹卒日为十二月二十四日，参看童振福《陈亮年谱》第18页。）</span><div id='poem_1283728' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283728' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283728?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先考移灵文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年12月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283728")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283728_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283728'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283728'>三年之丧，圣人之中制，非以人子之心至是为已极也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283728_comment'></div>某也积恶而不可掩，既已毒及我先君矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283728_comment'></div>葬不克自力，乃从人贷钱以葬；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283728_comment'></div>坟墓未乾，顽然欲以教人自名，求钱以偿其负，因得窃衣食以苟旦暮之活，至避宅以舍之，使几筵弗克即安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283728_comment'></div>将以明日迁置道旁之居，徒令妻孥以供饮食，而己则安于诵圣人之书以授人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283728_comment'></div>顾不识《礼》所谓「三日不怠，三月不解」，与夫「斩衰唯而不言」者，将阙之而不授乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283728_comment'></div>不然，则宇宙固不汝容矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283728_comment'></div>辜天负地，尚敢以告！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1283728_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　有《送吴恭父序》<div id='poem_1283481' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283481' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283481?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别吴恭父知县序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript:
