ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283481")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283481_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283481'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283481'>亮儿时闻行都有所谓太学者，四方之英大抵萃焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283481_comment'></div>于是新安二吴以文墨妙天下，而季吴独好使酒任气，空所有当摴蒱一掷，不为后掷计，而胜负往来，辄达旦未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283481_comment'></div>遇其倦时，间引恶色自污，不揖客径寝，有儿抚一世之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283481_comment'></div>然而月辄从侪辈较一日短长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283481_comment'></div>侪辈往往口诵心惟，吟哦上下，记忆不少休，试之夕，睫不得交，黎明，裹饭丛入，坐定，心摇摇特未宁，吏持题置之廊柱间，群起就视，相顾无人色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283481_comment'></div>君独凝然遥问侪辈：「题谓何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283481_comment'></div>已则不复伫思，开卷径书，笔不留行，率至日中辄办；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283481_comment'></div>出则歌呼如平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283481_comment'></div>更数日挂名，举眼皆惊曰：「果吴称也，为首选者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283481_comment'></div>他日又曰：「复吴称也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283481_comment'></div>侪辈率畏服之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283481_comment'></div>然嫉之者至于以为可杀，而皆不顾计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283481_comment'></div>久之，得第，尉鄞江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283481_comment'></div>鄞并海，海盗出没，鬼神不可踪迹，间来掠民家，辄去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283481_comment'></div>朝廷虽宿兵不能禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283481_comment'></div>君于是微布耳目，盗所至辄知之，单马径造，捕者踵至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283481_comment'></div>盗惊谓神，咸拱手叠足，死不恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283481_comment'></div>论功至不可计，君不以屑意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283481_comment'></div>犹得京秩，授饶之安仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283481_comment'></div>安仁故号冷邑，至则肃吏厚民，薄征缓赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283481_comment'></div>库不留一钱，遇有急须，片纸立办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283481_comment'></div>民熙熙田里间，而商贾之至者如归，江东壮县或愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283481_comment'></div>会旁境大旱，饥民什百为群，攫食偷活，恶少年乘之为盗，势骎骎且犯境。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283481_comment'></div>州以为忧，遣兵数百戍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283481_comment'></div>富民或劝君挈家就避，君奋然曰：「吾为令，顾委命若等，是谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1283481", 1283481, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>草间求活</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283481_comment'></div>吾宁与贼死，况不必死乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283481_comment'></div>籍丁壮阅之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283481_comment'></div>君驰马横槊于其间，声势张甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283481_comment'></div>邑无赖有袭旁境所为者，法外出新意，杀之以令，皆恐惧缩颈，盗不敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283481_comment'></div>事已，则自劾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283481_comment'></div>不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283481_comment'></div>不便者从而媒孽之，部使者一二捃摭，出条目以诘君，君慨然曰：「吾所为固自不应法，吾不胜法吏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283481_comment'></div>方急时，吾宁能计此耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283481_comment'></div>今鼎镬实甘」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283481_comment'></div>吏从旁为答之，持法者犹欲掇拾其不合以罪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283481_comment'></div>龙川陈亮曰：「成周议能之法，于是不可行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283481_comment'></div>犬羊小丑，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1283481", 1283481, "Clauses/110/Comments/0")'>孩弄</span>中国如无人，天子赫然，不欲赦之，未有以属也，于是且十年矣，顾不能为一壮士道地耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283481_comment'></div>人之有气力者，亦可叹也已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283481_comment'></div>余以积忧多畏之馀，遇君为之捉手起立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283481_comment'></div>于其别也，举酒相属，叹离合之不常、而毁誉之相寻而未已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283481_comment'></div>已而开口大笑曰：「是亦何足计较哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283481_comment'></div>遂行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1283481_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　撰《书家谱石刻后》<div id='poem_1283515' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283515' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283515?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书家谱石刻后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1173年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283515")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283515_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283515'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283515'>陈氏得姓，所由来甚详，今不复载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283515_comment'></div>自太丘长以来，逵既渡江，其后中微，霸先用以为陈，历历可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283515_comment'></div>及唐末五代，比于皇朝之初，陈氏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283515", 1283515, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>散落</span>为民，谱不可系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283515_comment'></div>今断自我七世祖始，从所逮闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283515_comment'></div>自我皇祖若诸从兄弟岁时祭祀，有所谓军阵者次尹，儿时不得问，今莫可质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283515_comment'></div>犹记湖州尚书一人，以待<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1283515", 1283515, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>博闻</span>者参考。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1283515_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　与叶衡有书信。作品：与叶衡书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1173&endYear=1173')">1173年</a>　日贫，欲托讲授为资身之策。浦江钱扩前来受业，不愿习时艺，陈亮劝勉之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年1月</a>　春正月，周葵卒，年七十七，撰文祭之。作品：祭周参政文。<div id='poem_1283718' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283718' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283718?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭周参政文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283718")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283718_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283718'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283718'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283718_comment'></div>万夫之特，天固生之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283718_comment'></div>百年之英，人实成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283718_comment'></div>堂堂故国，乔木则非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283718_comment'></div>火炎昆冈，玉不易为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283718_comment'></div>民生之久，一治一乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283718_comment'></div>道大德宏，遭变则见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283718_comment'></div>死生不易，况于贵贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283718_comment'></div>百圣列前，靖以自献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283718_comment'></div>宣和太学，佥曰新经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283718_comment'></div>公独不然，以自著称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283718_comment'></div>绍兴初论，朝是伊洛，夫岂御史，不知而作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283718_comment'></div>及其中间，人用惰安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283718_comment'></div>非彼生乱，势则容奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283718_comment'></div>权无底止，通国风靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283718_comment'></div>公以死争，屹然中峙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283718_comment'></div>所遭殊时，岂无一同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283718_comment'></div>公独何为，乐此困穷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283718_comment'></div>天定胜人，后将有考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283718_comment'></div>甫三十年，为时故老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283718_comment'></div>故起自山林，而渡江诸贤为之避路，及晚登廊庙，而一时后进安于前驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283718_comment'></div>进不得以遂其心，退不能以明其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283718_comment'></div>惟其忠言嘉话，上心之所独知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283718_comment'></div>至于盛业崇勋，人事犹有遗恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283718_comment'></div>安归田里，一无怼言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283718_comment'></div>烱烱此心，实昭于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283718_comment'></div>亮昔童稚，纵观废兴，大放于辞，愿试以兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283718_comment'></div>狂言撼公，一见而惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283718_comment'></div>借之齿牙，爰及公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283718_comment'></div>爱均骨肉，前辈典型。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283718_comment'></div>《中庸》《大学》，朝暮以听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283718_comment'></div>随事而诲，虽愚必灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283718_comment'></div>行或不力，敢忘其诚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283718_comment'></div>晚以三丧不举，无颜对公，故数年之约而一见之不果；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283718_comment'></div>未几而先人之死与公先后，故三年丧毕而一吊之未成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283718_comment'></div>第见人事之好乖，不知墓草之几生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283718_comment'></div>苟祭酹之可遣，岂蹉跎于此行！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283718_comment'></div>辜天负地，长恸失声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283718_comment'></div>尚为后图，期以自明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1283718_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年4月</a>　夏四月，迫于衣食，东奔西走，不能侍奉父灵，作文哀痛之。作品：先考卒哭文。<div id='poem_1283727' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283727' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283727?labeling=true' target='_blank'>先考卒哭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283727")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283727_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283727'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283727'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283727_comment'></div>我先君委不肖孤而去之，于今四见朔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283727_comment'></div>号天叫地，无所逮及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283727_comment'></div>又以迫于衣食，不能时奉几筵致其哀慕之极，得罪幽冥，死不足赎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283727_comment'></div>古者父母之丧，哭无时，圣人始为之制，曰「三日不怠，三月不解」，又曰「士三月而葬，是月而卒哭」，不欲其伤生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283727_comment'></div>今也朝夕俯首一号而止，其哭之卒也久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283727_comment'></div>朝夕之外，对人如平时，于生复何所伤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283727_comment'></div>及期，以告于灵曰「卒哭」，不即愧死，犹欲自齿于人，岂不以父之爱子死生无间，亦将曰「有故」，甚则曰「以我故」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283727_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283727_comment'></div>欲以自解，不惧无辞，惧宇宙之不汝容耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283727_comment'></div>呜呼羞哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283727_comment'></div>呜呼痛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283727_comment'></div>呜呼已哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1283727_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　六月，撰邑人吏部侍郎章公行状。<div id='poem_1283673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吏部侍郎章公德文行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283673")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283673'>初，公年十六，属方腊唱乱睦之清溪，环浙之东鞠为盗薮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283673_comment'></div>公父朝散惧无全理，则分幼子及衣一箱付公曰：「以是属汝，吾以汝母亦从此遁矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283673_comment'></div>公奉命崎岖山谷间，仅得不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283673_comment'></div>贼平，挟其弟归拜朝散，而箱故无恙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283673_comment'></div>自幼颖悟，读书不苟，善为词赋，而穷经旨至废寝食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283673_comment'></div>中绍兴二年进士第，释褐授处州青田县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283673_comment'></div>尝摄邑，两税旧法有上中下三限，是年夏税，太守风告诸邑：「及上限足者，吾任其材」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283673_comment'></div>公以为「民力不能办，且法不可为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283673_comment'></div>太守大怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283673_comment'></div>公辞邑事，不可，则以次第督之，使无越旧限而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283673_comment'></div>秩满，关升左从政郎，授处州丽水县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283673_comment'></div>改御前军器所干办公事，辟兼川陕宣谕使司书写机宜文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283673_comment'></div>以劳，得左承直郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283673_comment'></div>用荐者，改左奉议郎，干办行在诸军审计司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283673_comment'></div>磨勘，转左承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283673_comment'></div>公外舅枢密都承旨郑公刚中宣谕川陕，故辟公以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283673_comment'></div>郑公留宣抚四川，而公归矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283673_comment'></div>会权臣秦桧欲文致郑公死地，赖太上皇帝不可，犹以罪罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283673_comment'></div>公亦为言者论去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283673_comment'></div>未几，转左朝奉郎，主管台州崇道观，添差权通判宣州，转朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283673_comment'></div>时魏公良臣得罪里居，公尝以事忤之，良臣不堪，公不为动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283673_comment'></div>良臣由是知公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283673_comment'></div>秦桧死，良臣入参知政事，奏除公两浙提举市舶公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283673_comment'></div>舶司宝货之府，公自常俸外，例所可得，公一不取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283673_comment'></div>对人亦不辄非前例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283673_comment'></div>转左朝请郎，差知建州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283673_comment'></div>州军粮久不给，军情汹汹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283673_comment'></div>至之日，争走拜马前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283673_comment'></div>时公帑缗钱不能三万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283673_comment'></div>公徐谕之曰：「汝辈第各归营，得一月，当次第给矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283673_comment'></div>立案税籍，得豪民<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>奸胥</span>要领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283673_comment'></div>及期，军用沛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283673_comment'></div>于是省教条，宽科率，与吏民相与守法而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283673_comment'></div>不事风采，而去思盖不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283673_comment'></div>连丁朝散及夫人忧，服除，得知鄂州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283673_comment'></div>鄂当水陆之冲，虏分兵扼上流，朝廷出禁军戍鄂，一日至或须船千艘若马五千匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283673_comment'></div>公度不可办者奏闻，馀悉给，无留难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283673_comment'></div>当此之时，朝廷置武事不问馀三十年，并边百姓至不识兵革。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283673_comment'></div>虏卒弃好，流民不知所为，更居迭去，鄂往往不复故民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283673_comment'></div>公区处不遗馀力，民得不以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>兵事</span>恐动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283673_comment'></div>州纳秋租才五千斛，上供至万斛，他须称是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283673_comment'></div>公视酒税籍，得赢钱，立办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283673_comment'></div>人不测其所以至此，往往神之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283673_comment'></div>公戚焉若不自得，人亦莫解也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283673_comment'></div>鄂民相与遮监司自言：「公实爱我，愿从朝廷别借公一岁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283673_comment'></div>监司欲以闻，公笑谓曰：「诸公庸知非某意耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283673_comment'></div>且朝廷未易欺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283673_comment'></div>某不自爱，惧贻门下羞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283673_comment'></div>不果闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283673_comment'></div>除两浙西路提举常平茶盐公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283673_comment'></div>漕司常贷常平缗钱二万万，至是已数年，漕司置不复言，常平亦不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283673_comment'></div>公叹曰：「此非法意也，民不知赖矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283673_comment'></div>立移督之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1283673_comment'></div>而户部复请贷三万万，公甚难之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1283673_comment'></div>衔命小校耻不即得，出不逊语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1283673_comment'></div>公叱之曰：「此圣旨耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1283673_comment'></div>常平，民命也，犹当以法奏覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1283673_comment'></div>不然，奴何敢尔」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1283673_comment'></div>退而叹曰：「官不可为矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1283673_comment'></div>户部寻知不可，公亦不欲自异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1283673_comment'></div>今上登极，覃恩转左朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1283673_comment'></div>明年，转左朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1283673_comment'></div>又明年，召除尚书吏部员外郎，兼皇子庆王府直讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1283673_comment'></div>乾道改元，为郎中，除殿中侍御史兼侍讲，迁侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1283673_comment'></div>公上疏，大略言：「祖宗之大雠未报，中原之故地未复，尝胆之志可少忘乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1283673_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/169/Comments/0")'>欢好</span>常败于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_65_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/169/Comments/1")'>变诈</span>，师旅或兴于无名，歃血之好可久恃乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1283673_comment'></div>至于淮堧疮痍，江浙饥馑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1283673_comment'></div>邦财未裕，军政久隳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1283673_comment'></div>士风坏于奔竞，朝纲挠于私曲：此皆当今急务，不宜以偃兵而置度外也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1283673_comment'></div>又上言：「愿以财赋、边备二事专委大臣，集群臣之说，参订其可行者，置局措画，假之岁月以责其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1283673_comment'></div>如以为今之大臣不足任，愿精择可任者任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1283673_comment'></div>不然，因循苟简，臣恐后日不可悔也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1283673_comment'></div>又请「博求武勇，以备将帅之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1283673_comment'></div>三十年来，将帅以事废，罪不至误国者，愿一切与之自新」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1283673_comment'></div>又尝因水潦，有旨侍从台谏条具阙失，公上言：「苟人事皆得其实，是乃应天之实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1283673_comment'></div>人材欲取实能，政事欲取实效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1283673_comment'></div>诸所进用，必考其实，使一时虚名求售者不得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/206/Comments/0")'>冒进</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1283673_comment'></div>然后申敕有司，视朝廷利害如在其家与其身，不得以文移虚具上下相蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1283673_comment'></div>人修实行，事建实功，上施实德，下受实惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1283673_comment'></div>应天之实，宜无大于此者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1283673_comment'></div>时朝廷令两浙、江东人户为田一万亩者，籴米三千石，抑配度牒、关子之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1283673_comment'></div>公以为「事类科敛，无体民经国之意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1283673_comment'></div>朝廷以经用不足，议权拘郡县职田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1283673_comment'></div>公以为「所得不足以当大农一日之数，自为纷纷，损失大体」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1283673_comment'></div>户部侍郎朱夏卿以交子兑发诸道常平钱一百万缗，公上疏，以为「自立常平以来，其间用兵多故，主计之臣固尝出意趣办，独常平以民命故，法不得睥睨，夏卿何为者，而敢轻坏成法？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1283673_comment'></div>又公凿交子不得支用，欺罔不顾忌，法不可赦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1283673_comment'></div>知池州鲁察以竹生穗实为瑞竹，图之而囊其实来献，且言饥民实赖以食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1283673_comment'></div>公上疏，以为「物反常则为妖，竹非穗实之物，是反常也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1283673_comment'></div>竹生实则林必枯，是妖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1283673_comment'></div>以妖为瑞，是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_89_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/248/Comments/0")'>罔上</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1283673_comment'></div>况饥民有食糟糠者，有食草根木实者，食土之似粉者，岂以为是珍于五谷哉，犹愈于死而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1283673_comment'></div>察牧民，顾使其民至此，犹以为瑞而献之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1283673_comment'></div>佞邪成风，渐不可长」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1283673_comment'></div>又言：「给事中王时升似朴实诈，足以欺世乱俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1283673_comment'></div>右奉直大夫谢铎尝事伪楚，不宜叨世赏，无以示为臣者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1283673_comment'></div>上皆从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1283673_comment'></div>初，公尝上疏言：「陛下临御以来，首禁监司太守数易，今往往无故辄易矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1283673_comment'></div>添差官不许釐务，今稍稍放行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1283673_comment'></div>初改官人惟许注知县，今有经营得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_98_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/274/Comments/0")'>堂除</span>者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1283673_comment'></div>有差遣人不许再易，今图换易者纷然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1283673_comment'></div>至于荫补初出官者法当<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_100_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/277/Comments/0")'>铨试</span>，今有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_100_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/278/Comments/0")'>堂除</span>免试者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1283673_comment'></div>京官合入监当，今有径得职事官者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1283673_comment'></div>私意胜而公法为虚文，不严加<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_102_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/282/Comments/0")'>禁戢</span>，则公道荡然矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1283673_comment'></div>既而闻放未<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/284/Comments/0")'>铨试</span>人魏好信等已四五十人，参知政事虞允文意颇主之，公不乐也，即上言：「今春<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/288/Comments/1")'>铨试</span>，已中者率待五六年阙，而黜落者乃得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/290/Comments/0")'>美除</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1283673_comment'></div>以援废法，以私害公，事虽小而所系者大，乞并行追寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1283673_comment'></div>不惟略存公道，亦清仕流之一端也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1283673_comment'></div>朝廷尝拣发诸路厢、禁、土军若五分弓手，就阅行在所，籍为忠勇一军，隶步军都指挥使戚方，约防秋罢遣还所在郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1283673_comment'></div>隆兴元年留不遣，明年又留不遣，至是，犹未遣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1283673_comment'></div>军人相与诣台自言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1283673_comment'></div>公移牒枢密院，不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1283673_comment'></div>军人不堪，往往窜去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1283673_comment'></div>公即上言：「足食足兵，为政之先务，圣人以为必不得已则去兵去食，而信终不可去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1283673_comment'></div>今因兵而失信，无乃不可乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1283673_comment'></div>上语公曰：「此军朕所自阅，费不知限数，而欲尽遣耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1283673_comment'></div>公奏曰：「臣所不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1283673_comment'></div>臣所知者，人情事体尔」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1283673_comment'></div>上曰：「然则当尽逃乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1283673_comment'></div>公奏曰：「今逃数虽可掩，而人人心动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1283673_comment'></div>一旦空营迸散，不捕则废法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1283673_comment'></div>捕则相率旅拒，损威失体，重为天下笑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1283673_comment'></div>上曰：「当与大臣议之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1283673_comment'></div>数日，公又上言，以为逃数已不可掩，急遣犹虑无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1283673_comment'></div>上曰：「前日议犹未定」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1283673_comment'></div>公奏曰：「议未定者，是不可之辞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1283673_comment'></div>臣言不行，无所逃罪，重为朝廷惜此举动尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1283673_comment'></div>枢臣迎合圣意，得无后悔乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1283673_comment'></div>上颔之，曰：「更当徐议」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1283673_comment'></div>虞允文时兼同知枢密院事，一日召戚方议之，事复寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1283673_comment'></div>一军窜逸无留者，又相与拒斗，不可捕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1283673_comment'></div>将校以下皆贬官，而方独放罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1283673_comment'></div>公言：「方罪首也，不可赦」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1283673_comment'></div>落方龙神卫四厢都指挥使，仍旧管军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1283673_comment'></div>公慨然曰：「是不足问矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1283673_comment'></div>即上言：「参知政事兼知枢密院事虞允文轻狂倾险，敢为大言，以文武自将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1283673_comment'></div>今居其位而胸中无有，挟私任情，大略可验」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1283673_comment'></div>公以为允文不去，天下不复有法，连章论奏不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1283673_comment'></div>允文竟罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1283673_comment'></div>时参知政事钱端礼以肺腑与政，丞相久虚府，朝议以为旦夕当同拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1283673_comment'></div>允文去而端礼之议亦寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1283673_comment'></div>公亦得罪去国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1283673_comment'></div>初，公在浙西，梁俊彦得中旨措置酒库，公不以职事左右之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1283673_comment'></div>俊彦不满，比去，问公所欲，公唯唯不对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1283673_comment'></div>及俊彦干办皇城司转官，独不行台谢故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1283673_comment'></div>公劾俊彦废法，俊彦竟以赎论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1283673_comment'></div>会公除吏部侍郎，力请罢去，上怒公辞免不逊，有旨放罢，汀州居住。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1283673_comment'></div>或为公言：「是行，俊彦有力」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1283673_comment'></div>公正色曰：「吾事君不知大体，分应得罪，俊彦何为者邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1283673_comment'></div>且圣明岂受人耳语」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1283673_comment'></div>在汀七年，杜门观书，世念泊如也，独以不得展省先垄松楸为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1283673_comment'></div>既有旨自便，则归拜垄下，退语妻子：「今死无恨矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1283673_comment'></div>明年，得提举江州太平兴国宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1283673_comment'></div>又明年，以疾卒于正寝，实乾道九年闰正月之二日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1283673_comment'></div>享年六十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1283673_comment'></div>娶陈氏，早卒，赠宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1283673_comment'></div>再娶郑氏，四川宣抚副使公之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1283673_comment'></div>子男五人：涛，右迪功郎平江府长洲县主簿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1283673_comment'></div>渭，左从政郎临安府富阳县丞，先公八月卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1283673_comment'></div>涣，以公致仕恩奏上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1283673_comment'></div>充，从进士举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1283673_comment'></div>湜，奉公命出后公仲弟著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1283673_comment'></div>女四人：长适宣义郎两浙西路提点刑狱司干办公事郑枢孙，次适进士陈桧，次适迪功郎江州德化县主簿杨注，次适承奉郎监临安府粮料院郑庄孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1283673_comment'></div>孙男十人：机、桷、崧、云卿、矩、柄、采、棣，馀未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1283673_comment'></div>女三人：长适进士卢诚，馀幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1283673_comment'></div>涛将以淳熙元年九月十三日甲寅，奉公葬于永康县武平乡碧湍里三石湖之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1283673_comment'></div>前葬，涛以行实为请，且言：「先君实知子」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1283673_comment'></div>亮屡道罪逆不能，固辞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1283673_comment'></div>涛固以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1283673_comment'></div>亮自惟少年时不自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_167_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/462/Comments/0")'>爱重</span>，晚方悔悟，乡闾故不齿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1283673_comment'></div>独公一见得之，命其子弟相与共学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1283673_comment'></div>一日来过，则具杯酒从容侍公语，间论天下人物，往往意合，知公金玉人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1283673_comment'></div>因叹世之量人者甚浅，不足据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1283673_comment'></div>然尝闻之公之子弟：公尝诵古诗「每向秋山拾红叶，姓名那许世人知」，辄讽咏不能已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1283673_comment'></div>可以观公之志矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1283673_comment'></div>然则纷纷固非其所屑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1283673_comment'></div>每自幸晚学得依，而公遽下世，为之恸，且涕下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1283673_comment'></div>义当执笔状公之行，以告世之有道立言之君子，而语言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_175_1283673", 1283673, "Clauses/486/Comments/0")'>荒乱</span>失绪，辞不获，则姑次第之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1283673_comment'></div>公讳服，字德文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1283673_comment'></div>其先建之浦城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1283673_comment'></div>五代之乱，徙杭之盐官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1283673_comment'></div>国初来婺，因家永康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1283673_comment'></div>曾祖洞，祖玠，父俣，累赠右朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1283673_comment'></div>母应氏、陈氏，赠宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1283673_comment'></div>公及朝散在时为郡，朝散得封右奉议郎，乡人荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1283673_comment'></div>公有《论语》、《孟子》解各二卷，《易解》二卷，古律诗四卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1283673_comment'></div>淳熙元年夏六月晦，陈亮谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_184_1283673_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年6月</a>　寄《祭薛士龙知府文》给吕祖谦，吕谓皆肝膈中语。其后，祖谦薛士龙墓志铭成，陈亮有复信。作品：与吕伯恭正字。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　秋，归自天台，有《桂枝香》词寄吕祖谦。（天高气肃）<div id='poem_157255' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157255' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157255?labeling=true' target='_blank'>桂枝香 观木犀有感寄吕郎中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157255")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157255_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157255'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157255'>天高气肃。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157255'>正月色分明，秋容新沐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157255'>桂子初收，三十六宫都足。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157255'>不辞散落人间去，怕群花、自嫌凡俗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157255'>向他秋晚，唤回春意，几曾幽独。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157255_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157255'>是天上、馀香剩馥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157255'>怪一树香风，十里相续。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157255'>坐对花旁，但见色浮金粟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_157255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_157255'>芙蓉只解添愁思，况东篱、凄凉黄菊。<div id='poem_sentence_8_157255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_157255'>入时太浅，背时太远，爱寻高躅。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_157255_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_157255'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(157255)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　致书叶衡丞相，述别后五年境遇之屯蹇。作品：上叶丞相衡又书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　与刘元实、唐仲友陪叶衡丞相宴，即席赋《贺新郎》词。（修竹更深处）<span class='inlineComment2'>（一说《贺新郎》（修竹更深处）作于淳熙二年（1175），参见姜书阁《陈亮龙川词笺注》第1页。）</span><div id='poem_157248' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157248' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157248?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎 同刘元实唐与正陪叶丞相饮</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157248")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157248_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157248'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157248'>脩竹更深处。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157248'>映帘栊、清阴障日，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_157248", 157248, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>坐来</span>无暑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157248'>水激泠泠知何许，跳碎危栏玉树。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157248'>都不系、人间朝暮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157248'>东阁少年今老矣，况樽中、有酒嫌推去。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157248'>犹著我，名流语。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157248_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157248'>大家绿野陪容与。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157248'>算等閒、过了薰风，又还<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_157248", 157248, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>商素</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_157248'>手弄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_157248", 157248, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>柔条</span>人健否，犹忆当时雅趣。<div id='poem_sentence_8_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_157248'>恩未报、恐成辜负。<div id='poem_sentence_9_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_157248'>举目江河休感涕，念有君、如此何愁虏。<div id='poem_sentence_10_157248_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_157248'>歌未罢，谁来舞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_157248_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　为弟子徐硕之妻赵氏撰墓志铭。作品：徐妇赵氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徐妇赵氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283706")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283706'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283706'>余往贫不能自食，乡人徐介卿欲以子硕属余，而使食焉，余谢不敢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283706_comment'></div>其后计穷，竟出此，而介卿之死久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283706_comment'></div>自其故所往来，皆莫余助，其势独难于介卿在时，以是尤念介卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283706_comment'></div>已而闻硕联姻皇之近族，冀得官以立门户，余窃嗟是非介卿之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283706_comment'></div>然硕方务学不辍，晚又见其文日以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283706_comment'></div>今年春三月十有四日，其妇既归，殊不类贵家儿女，上下相顾欣然，其姑大恨得妇之晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283706_comment'></div>余时为客，亦以为事往往出意料之外，介卿于是可以瞑目矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283706_comment'></div>甫二月，而其妇病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283706_comment'></div>及余客临安，得硕书，告以妇死，惟恨不孝不克事姑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283706_comment'></div>硕哭之过悲，将以九月之十日葬妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283706_comment'></div>未及有子，异时孰知其妇之为可哀也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283706_comment'></div>曾祖某，嘉国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283706_comment'></div>祖某，集庆军节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283706_comment'></div>父某，今为武翼郎，主管台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283706_comment'></div>于是陈亮同甫与之铭，而叶适正则为之书其石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283706_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1283706'>徐氏再世之墓，其名曰季园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283706_comment'></div>旁有小冢，是为濮王六世之孙而硕之室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283706_comment'></div>为女二十有七岁，为妇一百有三十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283706_comment'></div>生死宜之，是为永毕。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1283706_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年10月</a>　十月，葬叔祖廷俊府君。作品：陈府君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283688")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283688'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283688'>永康之陈，大抵派自吴兴，盖其所从来远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283688_comment'></div>其居邑之南四十五里曰前黄者，远事今皆不论，论其耳目之所及者：溯亮而数之，凡八世，而亮年适四十矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283688_comment'></div>三十年得一世，其间又有过二十而得子者，陈氏于今往往近二百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283688_comment'></div>虽不能驰骤取功名富贵以自见于斯世，而衣食丰足，推其馀以及邻里，使一乡无憾于陈氏，盖自六世祖讳伯援，而邑人始有称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283688_comment'></div>更三世而守其家法，终始不坠，惟最长一支为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283688_comment'></div>百四五十年之间，衣被国家之饱煖，大家世族或已沦替而无馀，而一乡之望凝然如一日，此岂无所由致哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283688_comment'></div>亮之曾祖，幼丧其父，而高祖母以盛年守志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283688_comment'></div>于是六世祖老矣，家事悉以委之长子，讳文什，实能抚孤存寡，义不以一毫自私，使高祖母儿女之累释然终老而不悔者，恃其夫之有兄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283688_comment'></div>及曾祖死于王事，而先祖兄弟以摧丧之馀暴当门户，凛然惧不自保，而曾伯祖讳良佐实存抚之，所以终其父之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283688_comment'></div>其后先祖病废，先人常有不胜家事之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283688_comment'></div>曾伯祖之子廷俊与其继室叶氏，实左右有家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283688_comment'></div>人事固多故，而吾家三世被其三世之德，其大者可念而不可忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283688_comment'></div>公讳廷俊，字时乂，尝以纳粟辟尉靖之永平，然非其好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283688_comment'></div>先娶同邑吕氏，盖甚宜其家，而不幸早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283688_comment'></div>子男三人：克恭、克勤、克诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283688_comment'></div>女三人：适汪注、胡炳、徐良史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283688_comment'></div>孙男九人，恂、亢、亨、慥、光、恪、几、允、恺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283688_comment'></div>女三人：长适徐士龙，次卢垕，次幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283688_comment'></div>曾孙女二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283688_comment'></div>公生于大观戊子三月十有八日，殁于乾道戊子五月二十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283688_comment'></div>而男女之长者与公相继而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283688_comment'></div>又十有五年冬十月十有二日己酉，始克葬公于距家五里鸡鸣山先茔之旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283688_comment'></div>论次本末，以纳诸幽，诸孤以为责当在亮，谨再拜而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283688_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1283688'>生而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1283688", 1283688, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>敦庞</span>，以壮门户；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283688_comment'></div>长则克家，以光厥祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283688_comment'></div>世有隐德，细犹未数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283688_comment'></div>天道昭然，归安此土。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1283688_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　送叔祖主筠州高安簿，有序文。作品：送叔祖主筠州高安簿序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（一说送叔祖及撰文在前一年，即乾道九年（1173），参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第18页。）</span><div id='poem_1283478' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283478' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283478?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送三七叔祖主筠州高安簿序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283478")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283478_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283478'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283478'>「君子之仕也，行其义也」，自圣人常本诸人情而为是言矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283478_comment'></div>其后始有为贫之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283478_comment'></div>仕至于为贫，而吾道奈何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283478_comment'></div>自科举之兴，世之为士者往往困于一日之程文，甚至于老死而或不遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283478_comment'></div>义不能以自行，贫不能以自为，于其间得尺寸之便，则亦甘心俛首而屑为之，诚知夫义之所在，而贫或迫其后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283478_comment'></div>昔者吾之先祖，盖尝一踬于科举，终其身以为不足从事，而自肆于杯酒之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283478_comment'></div>而其仲氏则以为吾兄之志是或一道也，屡挫屡奋，穷且老而其志不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283478_comment'></div>晚从恩科得一官，冒寒为数千百里之行，而无怼辞怨色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283478_comment'></div>盖昔者伯夷羞与乡人处，而柳下惠至不以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283478", 1283478, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>袒裼裸裎</span>为浼，事固有大异不然者，各从其心之所安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283478_comment'></div>夫天与人每不相值，参差不齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283478_comment'></div>苟非得其所以然，能无几微见于颜面乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283478_comment'></div>此行亦足以观公之贤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283478_comment'></div>公少而力学，壮而有闻于学校间，计其所得乃如此，又足以见公之心固有所存，而不计其得之如何也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283478_comment'></div>某闻尚书郎芮公、刘公方将漕江外，芮公固研席之旧，而刘公则素厚某者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283478_comment'></div>大帅龚公之贤，宇内所闻，当不以贵贱尊卑穷达而相忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283478_comment'></div>而某之师友永嘉郑公，朝暮来总风宪，曩固尝加惠于公矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283478_comment'></div>四公，天下贤者：而邑僚则又有刘君子澄，闻其贤旧矣，而张、吕二君子交口而誉道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283478_comment'></div>往拜四公，退与君上下其论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283478_comment'></div>人生赢粮千里，求天下之贤者与处而或不遂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283478_comment'></div>此行况味良不恶，度公之志可以少伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283478_comment'></div>而某方谋葬公之兄，不及从公以行，书以寄刘公，使知天下之士其穷而可叹者至于如此，而部使者之权足以为时重，殆不可以一律而观士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283478_comment'></div>「不遗故旧，则民不偷」，公见芮公，倘或可以出此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283478_comment'></div>相对道旧，能不慨然！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283478_comment'></div>郑公之行，徐当寄书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283478_comment'></div>为某寄声刘君：「声求气应，何以教我」！</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1283478_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　《类次文中子》初稿成。作品：类次文中子。<span class='inlineComment2'>（一说《次类文中子》撰于后一年，即淳熙二年（1175），参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第25页。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　《三国纪年》诸赞及序成，就正于吕祖谦。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　有《书次类文中子后》<div id='poem_1283500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书类次文中子后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283500")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283500'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283500'>以《中说》方《论语》，以董常比颜子，与门人言而名朝之执政者，与老儒老将言而斥之无婉辞，此读《中说》者之所同病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283500_comment'></div>今按阮氏本则曰：「严子陵钓于湍石，尔朱荣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283500", 1283500, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>控勒</span>天下，故君子不贵得位」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283500_comment'></div>龚氏本则曰：「严子陵钓于湍石，民到于今称之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283500_comment'></div>尔朱荣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1283500", 1283500, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>控勒</span>天下，死之日，民无得而称焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283500_comment'></div>故模仿《论语》者，门人弟子之过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283500_comment'></div>龚氏本曰：「出而不声，隐而不没；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283500_comment'></div>用之则成，舍之则全」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283500_comment'></div>阮氏本则因董常而言，终之曰：「吾与尔有矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283500_comment'></div>故比方颜子之迹，往往过多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283500_comment'></div>「内史薛公使遗书于予，予再拜而受之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283500_comment'></div>推此心以往，其肯退而名杨素诸公哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283500_comment'></div>「薛公谓予曰：『吾文章可谓淫溺矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283500_comment'></div>予离席而拜曰：『敢贺丈人之知过也』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283500_comment'></div>谓其斥刘炫、贺若弼而不婉者，过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283500_comment'></div>至于以佛为圣人，以无至无迹为道，以五典潜、五礼错为至治，此皆撰集《中说》者抄入之，将以张大其师，而不知反以为累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283500_comment'></div>然仲淹之学如日星炳然，岂累不累之足云乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283500_comment'></div>姑以明予<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283500", 1283500, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>类次</span>之意如此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1283500_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　有《书文中子附录后》<div id='poem_1283501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书文中子附录后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283501")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283501'>《文中子世家》，阮氏本以为杜淹撰，龚氏本则曰福奖、福畤、福郊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283501_comment'></div>今虽不可考，而《世家》不可不录，故存其录而去其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283501_comment'></div>房、魏论礼乐事，出于福畤所录，虽其间语言不能无节，然参考太宗与诸公经营当时之事，宜必有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283501_comment'></div>今备存之，重去其旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283501_comment'></div>以余观之，魏徵、杜淹之于文中子，盖尝有师友之义矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283501_comment'></div>如房、杜，直往来耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283501_comment'></div>故尝事文中子于河汾者，一切抄之，曰门人弟子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283501_comment'></div>其家子弟见诸公之盛也，又从而实之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283501_comment'></div>夫文中子之道，岂待诸公而后重哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283501_comment'></div>可谓不知其师其父者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283501_comment'></div>关子明之筮，同州府君实书而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283501_comment'></div>备其本末者，亦福畤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283501_comment'></div>世往往以其筮为怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283501_comment'></div>《易》有理有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283501_comment'></div>数，出于理者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283501_comment'></div>得其理足以知百世之变，明其数足以计<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1283501", 1283501, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>将来</span>之事，而又何怪焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283501_comment'></div>如子明之论人谋天命，有后世儒生之所不及知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283501_comment'></div>文中子家世之明王道，子明盖有助焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283501_comment'></div>龚氏安得以私意易之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283501_comment'></div>故存此三书，曰《文中子附录》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1283501_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年7月</a>　七月，弟子孙贯死，哀之，有祭文。作品：祭孙冲季文。<div id='poem_1283754' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283754' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283754?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭孙冲季文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283754")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283754_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283754'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283754'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283754_comment'></div>天之生子，殆若有意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283754_comment'></div>变化倚伏，惟人自致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283754_comment'></div>是以君子，勉所未至，兢兢业业，天人之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283754_comment'></div>理之难知，乖其所恃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283754_comment'></div>念子之初，亦或可避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283754_comment'></div>彼其与之以识而偏于才，备其能而啬于德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283754_comment'></div>文足以自见而劳于成名，志足以自立而困于无命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283754_comment'></div>子忧其才之不足，余独以德为可贵；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283754_comment'></div>子方以名为可求，余独以命为可畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283754_comment'></div>今余不幸而言中，使子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1283754", 1283754, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>赍恨</span>而入地，重慈亲之忧，有幼子之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283754_comment'></div>父必以咎而自归，安在其子之有罪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283754_comment'></div>然皇帝王霸之道，圣贤士君子之学，平时乐与子共之者，万事瓦解，而余尤不自知其多涕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283754_comment'></div>叹来者之未涯，伤畴昔之有愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283754_comment'></div>苟子之姓名与我隐显于百世之下，则或为九泉之慰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1283754_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年9月</a>　九月，孙贯葬，陈亮与弟子卢任、徐硕等临其穴，并为之作墓铭。作品：孙贯墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283678' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283678' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283678?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙贯墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283678")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283678_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283678'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283678'>有宋中兴之四十六年，亮始取古今之书一二以读之，稍稍与其可者共学，而同邑孙氏之子懋实来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283678_comment'></div>余爱其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283678", 1283678, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>质性</span>之颖悟也，不爱吾力而琢磨之，日引月长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283678_comment'></div>阅四年，当淳熙乙未，余为易其名曰贯，字冲季，以观其成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283678_comment'></div>秋七月十有三日，冲季死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283678_comment'></div>余哭之恸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283678_comment'></div>冲季得年二十三岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283678_comment'></div>娶陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283678_comment'></div>一子，后七日亦死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283678_comment'></div>于是冲季之父名序，老矣，又鳏居，恃幼子以养，既而以书来告：「贯得吉卜，序复何心以葬贯也」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283678_comment'></div>九月二十八日丙午，余率其友卢任、徐硕、周扩、吕约、周作、喻宏、喻宽、何凝、胡括、钱廓、方坦临葬，深其坎，厚土以覆之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283678_comment'></div>买石识其墓曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1283678'>天地之生生不穷，则死宁有已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283678_comment'></div>惟其生死不信，是以铭之在此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1283678_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　为孙贯之母孙夫人周氏作墓志铭。作品：孙夫人周氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙夫人周氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283701")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283701'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283701'>始，孙贯从余游，余不知其母没若干年而其葬之与未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283701_comment'></div>于是时，余盖七年弗克葬其母矣，蚤夜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283701", 1283701, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>腐心</span>疾首，不忍闻天下之有是事，惟恐其我告，而敢以问人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283701_comment'></div>后二年，始克毕事，因顾谓其友：「即填沟壑无憾矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283701_comment'></div>独贯惨然于众人之中，若不能自容者，盖其母丧犹在殡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283701_comment'></div>贯家故贫，遇岁大旱，贯滋以恨恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283701_comment'></div>明年，淳熙乙未，谋掇其衣食之资，及秋而葬，且将乞铭于余，以告哀于百世之君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283701_comment'></div>立秋之一日，贯得疾不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283701_comment'></div>其父哭之，至于恸绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283701_comment'></div>少定，则祝曰：「吾不以汝死而不终汝志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283701_comment'></div>竟以九月丙午，葬其母于距家一里马双塘之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283701_comment'></div>先事遣其仲子恪泣且拜曰：「子其重哀我亡儿」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283701_comment'></div>余固哀之者，乃为其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1283701'>来徙永康周其姓，资则有女序来聘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283701_comment'></div>宜家宜子又宾敬，四十有二寿则竟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283701_comment'></div>七年乃葬贫斯病，子知其罪制于命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283701_comment'></div>父不忍欺情之正，我非其人铭岂称！</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1283701_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　叶衡罢相,约是年与叶衡书。作品：与叶丞相衡。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　冬,撰商夫人陈氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283702' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283702' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283702?labeling=true' target='_blank'>商夫人陈氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283702")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283702_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283702'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283702'>义乌商盘奉其父命，将以淳熙二年十二月二十日丁酉，葬其母夫人于去家五里横塘之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283702_comment'></div>先事踵门升堂而再拜曰：「天不降不孝之罪于盘之身，而夺其母，泪彻九原而不能以有及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283702_comment'></div>至于免丧，又不克即死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283702_comment'></div>惟是得葬日月迁延至此，生死愧恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283702_comment'></div>敢丐一言以诏其墓于永久，以宽其万分之罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283702_comment'></div>余为之恻然，答拜曰：「此孝子慈孙之请，昔之君子所不爱其力者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283702_comment'></div>然余尝叹：士之把笔为文章以自名于时者，何尝不为不朽之虑，人亦往往乐得其言以自托，至或身未及殁而已无传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283702_comment'></div>其尤长者，由是而数十百年而零落尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283702_comment'></div>始望之不酬，所谓文者果足愿乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283702_comment'></div>况余<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1283702", 1283702, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>志念</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1283702", 1283702, "Clauses/26/Comments/1")'>衰索</span>，图所以及身之计，惧不自保；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283702_comment'></div>虽欲应子之求，其何以应子之求！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283702_comment'></div>今子之邑已多贤士大夫，且吾亦诚惧夫不韪之罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283702_comment'></div>盘无以答，而强请不已，又使吾之亲友故旧交逼而致其辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283702_comment'></div>余不得自通其意，独念其嗜好之不类，或者文之不足托而后世当有悲其志者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283702_comment'></div>夫人姓陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283702_comment'></div>曾祖裕，祖镗，父宗卨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283702_comment'></div>年十七嫁同邑商君锜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283702_comment'></div>子男颂，次则盘，浩先卒，岩、质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283702_comment'></div>女六人，其婿楼知点、陈谦亨、喻宪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283702_comment'></div>馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283702_comment'></div>孙男一、女一，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283702_comment'></div>以乾道九年十月十七日殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283702_comment'></div>于是永康陈亮铭其墓曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1283702'>夫不以穷自怼，而为是邦之彦；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283702_comment'></div>子不以爱自骄，而为处子之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283702_comment'></div>得年四十有八，是为夫人之寿。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1283702_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1175')">1175年</a>　撰蔡元德墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蔡元德墓碣铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283675")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283675'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283675'>崇宁、大观以来，祖宗之涵养天下盖百五六十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283675_comment'></div>三光五岳浑为一气，士之及生其时者，大抵魁梧质重，无自喜多易之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283675_comment'></div>故自渡江后，虽里闾人物往往不自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283675", 1283675, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>促狭</span>：进不得志于科举，退必有以自见于其乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283675_comment'></div>昔亮得之先人者如此，退而私察其同时并举之人，又得东阳蔡君元德焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283675_comment'></div>君尝学于前参知政事王公次翁，去举漕台，不中，始相父经纪其家，以镇其里闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283675_comment'></div>敬老慈少，使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1283675", 1283675, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>诡猾</span>暴横者不得自肆，平民安之，而官事赖以省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283675_comment'></div>及其父春秋日以高，为园池以婆娑自乐，家事一不关焉，遂以忘其老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283675_comment'></div>君卒于乾道九年十二月之朔，后二十有四日，吾先人亦自委弃诸孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283675_comment'></div>其后里闾所见人物，非复往时之旧，愈为之悲伤焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283675_comment'></div>其孤将以淳熙二年十月二十有五日葬于所居相望南溪之原，病世俗之侈于葬，思欲效古以宁其父，大惧力不胜俗，谋之永康陈亮曰：「是惟子之所以自献耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283675_comment'></div>遂属以铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283675_comment'></div>铭非吾任也，不忍使先友之无传、而人物气类之变无考焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283675_comment'></div>君讳弥邵，元德其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283675_comment'></div>不能言其所自来，盖蔡氏之居于蔡塘旧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283675_comment'></div>曾祖讳亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283675_comment'></div>祖讳材，秉义郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283675_comment'></div>父讳友文，从义郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283675_comment'></div>君享年五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283675_comment'></div>娶戚氏，故处州缙云县丞观光之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283675_comment'></div>子男三人：仲熊、仲虎、仲麟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283675_comment'></div>女三人，陈次皋、黄焕、李开，其婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283675_comment'></div>孙男六人，女三人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283675_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1283675'>生足自效于州长县正，而古制之未复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283675_comment'></div>死则自随于敝车羸马，而非以矫其俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283675_comment'></div>尚有铭焉，相墓之木。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1283675_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　刊《三先生论事录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　刊《礼书补遗》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　刊《林勳本政书》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ada89821170a4f379727a301b6e816dc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ada89821170a4f379727a301b6e816dc");'><span id='ada89821170a4f379727a301b6e816dc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>，34岁</div><div id='ada89821170a4f379727a301b6e816dc' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>弟昭甫复归。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，郑伯熊（景望）访于龙窟。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>丁少詹来学。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>为邑人林公材撰墓志铭。作品：林公材墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283677' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283677' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283677?labeling=true' target='_blank'>林公材墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283677")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283677_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283677'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283677'>君姓林氏，讳崧，字公材，婺之永康人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283677_comment'></div>其先从天台来，于君九世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283677_comment'></div>初，君祖父浚、父思聪，自田闾间积勤服业以起其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283677_comment'></div>至君兄弟，且耕且学，以无忘先世之绪而开其来者，自是子弟始一于学矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283677_comment'></div>然君犹以为艰难之易失也，讫晚岁，不自侈大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283677_comment'></div>余尝至其门，崎岖桑柘间，得小径并墙以入，计君之力非不足也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283677_comment'></div>独至于为其子问学之费无所靳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283677_comment'></div>君容貌魁然，事亲能自异于等人，宜其于缓急轻重之际有足观者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283677_comment'></div>不幸得年五十有二，以淳熙二年十一月二十七日甲戌卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283677_comment'></div>娶徐氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283677_comment'></div>子男三人：慬、愉、慥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283677_comment'></div>愉先君五年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283677_comment'></div>孙男女三人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283677_comment'></div>君殁之明年，其孤将以十月甲申日葬于去家一望西山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283677_comment'></div>一日，慥泫然拜于庭下曰：「昔慥实从章氏兄弟以来，今其葬者大抵有铭矣，奈何以处慥父」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283677_comment'></div>余无以答，乃为其铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1283677'>不失其朴，而示以文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283677_comment'></div>尔祖尔父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283677_comment'></div>尔子尔孙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1283677_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>撰章妇胡氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>章妇胡氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283703")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283703'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283703'>故太常寺主簿缙云胡权经仲，能以其学行奔走数州之士，士往往以不得从其游为耻，然亦争好传道其所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283703_comment'></div>初，章德文侍郎有从子，年十许岁失父，精神已自能淩逼人，人固奇之，而亦以此不保其他日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283703_comment'></div>经仲独托以女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283703_comment'></div>稍长，名浩，而字曰养直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283703_comment'></div>及胡氏女既归，其姑殊爱之，养直亦更折节自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283703_comment'></div>妇又事事可人意，以经仲故，相传闾里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283703_comment'></div>养直晚于家事乃有不自得于中者，时时以杯酒自放，妇盖忧之，亦不敢伤其意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283703_comment'></div>然独奉事其姑弥谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283703_comment'></div>一日，相其姑色微有不悦意，时盖已属疾矣，为之数日不食，曰：「十四五年妇姑团圞之意，乃更以指尖事破坏耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283703_comment'></div>我不足为妇明矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283703_comment'></div>且死，常若不释然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283703_comment'></div>死时年三十六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283703_comment'></div>余与养直早相善，入吊，其二儿长短相去案上下间耳，恸哭对客，悲哀伏地如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283703_comment'></div>旁有女奴抱一婴儿以立，意惨惨泣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283703_comment'></div>余为堕泪而出，有以知其母之可书者众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283703_comment'></div>养直于其死若干日，葬之某所之原，实淳熙三年九月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283703_comment'></div>间泣为余言：「甚矣吾哀之不可纾也，吾妇今亡矣」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283703_comment'></div>余使归具石而次所闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283703_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1283703'>生而事姑，死犹不满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283703_comment'></div>此心昭然，其存弥远。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1283703_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>冬，门人胡括为其母请铭，撰胡夫人墓铭。作品：胡夫人吕氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>胡夫人吕氏墓碣铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283704")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283704'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283704'>往余闻吕氏母劳苦有功于家，晚以其女孙妻吾从叔次愈，盖犹及识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283704_comment'></div>于是时年七八十岁，言语质实无饰，抚问其旁儿女子，谆谆有恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283704_comment'></div>因叹承平<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283704", 1283704, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>遗民</span>，虽妇人犹能如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283704_comment'></div>其女孙之嫁胡氏者，有子从余游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283704_comment'></div>闻其始嫁时盖甚少，舅姑辛勤起家，冀得妇以相吾事，且又未有他妇，已自能劳苦以取其舅姑欢心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283704_comment'></div>诸叔之幼小者，抚视加恳恻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283704_comment'></div>其后各各有妇，常先后弥缝之，故上下无大阙失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283704_comment'></div>要之，虽女训久废不用，彼其在父母家习见其尊上人所为，宜不误人家事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283704_comment'></div>吕氏世居婺之永康，曾祖孟，祖该，父章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283704_comment'></div>年十九嫁同邑胡汝弼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283704_comment'></div>从余游之子名括，余爱其可与共学者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283704_comment'></div>下有二子，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283704_comment'></div>一女，适东阳陈师古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283704_comment'></div>嫁之二十九年，以淳熙二年三月二十五日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283704_comment'></div>明年十有二月甲申，葬于去家二里先茔之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283704_comment'></div>先事，括拜且泣曰：「括无以自致于其母者，且伤吾母之德由是而澌尽矣，虽其邱垄，他日未可知也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283704_comment'></div>余无力以重之，为书其石曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1283704'>吾叙次夫人，以存其大母之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283704", 1283704, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>遗风</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283704_comment'></div>吾因其大母，以著太平之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1283704", 1283704, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>遗民</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283704_comment'></div>铭乎远矣，庶及其坟。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1283704_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>为邑人章德文之弟撰墓铭。作品：章晦文墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283679' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283679' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283679?labeling=true' target='_blank'>章晦文墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1176年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283679")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283679_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283679'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283679'>章氏世居建安，国初有来婺者，始为永康人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283679_comment'></div>自郇公申公相继为宰相，故建安之章闻天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283679_comment'></div>其后百有馀年，侍郎公始以进士起家永康，晚入台为侍御史，以吏部侍郎去位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283679_comment'></div>侍郎兄弟四人，而名著字晦文者为同母兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283679_comment'></div>晦文自少容貌伟然，把笔为诗文，便能有不凡语，父兄特爱之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283679_comment'></div>及长，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1283679", 1283679, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>疏豁</span>奋励，不能依阿善恶间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283679_comment'></div>不幸得年四十以死，实绍兴乙亥十二月二十七日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283679_comment'></div>曾祖洞，祖玠，父俣，故赠右朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283679_comment'></div>娶姚氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283679_comment'></div>无子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283679_comment'></div>一女，适进士徐日休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283679_comment'></div>他日，侍郎公叹曰：「吾无兄弟矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283679_comment'></div>我死，吾惧吾弟之不食也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283679_comment'></div>命其取所爱子曰湜者奉其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283679_comment'></div>初，君死时，用子弟礼以葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283679_comment'></div>当淳熙三年，湜盖年十有七矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283679_comment'></div>顾瞻不宁，始议改卜，将以七月乙酉葬于蔡山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283679_comment'></div>礼：无子，以兄弟之子为之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283679_comment'></div>先君之肢体一也，使其一体不废，足矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283679_comment'></div>天理人情之至，圣人所用以为天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1283679", 1283679, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>通制</span>者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283679_comment'></div>使为之后者更力学以显扬其绪，则死生均可以无憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283679_comment'></div>湜尝从予游，盖亦知动心于此者，是以求铭君之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283679_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1283679'>体安于土，魂从其祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283679_comment'></div>谓君无子，亦既有子。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1283679_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d020978049d542df863347a9d5a675ff_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d020978049d542df863347a9d5a675ff");'><span id='d020978049d542df863347a9d5a675ff_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>，36岁</div><div id='d020978049d542df863347a9d5a675ff' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>书上，帝欲官之。亮辞，渡江而归。有答吕祖谦书，称上书非为获己。作品：与吕伯恭正字书。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>复何叔厚书，叙述上书而不得面对，乃出于人力沮遏。<div id='poem_1283440' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283440' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283440?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复何叔厚书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283440")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283440_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283440'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283440'>亮顿首，复书辱答示，甚慰相念之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283440_comment'></div>讯后不审侍奉复何如？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283440_comment'></div>承闻有失子之戚，公方盛年，正不足为忧，他时恐患多耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283440_comment'></div>然处心平夷，亦吾人所当常念也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283440_comment'></div>亮寓临安，却都无事，但既绝意于科举，颇念其平生所学，不可不一泄之以应机会，前日遂极论国家社稷大计，以彻于上听，忽蒙非常特达之知，欲引之面对，乃先令召赴都堂审察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283440_comment'></div>亮一时率尔应答，遂触赵同知之怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283440_comment'></div>亮书原不降出，诸公力请出之，书中又重诸公之怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283440_comment'></div>内外合力沮遏之，不使得面对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283440_comment'></div>今乃议与一官，以塞上意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283440_comment'></div>亮虽无耻，宁忍至此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283440_comment'></div>只俟旦夕命下，即缴还于上而竟东归耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283440_comment'></div>岂有欲开社稷数百年之基，乃用以博一官乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283440_comment'></div>事之不济，此乃天也，亦岂诸公所能沮遏哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283440_comment'></div>吾友所谓纷纷可畏之论，当谓此尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283440_comment'></div>丈夫出处自有深意，难为共儿曹语，亦难以避人谤毁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283440_comment'></div>此怀惟吕丈知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283440_comment'></div>叔范相聚甚好，亮固已知其不凡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283440_comment'></div>但世间大有事，未可便认以为是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283440_comment'></div>仓卒未暇答渠书，相见且勉以志其远者大者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283440_comment'></div>上聪明睿智，度绝百代，一见亮书，便有榜之朝堂以励群臣之意，若使得对，何事不可济！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283440_comment'></div>但绝江之时，已卜知天意未顺，仲几盖与此谋也<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1283440_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，送戴少望参吏部选官之试，作《念奴娇》词。（西风带暑）<div id='poem_157227' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157227' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157227?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇 送戴少望参选</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157227")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157227_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157227'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157227'>西风带暑，又还是、长途利牵名役。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157227'>我已无心，君因甚，更把青衫为客。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157227'>邂逅卑飞，几时高举，不露真消息。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157227'>大家行处，到头须管行得。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157227_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157227'>何处寻取狂徒，可能著意，更问渠侬骨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157227'>天上人间，最好是、闹里一般岑寂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157227'>瀛海无波，玉堂有路，稳著<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_157227", 157227, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>青霄翼</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157227_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157227'>归来何事，眼光依旧生碧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157227_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，叶适来访。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>冬，叶适母亲亡故，为文祭之。作品：祭叶正则母夫人文。<div id='poem_1283772' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283772' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283772?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭叶正则母夫人文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283772")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283772'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283772'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283772_comment'></div>昔余识夫人之子于稚年，固已得其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283772", 1283772, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>昂霄</span>耸壑之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283772_comment'></div>自其客居永康，每一食未尝不东向悽然，有时继以泪下，曰：「吾家甚贫而吾母病，饮食医药宜如何办？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283772_comment'></div>又以劳吾父之心，吾将何以为人子」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283772_comment'></div>余于是时，虽未获登堂之拜，固知夫人之甚慈其子，而为之子者固自为可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283772_comment'></div>且余有父不能养，余甚有愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283772_comment'></div>数年以来，夫人之子大放于古今之书，凡圣贤之用心，与夫后来英雄豪杰之行事，观其会通而得其所以与时偕行者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283772_comment'></div>于是四海友朋如夫人之子者可以一二数，而天下之人有以观夫人之为人母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283772_comment'></div>既而夫人之子又以甲科归拜其亲于庭，并世俗之所谓荣者而并得之，人皆谓夫人之疾宜自是脱然，而竟以不救，岂世俗之是非休戚一不以撄其心，而由疾至死一一自有条理耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283772_comment'></div>疾与死非人力之所可为，而所可为者夫人既加于人一等矣，常情之遗憾，又何以陈之夫人之前耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283772_comment'></div>然夫妇母子，人之至情，死生之际，不可以理譬解，夫人之子与其父，宜何以为心，而朋友之涕亦不自知其潸然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283772_comment'></div>重冈一水，寓哀于文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283772_comment'></div>匍匐之救，有腼古人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1283772_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>为学生椿与允之母章夫人田氏撰墓志铭。作品：章夫人田氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>章夫人田氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283705")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283705'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283705'>始余于送往事居之礼，缺然未知所图，托于讲授以自衣食，而章氏之子椿实左右之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283705_comment'></div>明年，其弟与允相继至，自是岁时往来如旧故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283705_comment'></div>每见其父巨川终日对客，足未尝越户限，而饮食以时，品具精洁，户内如无人声，余固心知其得助矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283705_comment'></div>久而习知其家事，则又有异焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283705_comment'></div>巨川少时颇自豪，视钱如粪土；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283705_comment'></div>已更折节以事生产。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283705_comment'></div>夫人不使户内有一毫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1283705", 1283705, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>渗漏</span>，以发越其志而昌其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283705_comment'></div>及夫人之父春秋日以高，相其甘旨，使无阙而已，不欲其兄弟为资人以生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283705_comment'></div>巨川课诸子以学，曰：「及吾尚健，家事不以累汝」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283705_comment'></div>至于房闱细碎，夫人亦必为之区处，曰：「无以分其心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283705_comment'></div>闻其有称焉，夫妇相对欢笑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283705_comment'></div>否则失声懊恨：「有子何业」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283705_comment'></div>至女之已有归者，问其能事人与否，而不及其他也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283705_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283705_comment'></div>三纲五常，圣人致意于其间者详矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283705_comment'></div>学之不讲，自男子处之不能以得其道，况女训之废于今千载，如夫人之资性适有合者，余甚异焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283705_comment'></div>夫人姓田氏，世居处之缙云。<div class='inline'
