id='poem_sentence_16_1283705_comment'></div>曾祖玉，祖褒，父大亨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283705_comment'></div>年二十，归永康章济巨川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283705_comment'></div>后三十有三年，当淳熙乙未，以十一月二十三日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283705_comment'></div>又三年正月十四日，乃克葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283705_comment'></div>子男三人，从予游者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283705_comment'></div>女三人：长适沈骥，次许嫁胡梓，次未笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283705_comment'></div>孙男女合六人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283705_comment'></div>三子者奉其父命与吾友徐元德居厚之书以来，曰：「愿有述」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283705_comment'></div>乃系之以铭：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1283705'>黄顷之原，四山壁立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283705_comment'></div>幽固静深，夫人之室。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1283705_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>为学生钱廓之父钱元卿撰墓志铭。作品：钱元卿墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钱元卿墓碣铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283681")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283681'>浦江于婺为山邑，非宾客商贾之所奔凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283681_comment'></div>民生其间者，往往朴茂质实，力农务本，家以不欠赋租相尚，人以不历公庭为常，耻于华言少实而以士自命，故间岁之群至于有司者，亦自有数，长吏至，则相与安乐其俗而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283681_comment'></div>其或贪暴自肆，则熟视咨嗟而不敢出一怨愤语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283681_comment'></div>此虽书传所载古者礼义之俗，不过如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283681_comment'></div>往时浦江有钱氏之子廓，从余学，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1283681", 1283681, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>沈静</span>和雅，语如不能出口，称其里中儿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283681_comment'></div>及其学有端绪而归，乡之大人长者相与审问延誉，或折辈行与之交，此皆他邑之所未见者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283681_comment'></div>始，其祖父良臣以辛勤起家，年且七十许，犹无恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283681_comment'></div>其父赞固已学为士，而又甚笃于廓者，俯首书册中，口诵手钞，穷日夜不辍止，然得年二十有六，以绍兴丙子八月之三日死，卒不能少自见于场屋间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283681_comment'></div>死时，有二男一女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283681_comment'></div>其妻为同里金氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283681_comment'></div>金氏抚育其男女，劳苦有恩意，凡十三年亦死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283681_comment'></div>男之长者名抑，疏豁足当门户；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283681_comment'></div>少则廓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283681_comment'></div>女已嫁兰溪方大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283681_comment'></div>其葬在距家五里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283681_comment'></div>他日，二男上冢，痛其父之葬不及待儿之有知也，环视墓门不甚固，谋以淳熙戊戌十一月庚申朔徙葬其地之高处，一一令如法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283681_comment'></div>未徙前六七日，廓以书来曰：「廓得事先生之日久，廓先人宜得铭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283681_comment'></div>余宁有爱于廓，顾铭以立就，惧不足为铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283681_comment'></div>通化之钱尝有显者，余不能详其谱之离合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283681_comment'></div>而三数年来，浦江之俗所闻日与向异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283681_comment'></div>风俗之移人亦甚为廓惧也，非复余向者之所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283681_comment'></div>虽廓之通敏愈于昔，而其朴亦异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283681_comment'></div>后十五日，永康陈亮为之揭铭墓上，以识其向之为士者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283681_comment'></div>盖赞之字曰元卿云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283681_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1283681'>新塘之原，有立其石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283681_comment'></div>是为昔墓，过者必式。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1283681_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='99ba9681c04b4146ac1e639c0351b979_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("99ba9681c04b4146ac1e639c0351b979");'><span id='99ba9681c04b4146ac1e639c0351b979_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1180')">1178-1180年</a>，36-38岁</div><div id='99ba9681c04b4146ac1e639c0351b979' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　为义乌宗武撰墓志铭，宗武乃名将宗泽之从孙。作品：宗县尉墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宗县尉墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283676")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283676'>靖康、建炎之间，故忠简宗公泽起家知磁州，当虏人长驱而南，迸散横溃不可收拾之时，独凭城死守，为天下倡，遂副太上皇帝开元帅府于济南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283676_comment'></div>及太上膺命南京，公留守京师，能以忠义鼓百战之群盗，以婴方锐无前之锋，𢥠然如老罴之当道，馀民因得贾勇从公以奋，而河北已没郡县番为国守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283676_comment'></div>功虽不竟，江南卒赖以立国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283676_comment'></div>是为一代之人豪，中兴之元勋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283676_comment'></div>公世家婺之义乌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283676_comment'></div>皇考某，累赠大中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283676_comment'></div>公兄沃之子稷，亦以公故，得官至修职郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283676_comment'></div>公守磁之岁，稷生子曰武，端整重厚，绝不类常儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283676_comment'></div>比长，能为文章，有声场屋间，三上，卒能取世科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283676_comment'></div>释褐，授饶州德兴尉，便若素闲吏道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283676_comment'></div>平生与人交，乐于倾盖，不为龃龉疑伪意态，有承平时士君子之气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283676_comment'></div>人以谓公耕之炊之，而其诸孙食之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283676_comment'></div>然代满甫及家，以淳熙丙申七月二十三日死，是果何理哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283676_comment'></div>县尉字成老，娶叶氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283676_comment'></div>子男二人：楷、林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283676_comment'></div>女六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283676_comment'></div>何大辩，某某，其婿也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283676_comment'></div>幼未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283676_comment'></div>楷将以戊戌十月丁酉，葬县尉于去家十里熟水塘之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283676_comment'></div>大辩者，永康陈亮妻之弟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283676_comment'></div>楷之妻又其女弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283676_comment'></div>磨圹石，再三乞书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283676_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1283676'>我思忠简，不数士稚，惟其血诚，闻者兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283676_comment'></div>中兴姓名，与国同纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283676_comment'></div>从孙世科，家庭之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283676_comment'></div>不卒壮图，以厚来祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283676_comment'></div>后不复究，其藏在此。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1283676_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　跋中兴五论。作品：中兴五论跋。<div id='poem_1283522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中兴论<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>中兴五论序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283522")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283522'>臣闻治国有大体，谋敌有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>大略</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283522_comment'></div>立大体而后纪纲正，定<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>大略</span>而后机变行，此不易之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283522_comment'></div>仰惟陛下以睿圣神武之资，充硕大光明之学，留神政事，励志恢复，罔敢自暇自逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283522_comment'></div>而大欲未遂，大业未济，意者大体之未立而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>大略</span>之未定欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283522_comment'></div>臣尝为陛下有忧于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283522_comment'></div>尝欲输肝胆，效情愫，上书于北阙之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283522_comment'></div>又念世俗道薄，献言之人动必有觊，心虽不然，迹或近似，相师成风，谁能不疑！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283522_comment'></div>既已疑矣，安能察其言而明其心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283522_comment'></div>此臣之所大惧而卒以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>自沮</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283522_comment'></div>今年春，随试礼部，侥倖一中，庶几俯伏殿陛，毕写区区之忠以彻天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283522_comment'></div>有司以为不肖，竟从黜落，不得进望清光以遂昔愿，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>索手</span>东归，杜门求志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283522_comment'></div>因以为功名之在人，犹在己也：怀愚负计，而不以裨上之万一，是忿世也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283522_comment'></div>有君如此而忠言之不进，是匿情也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283522_comment'></div>己无他心而防人之疑，是自信不笃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283522_comment'></div>故书其《中兴论》一千八百馀言，大体<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>大略</span>，于斯见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283522_comment'></div>并论开诚、执要、励臣、正体之道，合五篇，上干天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283522_comment'></div>惟陛下宽其万死，不以为草茅之言而留神财幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283522_comment'></div>是天下社稷之福也，于臣何有！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1283522_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年4月</a>　春四月，为王晦叔跋米芾帖。作品：跋米元章帖。<div id='poem_1283520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋米元章帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283520")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283520'>本朝诗文字画之盛，到元祐更无着手处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283520_comment'></div>元章以晚辈一旦驰骤诸公间，声光烨然，此帖亦可窥一斑乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283520_comment'></div>淳熙己亥四月之晦，龙川陈亮为先友之子王晦叔书之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1283520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　春，撰汪夫人曹氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汪夫人曹氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283708")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283708'>绍兴癸亥岁，从事郎金华汪公浃，自江州德化县主簿罢归，久之，以是岁卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283708_comment'></div>其后葬邑之庆云乡所谓东弥坞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283708_comment'></div>又三十有五年，当淳熙丁酉三月辛亥，其配曹氏卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283708_comment'></div>子泌等将以己亥二月丙申举而合葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283708_comment'></div>先事，泌以母夫人行实一通哭授其子俊臣，奔走以告永康陈亮曰：「泌愿有谒于子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283708_comment'></div>泌之母葬有日矣，惟是不得离其柩跣行以谒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283708_comment'></div>昔者先伯氏有子，实婚于陈氏，于泌之母为诸妇，阃内之事不能以欺子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283708_comment'></div>吾子幸而赐之铭，以宣昭先懿，使后此千百载不知其为汪氏之时犹赖以存其墓，岂惟以掩蔽其孤之不肖，而异时姓字又获比数，故愿吾子之哀泌也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283708_comment'></div>亮顿首对客以「不能」辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283708_comment'></div>又念君之力足以取一时有名位者之辞以自厌满；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283708_comment'></div>假如足以及君所言，犹且不敢，况又非所及乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283708_comment'></div>俊臣奉其父命，缕缕不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283708_comment'></div>亮复以为「意方热时，忽忽不自觉尔，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1283708", 1283708, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>久后</span>固将大悔，第归熟计之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283708_comment'></div>亮退而读其状，见其所载主簿公与其兄将仕义居三十年，闺门<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283708", 1283708, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>肃睦</span>，如其为父子之居者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283708_comment'></div>将仕凡三娶，先后之姓不能以皆同，而夫人处之如一姒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283708_comment'></div>主簿殁时，夫人年方四十，四男两女皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283708_comment'></div>夫人缉理门户，咸有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283708", 1283708, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>节法</span>，过者不知其寡居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283708_comment'></div>蚤夜自躬其劳，以进其男子于学，女子非女功不辄习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283708_comment'></div>故泌与其弟天锡、澄、溥皆令入粟补官，以试其艺业于计台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283708_comment'></div>女之长者，以归奉议郎通判宁国军府事王统；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283708_comment'></div>次嫁时诠，诠固大家子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283708_comment'></div>不幸天锡、澄、溥皆相继先夫人而亡，夫人又为之存抚其孤儿，使各各有立，视其父之存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283708_comment'></div>今其孙九人，曰正臣、表臣、俊臣、廷臣、尧臣、良臣、鼎臣、周臣、舜臣者，皆能不废书册以自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283708_comment'></div>女孙十六人，其三人已嫁，杨潨、王杞、曹蒙，其婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283708_comment'></div>杞为承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283708_comment'></div>使主簿而在，所以处其子若孙者，宜不过如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283708_comment'></div>然夫人不自以为功，每曰：「是其先君之遗泽也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283708_comment'></div>晚岁，一切委事于二三妇，又如不谙其有家者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283708_comment'></div>其他闺闱细碎，可纪尚多，与亮所闻皆合，然后知亮之果不足以任此铭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283708_comment'></div>既而泌以书来，曰：「泌宁独不悔而已，苟不得，不止也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283708_comment'></div>乃叙次而使刻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283708_comment'></div>曹氏在金华为良大家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283708_comment'></div>曾大父随，大父介，父韶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283708_comment'></div>夫人享年若干岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283708_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1283708'>在昔夫存，视其弟昆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283708_comment'></div>其居既寡，视子若孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283708_comment'></div>既老而休，则视诸妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283708_comment'></div>死则已矣，视此韵语。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1283708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年10月</a>　冬十月，送严起叔之广东，有序。作品：送严起叔之官序。<div id='poem_1283484' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283484' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283484?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送岩起叔之官序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283484")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283484_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283484'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283484'>陈氏以财豪于乡旧矣，甫五世而子孙散落，往往失其所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283484", 1283484, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>庇依</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283484_comment'></div>其盛衰相寻于无穷，岂必其人之罪哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283484_comment'></div>吾叔岩起以未冠之年，慨然有狭乡闾之志，奋臂出游，往来于江淮之东西而定居于临安者，大较馀三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283484_comment'></div>诸公贵人，其未达而旅处者，岩起或出力以自效，或终日相与嬉游，不问其官崇卑，一接以恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283484_comment'></div>盖既贵而能相记忆，虽相忘而不见及者，皆所不较也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283484_comment'></div>亮以是知士非有侠气者，岂能奋空拳以自托其身于一世哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283484_comment'></div>晚得一官，将就食于广东部使者之麾下，冒寒挈妻子而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283484_comment'></div>问其行装，则曰：「我固索手自奋者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283484_comment'></div>然世态日异，此行虽我亦忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283484_comment'></div>子尝论交于四方，其何以为我道地乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283484_comment'></div>亮因告之曰：「四方之豪俊，不鄙而辱与之游者，不知其几人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283484_comment'></div>然自索居以来，黜陟不知，书问断绝，将何所指名而告语之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283484_comment'></div>亮又力不足者，徒能浡然兴怀，姑次第其语，以为送行序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283484_comment'></div>道逢其与亮游者，出以示之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283484_comment'></div>其藐然而无意者，必非与亮游者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283484_comment'></div>吾叔其勉之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283484_comment'></div>堂堂大国，一行数千里，岂无一英特知义之人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283484_comment'></div>使壮士困于泥涂，则其耻有归矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283484_comment'></div>淳熙六载冬十月朔，永康陈亮书于恕斋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1283484_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　冬，撰周叔辩夫妇祔葬墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283686' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283686' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283686?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周叔辩夫妻祔葬墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283686")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283686_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283686'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283686'>周氏不知其所从来，或曰由建安徙处之缙云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283686_comment'></div>然自讳元者徙居永康之上衢，于今可考者五世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283686_comment'></div>元生谓，谓生琛，琛生褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283686_comment'></div>世有吉德，不竞利于其乡，而衣食财取足，故乡人无憾于周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283686_comment'></div>然褒死于辛丑之乱，所存惟妇人女子，其祸亦惨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283686_comment'></div>又得其弟之子若讷字叔辩者为之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283686_comment'></div>叔辩之吉德，视父祖有加焉，此岂所谓天定者耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283686_comment'></div>然叔辩又无子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283686_comment'></div>其母弟谦，既已出后从父矣，叔辩以其子晃为子，晃左右就养无违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283686_comment'></div>叔辩得年七十有六，晏然逝去，实淳熙己亥八月之六日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283686_comment'></div>先是，其妻黄氏，以丁酉七月九日盖年八十而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283686_comment'></div>夫妻以寿考瞑目，可以观晃之为子矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283686_comment'></div>天人交际之理，厥应不忒，而变化倚伏，要之于其终可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283686_comment'></div>兄弟之子，独非吾子耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283686_comment'></div>形骸一隔而尔汝判然，虽圣人亦末如之何矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283686_comment'></div>始，叔辩尝出求仕，事不如意，辄弃去不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283686_comment'></div>其所后之父有女子三人，尽以其产自随，斥其毫末以与叔辩，已又以势夺之，叔辩亦不较也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283686_comment'></div>叔辩与先大父俱娶黄氏，视亮盖诸孙行，而待之如尊客，虽其他小儿亦未尝易侮之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283686_comment'></div>及若亲戚之贫者，不独不替其礼，又欲忘其力之不足而卵翼之，今之读书为士者，往往多未之及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283686_comment'></div>故吾于叔辩，敢不论天人之理以待后之君子乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283686_comment'></div>叔辩所后之母施氏，块然独葬于去家一里之坡上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283686_comment'></div>叔辩尝登墓喟然顾子孙而叹：「他日必葬我夫妻于其侧，以明所后之义」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283686_comment'></div>晃不敢违，以十有二月十三日祔葬，而问铭于同邑陈亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283686_comment'></div>其辞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1283686'>母居其中，子左妇右，既绝复续，以昌其后。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1283686_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1179&endYear=1179')">1179年</a>　为姨母周夫人撰墓志铭。作品：周夫人黄氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283709' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283709' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283709?labeling=true' target='_blank'>周夫人黄氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1179年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283709")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283709_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283709'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283709'>亮外大父閤门宣赞舍人黄公大圭，自其父训武公琫，当妖贼炽甚时，以死捍乡里，而舍人公亦能擒虏别将以自见，故黄氏在永康为闻家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283709_comment'></div>舍人六男，皆早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283709_comment'></div>长女嫁同邑陈氏，是为我先夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283709_comment'></div>次女年十有四，则嫁同邑周晃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283709_comment'></div>三男：曰扩，曰扬，曰抗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283709_comment'></div>两女：一以归亮之弟充，一归缙云潜万中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283709_comment'></div>又三十有三年，以淳熙己亥六月二十有四日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283709_comment'></div>其年十有二月二十三日，葬于去家十里长兰山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283709_comment'></div>其地盖属缙云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283709_comment'></div>其女兄之子实铭其圹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283709_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1283709'>痛父家之将遂沦坠，念夫家之未有显者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283709_comment'></div>覆厚土于其藏，尔后人其勿舍。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1283709_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　是岁，说《易》，《春秋》，《周礼》，吕祖谦恨未得听教。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　五月，周必大任参知政事。亮与之书，论年荒及时事。作品：与周参政必大书。<div id='poem_1283421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与周立义参政<span class='inlineComment2'>（葵）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283421")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283421'>仆愚不肖，百罔一有，顾尝习为文字，用以获知于门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283421_comment'></div>自惟无以报称，每思求天下之贤士，致之于公门，使本朝诸公不得擅美于前，斯亦仆区区报称万一之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283421_comment'></div>故向者辄诵其所知，而执事未辱留念；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283421_comment'></div>敢复拔其尤者而论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283421_comment'></div>左宣教郎胡权，研《六经》之旨要，得圣人之心传，持身端方，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1283421", 1283421, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>俯仰无愧</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283421_comment'></div>若置之讲劝之地，当有以增助君德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283421_comment'></div>左文林郎王道，强学力行，内严外顺，通究民情之利病，明于事体之是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283421_comment'></div>若置之论议之地，当有以资补时政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283421_comment'></div>左朝奉郎叶衡，右迪功郎孙伯虎，文章<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283421", 1283421, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>清古</span>，议论正当，临机明敏，莅政公方，化顽猾而有条，处剧烦而不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283421_comment'></div>衡见知临安之于潜，百姓未尝有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1283421", 1283421, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>翻词</span>至府，一境之内，风化肃然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283421_comment'></div>伯虎尉婺之永康，民有词讼，皆请于州，愿决之于尉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283421_comment'></div>及摄邑事，民相戒无以曲事至县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283421_comment'></div>此皆众耳目之所共知，非仆敢为过言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283421_comment'></div>若置之繁难之地，必能随机处置，井井有理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283421_comment'></div>凡兹四人，皆当今人材中可以一二数者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283421_comment'></div>执事傥论荐之于朝，天下将翕然以为得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283421_comment'></div>苟一口以为不然，仆亦当得诛绝于门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283421_comment'></div>今丑虏未灭，边防尚扰，财匮兵乏，士怨民离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283421_comment'></div>执事方当大政，宜日夜搜求人才，致之于朝，以共办兹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283421_comment'></div>倘曰「京局未有阙员，姑为后图」，日复一日而事去矣，虽伊、吕更生，亦何救哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283421_comment'></div>区区之心，如此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283421_comment'></div>伏惟钧慈，特加裁察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1283421_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8757925f7dde408ea33bfd0a619231b8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8757925f7dde408ea33bfd0a619231b8");'><span id='8757925f7dde408ea33bfd0a619231b8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1181')">1180-1181年</a>，38-39岁</div><div id='8757925f7dde408ea33bfd0a619231b8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　冬，为义乌喻夫人撰改葬墓志铭，喻夫人之子孙皆从陈亮学。作品：喻夫人王氏改葬墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喻夫人王氏改葬墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283707")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283707'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283707'>往时义乌何茂恭以文称，乡人之欲铭其墓者必属笔于茂恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283707_comment'></div>余犹记乾道初，余就姻茂恭家，见茂恭铭其从母王夫人之墓，其文工甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283707_comment'></div>茂恭口诵一二过，余能随记其文，复为客道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283707_comment'></div>茂恭抚掌欢笑：「世有强记如此者」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283707_comment'></div>今十四五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283707_comment'></div>当淳熙庚子，夫人之夫喻君夏卿将以十月二十七日改葬夫人于智者乡雷公山之下，以茂恭旧所为铭文示余，求改葬志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283707_comment'></div>茂恭死八九年，其文愈可贵重，余读其所为铭文，为坠泪久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283707_comment'></div>余安能志人之墓，况又能于茂恭文外更着笔耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283707_comment'></div>第以夏卿一子三孙从余学，无辞以却夏卿之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283707_comment'></div>夏卿四子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283707_comment'></div>次子大方早夭，其孤遐老又夭，妇陈氏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1283707", 1283707, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>守义</span>不去，以桧老为嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283707_comment'></div>夏卿与夫人又以长子义方之子槐老重慰安之，下至房帏碎事，夫人不使陈氏有所憾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283707_comment'></div>义方早丧妇，一女又孤，夫人亦命陈氏母之，惟留子楠老一人，故义方安于再娶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283707_comment'></div>知方有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283707", 1283707, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>瘖疾</span>，夫人怜之，亦令得所配。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283707_comment'></div>夫人在时，有子梼老，今又有林老者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283707_comment'></div>夫人最爱幼子汝方，勉使为学而已，卒不以一事损其均平之德，独以不及见其有子为恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283707_comment'></div>今有子四人，曰榉老、榆老、樠老、槿老，而汝方亦能以学问自见于乡闾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283707_comment'></div>楠老今名宏，有俊称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283707_comment'></div>桧老名宪，能经纪家事而不废学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283707_comment'></div>槐老名演，郡以其名上礼部：而夫人皆不能待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283707_comment'></div>两女，嫁商克忠、赵悌，丰约一取命于夏卿，夫人止计其女功所当为者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283707_comment'></div>彼其一家之所以和平而无间言，虽夏卿处之有道，而夫人之为虑亦甚密。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283707_comment'></div>其大略之可言者如此，而余不及知其详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283707_comment'></div>茂恭之所已载者，今皆不著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283707_comment'></div>茂恭名恪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283707_comment'></div>夏卿名上从师，下则余先祖私讳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283707_comment'></div>而余永康陈亮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283707_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1283707'>一夫一妇，本无可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283707_comment'></div>有子及孙，如十指然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283707_comment'></div>生既无一毫之憾，死以著夫人之贤。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1283707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　吕祖谦来永康，访陈亮于寿山石洞，与讲其所学，陈、吕门人翕然向往。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年5月</a>　五月，郑景望还永嘉，陈亮与徐居厚于馆头迎候。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e7b5a07be98b4839a439d7321dbc26e9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e7b5a07be98b4839a439d7321dbc26e9");'><span id='e7b5a07be98b4839a439d7321dbc26e9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1183')">1181-1183年</a>，39-41岁</div><div id='e7b5a07be98b4839a439d7321dbc26e9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年9月</a>　秋九月，宰相王淮荐朱熹提举浙东常平盐茶公事，即日就道。朱熹至永康访陈亮，互究所学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　秋，为门人方元卿撰墓志铭。作品：方元卿墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>方元卿墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283684")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283684'>谱牒之不明久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283684_comment'></div>卿士大夫能谱其世家，使始末可考见者，盖仅有之，而况崛起田庐，能由其所起之祖，至或一二百年而不坠，是亦可尚已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283684_comment'></div>浦江真溪之方氏，自其讳耸者奋以有家，至其子超，孙允脩，资日以钜，遂为邑之望族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283684_comment'></div>允脩之子彦老，守其先人之业，能以尺度自律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283684_comment'></div>天资恕厚，与人无怨恶，不求甚美以自侈，亦不慕非人情所有之美以求名声，期自出于先世之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283684_comment'></div>盖其自处者求无甚愧于心而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283684_comment'></div>是真《易》之所谓「克家」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283684_comment'></div>其字曰元卿，生于宣和癸卯之二月二十八日，殁于淳熙六年之十月二十五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283684_comment'></div>娶柳氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283684_comment'></div>子男三人：友益、温、友贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283684_comment'></div>温后君三年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283684_comment'></div>女三人：归东阳贡士单肖，钱伯明，朱宗祐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283684_comment'></div>孙男四人：坦、概，馀幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283684_comment'></div>孙女六人，其一归毛友多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283684_comment'></div>坦尝从余游，一日，其父来视坦，每进见，亦若诸生然，其恭而笃于教子若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283684_comment'></div>今将以淳熙八年九月十二日葬君于邑之政内乡大姑之原，而以墓石累余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283684_comment'></div>余惧后世不知永康陈亮之为谁，而况能及君乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283684_comment'></div>盖自昔常如此，而人终未悟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283684_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1283684'>不坠先业，以勉其身，其馀以待后人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1283684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　冬，撰胡公济墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>胡公济墓碣铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283683")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283683'>东阳胡公济年四十七而丧其配，悉以其家事付子绩，而筑庵以居，不复作世间念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283683_comment'></div>然犹铢积寸累，别为田数百亩，曰：「吾为诸孙地也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283683_comment'></div>释氏以理为障，以身为幻，以孙子为赘，其于君臣父子兄弟夫妇之大伦，一切废弃而不论，专求其所谓出世间法者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283683_comment'></div>夫既已有身矣，则世其可出乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283683_comment'></div>世不可出，则安得而无孙子之情乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283683_comment'></div>以公济之志，足以知所取舍如此，宜其享有福寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283683_comment'></div>盖年八十有一，康强无疾而终，里闾有遗思焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283683_comment'></div>余闻公济少颇自豪，家故饶财，入手则净尽不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283683_comment'></div>既而小用其志能，家道辄如初，又复能藏锋以休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283683_comment'></div>公济于余为大父行，及际其晚岁泊然之时，睹其风貌敦厚，气质<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1283683", 1283683, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>凝重</span>，可以想像承平之里闾遗老，而惜不及其壮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283683_comment'></div>子绩，字彦功，与先人俱娶黄氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283683_comment'></div>彦功端然坐家，为里闾信服，不啻官府，能光显公济馀业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283683_comment'></div>此其父子皆有过人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283683_comment'></div>余伤其有能之不试，而彦功又将老矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283683_comment'></div>天地之正气发泄于人，而里闾之所易见者已不满人意如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283683_comment'></div>彼其遗憾果何在，亦可以人之思虑所及而参酌其中，以应天地之运乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283683_comment'></div>又将有大于此者，则亦同此慨叹而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283683_comment'></div>今年春正月十有四日，彦功既禫，又十二月癸酉，葬公济于家旁之北山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283683_comment'></div>葬罢，将刻铭墓上，以其辞委余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283683_comment'></div>余固心知彦功者，居相邻，亲相属焉，其奚辞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283683_comment'></div>胡氏得姓，所从来甚远，且与陈为同姓，其谱系远不可记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283683_comment'></div>有讳远者，始居东阳永康之间，至公济之父，遂大其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283683_comment'></div>公济讳航。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283683_comment'></div>娶戚氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283683_comment'></div>子男一人，绩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283683_comment'></div>女二人，嫁蔡牺、陈扩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283683_comment'></div>孙男四人：廷芝、廷茂、廷芬、廷芳，业进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283683_comment'></div>孙女四人：嫁从政郎梁竦，承信郎陈兖，将仕郎曹致中，进士黄公辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283683_comment'></div>曾孙男女合二十五人，玄孙一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283683_comment'></div>于是淳熙八改岁矣，永康陈亮为铭其石曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1283683'>士以文进，异能尽废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283683_comment'></div>我铭之悲，独一公济！</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1283683_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　和赵周锡作《水调歌头》（事业随人品）<span class='inlineComment2'>（该词难系年，以赵周锡仕历观之，疑或作于乾道末淳熙初，即1171至1181年间，姑附于此。）</span><div id='poem_157214' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157214' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157214?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头 和赵周锡</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157214")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157214_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157214'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157214'>事业随人品，今古几麾旌。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157214'>向来谋国，万事尽出汝书生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157214'>安识鹍鹏变化，九万里风在下，如许上南溟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157214'>斥鴳旁边笑，河汉一头倾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157214_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157214'>叹世间，多少恨，几时平。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157214'>霸图消歇，大家创见又成惊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157214'>邂逅汉家龙种，正尔乌纱白纻，驰骛觉身轻。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157214_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157214'>樽酒从渠说，双眼为谁明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157214_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年</a>　怀叶八十推官作《踏莎行》（书册如仇）<span class='inlineComment2'>（叶八十推官疑为叶适，此阕当作于淳熙五年（1178）后两三年，姑附于此。）</span><div id='poem_157273' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157273' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157273?labeling=true' target='_blank'>踏莎行 怀叶八十推官</a><span class='authorDate'>（1181年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157273")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157273_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157273'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157273'>书册如仇，旧游浑讳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157273'>有怀不断人应异。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157273'>千山上去梦魂轻，片帆似下蛮溪水。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157273_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157273'>已共杯酒，长坚海誓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157273'>见君忽忘花前醉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157273_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157273'>从来解事苦无多，不知解到毫芒未。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_157273_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　春正月，朱熹巡历婺州、衢州，陈亮访其于衢、婺间，旬日乃别。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年3月4日</a>　三月初四巳时，得一男。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　夏，婺州大旱，有书信致朱熹述旱灾，并附杂论五篇，请朱熹评阅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　做石井祈雨文。<div id='poem_1283796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>石井祈雨文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283796")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283796'>惟龙伸缩变化，吁吸云雨，一潭之间，龙则安焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283796_comment'></div>民有不告，其答如响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283796_comment'></div>惟此境被龙之泽旧矣，岁一不周，亦龙之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283796_comment'></div>龙之泽不终朝而被天下，十里之间嗷嗷如此，岂龙之所安乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283796_comment'></div>油然之云雨既有绪，起而成之，何啻反掌之易也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1283796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　撰祈雨文。作品：佑顺侯祈雨文。<div id='poem_1283798' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283798' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283798?labeling=true' target='_blank'>佑顺侯祈雨文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283798")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283798_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283798'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283798'>民至愚也，而独虔于神，苟可以用其勤者，虽发肤有所不爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283798_comment'></div>神亦察其愚而矜之，往往辄应，故民之言神者多异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283798_comment'></div>惟神之正大，岂为异以惊动夫愚民哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283798_comment'></div>人情皇皇，其势自尔，而非神之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283798_comment'></div>亮于民之中又愚之尤者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283798_comment'></div>平居不能事神，缓急亦将有求于神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283798_comment'></div>顾何时而必神之答？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283798_comment'></div>乃其心以为丛祠相望，灵响百出，其异不足依；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283798_comment'></div>可尊而信者惟神，正大而不为异者惟神，以昔圣贤所以恻然兴仁、泽人利物、而不蕲乎报者而望乎神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283798_comment'></div>今苗稼焦然，一日二日不雨，苗且槁死，藁秸将不能以及牛马，神宁忍闻此而惜一举足之力哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283798_comment'></div>故亮率其徒敬拜祠下，而致其心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283798_comment'></div>于其间又有为浮屠之法以乞灵于神者，彼其心以为舍此无所用其诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283798_comment'></div>亮之力不足以达神之心，一切听其所以自致者，危窘至此，神宜如何矜之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283798_comment'></div>凡相与而来者，察其心皆无所爱，独亮期神以正大之事，始末不渝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283798_comment'></div>神不亮听，于亮自为得其分，顾民之置神于异者终不已，而神之事果非亮之所能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283798_comment'></div>亮足未尝登此岩也，而心独至焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283798_comment'></div>今兹来登而又不答，岂惟望于世者狭，而望于神者亦狭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283798_comment'></div>敢有再渎，神则殛之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1283798_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　问答撰成。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　冬，为金华刘夫人撰墓志铭。作品：刘夫人陈氏墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见颜虚心《宋陈龙川先生亮年谱》第80页。）</span><div id='poem_1283710' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283710' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283710?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘夫人陈氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1182年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283710")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283710_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283710'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283710'>夫人陈姓，世居婺之金华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283710_comment'></div>曾大父良直，大父忠，父文德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283710_comment'></div>年十九，嫁同邑刘君大礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283710_comment'></div>生男三人：淮、渊、演。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283710_comment'></div>女三人，长适杨颋，次在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283710_comment'></div>嫁之三十二年，当淳熙壬寅七月二十五日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283710_comment'></div>其年十有二月一日丁酉，葬邑之庆云乡杉塘原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283710_comment'></div>先葬，渊以刘君之命问铭于永康陈亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283710_comment'></div>数年以来，亮以与世不合，甘自放弃于田夫樵子之间，誓将老死而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283710_comment'></div>一日，金华二三子相寻萧寺中，问其旧学为何事，使人惘然如有所失坠，思欲温旧起废，而忘其志念之既落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283710_comment'></div>其一人则渊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283710_comment'></div>今年春，渊之母夫人疾既笃矣，然犹往来不辍，朝记夕省，若学之不可以顷刻已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283710_comment'></div>问其故，则曰：「吾母之志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283710_comment'></div>未几而遂死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283710_comment'></div>余悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283710_comment'></div>推此道也，则所以事其舅姑以及其夫者，宜其皆可观，而其详不得而具也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283710_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1283710'>不自悯病，而淑其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283710_comment'></div>曰母之爱，则有馀美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283710_comment'></div>是其藏也，可以诏千万年者未耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283710_comment'></div>言之不文，理则近是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283710_comment'></div>在尔后之人，尚其克嗣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1283710_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　为伯祖廷俊作墓志铭。作品：陈府君廷俊墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见颜虚心《宋陈龙川先生亮年谱》第80页。）</span><div id='poem_1283688' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283688' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283688?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈府君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283688")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283688_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283688'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283688'>永康之陈，大抵派自吴兴，盖其所从来远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283688_comment'></div>其居邑之南四十五里曰前黄者，远事今皆不论，论其耳目之所及者：溯亮而数之，凡八世，而亮年适四十矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283688_comment'></div>三十年得一世，其间又有过二十而得子者，陈氏于今往往近二百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283688_comment'></div>虽不能驰骤取功名富贵以自见于斯世，而衣食丰足，推其馀以及邻里，使一乡无憾于陈氏，盖自六世祖讳伯援，而邑人始有称焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283688_comment'></div>更三世而守其家法，终始不坠，惟最长一支为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283688_comment'></div>百四五十年之间，衣被国家之饱煖，大家世族或已沦替而无馀，而一乡之望凝然如一日，此岂无所由致哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283688_comment'></div>亮之曾祖，幼丧其父，而高祖母以盛年守志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283688_comment'></div>于是六世祖老矣，家事悉以委之长子，讳文什，实能抚孤存寡，义不以一毫自私，使高祖母儿女之累释然终老而不悔者，恃其夫之有兄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283688_comment'></div>及曾祖死于王事，而先祖兄弟以摧丧之馀暴当门户，凛然惧不自保，而曾伯祖讳良佐实存抚之，所以终其父之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283688_comment'></div>其后先祖病废，先人常有不胜家事之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283688_comment'></div>曾伯祖之子廷俊与其继室叶氏，实左右有家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283688_comment'></div>人事固多故，而吾家三世被其三世之德，其大者可念而不可忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283688_comment'></div>公讳廷俊，字时乂，尝以纳粟辟尉靖之永平，然非其好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283688_comment'></div>先娶同邑吕氏，盖甚宜其家，而不幸早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283688_comment'></div>子男三人：克恭、克勤、克诚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283688_comment'></div>女三人：适汪注、胡炳、徐良史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283688_comment'></div>孙男九人，恂、亢、亨、慥、光、恪、几、允、恺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283688_comment'></div>女三人：长适徐士龙，次卢垕，次幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283688_comment'></div>曾孙女二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283688_comment'></div>公生于大观戊子三月十有八日，殁于乾道戊子五月二十六日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283688_comment'></div>而男女之长者与公相继而卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283688_comment'></div>又十有五年冬十月十有二日己酉，始克葬公于距家五里鸡鸣山先茔之旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283688_comment'></div>论次本末，以纳诸幽，诸孤以为责当在亮，谨再拜而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283688_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1283688'>生而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1283688", 1283688, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>敦庞</span>，以壮门户；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283688_comment'></div>长则克家，以光厥祖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283688_comment'></div>世有隐德，细犹未数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283688_comment'></div>天道昭然，归安此土。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1283688_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　朱熹按唐仲友不法，唐疑陈亮相谮。陈亮致书朱熹声辩。作品：癸卯与朱元晦通书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　七月，妻父何恢（茂宏）卒，为文祭之。作品：祭妻父何茂宏文。<div id='poem_1283750' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283750' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283750?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭妻父何茂宏文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283750")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283750_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283750'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283750'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283750_comment'></div>既以有生，安得无死！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283750_comment'></div>自死自生，滔滔皆是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283750_comment'></div>生既非真，死亦云妄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283750_comment'></div>超出死生，是名实相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283750_comment'></div>惟彼圣贤，其道则殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283750_comment'></div>不使生死，总之为虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283750_comment'></div>生如不生，麋鹿与俱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283750_comment'></div>死则死矣，木石之枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283750_comment'></div>生事爱敬，死事哀戚，人道始终，一用其极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283750_comment'></div>前贤未辨，我任其责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283750_comment'></div>责苟在我，有死无易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283750_comment'></div>昔公少年，相父起家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283750_comment'></div>食不厌粗，衣不慕华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283750_comment'></div>父死我在，事靡有他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283750_comment'></div>或费或啬，先志未遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283750_comment'></div>欲知其人，视其家道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283750_comment'></div>以其馀力，发为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1283750", 1283750, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>辞藻</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283750_comment'></div>两登荐书，门户华好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283750_comment'></div>迄用有成，难弟敏妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283750_comment'></div>家日昌矣，而弟遽亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283750_comment'></div>弟有遗责，并此乎当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283750_comment'></div>同时孰在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283750_comment'></div>彼俊者郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283750_comment'></div>笔砚其间，而视茫茫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283750_comment'></div>既老未休，心非外慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283750_comment'></div>不耋之嗟，莫求其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283750_comment'></div>纵不尊荣，终此大数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283750_comment'></div>无宁少留，观我常度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283750_comment'></div>唯公平生，皎然不欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283750_comment'></div>质直敢前，恭俭自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283750_comment'></div>无疾而逝，胡宁有疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283750_comment'></div>死生大矣，不足与移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283750_comment'></div>某独何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283750_comment'></div>感念昔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283750_comment'></div>托我以女，匪其可且。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283750_comment'></div>幸能谋食，于道未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283750_comment'></div>晚蒙公知，异礼是假。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283750_comment'></div>言疏意拙，忠故不舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283750_comment'></div>二十年间，付之土苴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283750_comment'></div>持此丹心，对越泉下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283750_comment'></div>尚想音容，酒倾泪洒。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1283750_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年9月15日</a>　九月十五日，作《水调歌头》寿朱熹。（人物从来少）<div id='poem_157215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157215' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157215?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头 癸卯九月十五日寿朱元晦</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年9月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157215")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157215_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157215'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157215'>人物从来少，篱菊为谁黄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157215'>去年今日，倚楼还是听行藏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157215'>未觉霜风无赖，好在月华如水，心事楚天长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157215'>讲论参洙泗，杯酒到虞唐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157215_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157215'>人未醉，歌宛转，兴悠扬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157215'>太平胸次，笑他<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_157215", 157215, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>磊磈</span>欲成狂。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157215'>且向武夷深处，坐对云烟开敛，逸思入微茫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157215'>我欲为君寿，何许得新腔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157215_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　为同邑陈性之撰墓志铭，性之子颐从陈亮学。作品：陈性之墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（一说《陈性之墓志铭》撰于淳熙十三年（1186），参见颜虚心《宋陈龙川先生亮年谱》第108页。）</span><div id='poem_1283680' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283680' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283680?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈性之墓碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283680")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283680_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283680'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283680'>往尝论乡之富人，以陈性之为第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283680_comment'></div>吾友徐元德居厚亦知此翁可人意，而乐妻其少女焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283680_comment'></div>居厚以对策切直，得从事浙东观察府，竟以不能曲折上官罢去，独<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283680", 1283680, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>敬惮</span>性之，盖相处数年如一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283680_comment'></div>余尝款性之门，阒然如无人声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283680_comment'></div>顷之，一僮出，问客姓氏，已而肃客入，主人相与为礼，已而杯盘罗至，终不见喧嘈之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283680_comment'></div>性之面目严冷，与人寡合，虽大会集，率不过三数客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283680_comment'></div>遇有所往，虽百里夜半，亦疾驰竟归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283680_comment'></div>一日，与乡士大夫过予，自命行庖具饭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283680_comment'></div>食毕，从容言曰：「某素不解饮，一饱之外，虽留何用」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283680_comment'></div>予亦不强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283680_comment'></div>衣食取足，不为分外经营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283680_comment'></div>不交涉邑官吏，谒入县庭，则不问可以知其令之贤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283680_comment'></div>盖其自为过多，为人过少，若有取于杨朱之道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283680_comment'></div>然予闻性之官剑浦，乡人陈公质且老，而羁置在焉，性之曲意抚存之，使之自忘其为罗戾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283680_comment'></div>居亡何，公质死，性之还自旁郡，道逢兵马都监者往验其死，性之嘱以徐行：「有檄止君矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283680_comment'></div>性之亟趋郡白事，得追还其都监者，又为治其后事颇悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283680_comment'></div>盖古之义侠所谓「不以存亡为解」者，大率亦此类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283680_comment'></div>由此言之，士之素守里闾，曾不得少自概见于世者，岂必曰乡称善人而已乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283680_comment'></div>性之以赀补迪功郎，尝主南剑之剑浦簿，以忧去官，而不复调矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283680_comment'></div>性之陈氏，讳良能，性之其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283680_comment'></div>曾大父本，大父思忠，父填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283680_comment'></div>子男三人：琳、正己、颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283680_comment'></div>女四人：长适奉议郎詹宗尧，次曹钺，次何椿，季则徐氏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283680_comment'></div>孙男五人：大年、大任、恂、愉、明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283680_comment'></div>孙女七人：长适何源，次许嫁曹湘，馀幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283680_comment'></div>性之之配为胡氏，以淳熙四年六月二十七日卒，明年正月七日，葬邑之承训乡横渡山之东原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283680_comment'></div>又八年十有一月庚寅，性之始合葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283680_comment'></div>性之家故多竹，不以与人，多美器用，不轻以假人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283680_comment'></div>居厚每笑于余无所不可，墓上之铭，宜颐之有请也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283680_comment'></div>颐尝从予游，郡以其名上礼部，而性之死矣，盖癸卯十有二月七日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283680_comment'></div>得年凡七十岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283680_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1283680'>永康之陈，曰龙山，曰墓西，曰石牛，曰西门，皆尝有列于朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283680_comment'></div>曰白岩，曰前黄，则富尝甲于乡闾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283680_comment'></div>自君父祖崛起清渭，俨然遂为七族，而谱牒之相通则未有考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283680_comment'></div>宗法不立，难乎著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283680_comment'></div>起其宗者，以人而称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283680_comment'></div>有蓄不救，事特未定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283680_comment'></div>莫为之先，孰承斯庆？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283680_comment'></div>铭之存也，亦以令也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1283680_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4943f81219764565a76acee36bcda2cc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4943f81219764565a76acee36bcda2cc");'><span id='4943f81219764565a76acee36bcda2cc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1184')">1183-1184年</a>，41-42岁</div><div id='4943f81219764565a76acee36bcda2cc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　怀王道甫作《鹧鸪天》（落魄歌行记昔游）<span class='inlineComment2'>（该词系年难定，以词意测之，王道甫官位尚低，当在淳熙年间，不会逾淳熙十年（1183），姑附于此。）</span><div id='poem_157276' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157276' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157276?labeling=true' target='_blank'>鹧鸪天 怀王道甫</a><span class='authorDate'>（1183年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157276")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157276_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157276'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157276'>落魄行歌记昔游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157276'>头颅如许尚何求。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157276'>心肝吐尽无馀事，口腹安然岂远谋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157276_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157276'>才怕暑，又伤秋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157276'>天涯梦断有书不。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157276'>大都眼孔新来浅，羡尔微官作计周。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_157276_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_157276'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(157276)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　乡人宴会，同坐者归而暴亡，陈亮以药人之诬，再次下狱。经辛弃疾、罗点等营救，五月二十五日脱狱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　六月二日到家。后自妻家回，遭遇强盗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　为朱熹作画像赞。作品：朱晦庵画像赞。<div id='poem_1283669' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283669' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283669?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朱晦庵画像赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283669")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283669_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283669'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283669'>体备<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283669", 1283669, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>阳刚</span>之纯，气含喜怒之正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283669_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283669", 1283669, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>睟面盎背</span>，吾不知其何乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283669_comment'></div>端居深念，吾不知其何病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283669_comment'></div>置之钓台捺不住，写之云台捉不定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283669_comment'></div>天下之生久矣，以听上帝之正命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283669_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1283669_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　答朱熹书，为汉唐之辨。作品：甲辰答朱晦庵书。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8cb69af2e492434d9d5a07cffcc9a23c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8cb69af2e492434d9d5a07cffcc9a23c");'><span id='8cb69af2e492434d9d5a07cffcc9a23c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1185')">1184-1185年</a>，42-43岁</div><div id='8cb69af2e492434d9d5a07cffcc9a23c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　赋《蝶恋花》寿朱熹。（手撚黄花还自笑）<div id='poem_157272' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157272' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157272?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蝶恋花 甲辰寿元晦</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157272")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157272_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157272'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157272'>手撚黄花还自笑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157272'>笑比渊明，莫也归来早。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157272'>随世功名浑草草。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157272'>五湖却共繁华老。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157272_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157272'>冷淡家生冤得道。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157272'>旖旎妖娆，春梦如今觉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157272'>管今岁华须到了。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157272_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157272'>此花之后花应少。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157272_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　冬，撰孙天诚墓志铭。作品：孙天诚墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见颜虚心《宋陈龙川先生亮年谱》第90页。）</span><div id='poem_1283685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>孙天诚墓碣铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283685")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283685_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283685'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283685'>丙戌之春，乡人徐木子才、胡达可行仲，联登进士第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283685_comment'></div>方二君未第时，行仲之贫特甚，孙君天诚皆妻以女而左右之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283685_comment'></div>至是，莫不欢言孙君之知人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283685_comment'></div>孙君又自喜教其子，遇州县学时节校艺，孙氏子常不在三两人后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283685_comment'></div>予时尚少，罕与人接，亦知孙君能自别于他富人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283685_comment'></div>夫争名者于朝，争利者于市，而善致富者则曰：「人弃我取，人取我与」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283685_comment'></div>其抑扬阖辟盖加一等矣，然犹较尺短寸长于其冲也，孰能运其智力于不争之地，使范蠡计然之策一切在下风乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283685_comment'></div>盖余居之南十四五里，地虽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283685", 1283685, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>卤瘠</span>而非人之所必争，孙君乃自邑而徙居焉，勤取啬出，以尽有其土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283685_comment'></div>大较二十年间，富比他人，而省事过之，此其为富，有概于余心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283685_comment'></div>孙君讳亶，天诚其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283685_comment'></div>曾祖继先，祖无党，父轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283685_comment'></div>君生于崇宁乙酉十月二十有四日，殁于淳熙辛丑十二月十有三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283685_comment'></div>娶周氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283685_comment'></div>子男二人：长克和；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283685_comment'></div>次光祖，早死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283685_comment'></div>女四人：长归徐氏，次嫁赵端夫，次则胡氏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283685_comment'></div>季适梁季璿，故户部尚书汝嘉仲谋之诸孙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283685_comment'></div>归徐氏之女寻死，而子才既得邑定海矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283685_comment'></div>孙氏其先富春人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283685_comment'></div>方汉氏失道，海内相与竞智角力以觊非望，而曹孟德以盖世之雄执缚略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283685_comment'></div>孙讨逆盖破虏之子，翻然欲与之争锋，孟德盖甚难之，不幸早世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283685_comment'></div>仲谋据江东之地，因曹氏之篡，自帝一隅，使魏不得为正于天下，而天命不知所归者殆数百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283685_comment'></div>区区一时之自营，其所关系乃如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283685_comment'></div>及其四世之馀，子孙散落为民，分适旁郡，况又历七八百年，则其间何所不有！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283685_comment'></div>故来隶永康者，亦不能言其于今凡几世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283685_comment'></div>而克和将以甲辰冬十二月二十九日甲申，葬君于去家二里姚岭之原，以墓石委余。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283685_comment'></div>余悲夫盛衰兴废之相寻，长短小大之相形，而人之智于是出焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283685_comment'></div>要其事为有可言者，其于孙君安得而已乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283685_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1283685'>生垦其地，死营其旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283685_comment'></div>何以识之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283685_comment'></div>孙君之乡。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1283685_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1184&endYear=1184')">1184年</a>　撰钱叔因墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283696' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283696' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283696?labeling=true' target='_blank'>钱叔因墓碣铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1184年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283696")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283696'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283696'>绍兴辛巳、壬午之间，余以极论兵事，为一时明公巨臣之所许，而反授以《中庸》、《大学》之旨，余不能识也，而复以古文<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283696", 1283696, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>自诡</span>于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283696_comment'></div>道德性命之学亦渐开矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283696_comment'></div>又四五年，广汉张栻敬夫，东莱吕祖谦伯恭，相与上下其论，而皆有列于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283696_comment'></div>新安朱熹元晦讲之武夷，而强立不反，其说遂以行而不可遏止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283696_comment'></div>齿牙所至，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1283696", 1283696, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>嘘枯吹生</span>，天下之学士大夫贤不肖，往往系其意之所向背，虽心诚不乐而亦阳相应和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283696_comment'></div>若余非不愿附，而第其品级不能高也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283696_comment'></div>余亦自咎其有所不讲而未敢怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283696_comment'></div>壬辰、癸巳而贫日甚，欲托于讲授以为资身之策，乡闾识其素而不之信，众亦疑其学之非是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283696_comment'></div>而浦江钱氏之子扩来，曰：「扩于时文未之能，虽能亦不愿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283696_comment'></div>区区之意，欲学其所当学者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283696_comment'></div>余为之有慨于心，曰：「我亦将从此而学也，试与吾子共学之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283696_comment'></div>因以为：人眇然一身，与天地并立而为三才，其阙一不可之本为安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283696_comment'></div>又以为：洪荒之初，圣贤继作，道统日以脩明，虽时有治乱，而道无一日不在天下也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283696_comment'></div>而战国、秦、汉以来，千五百年之间，此道安在？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283696_comment'></div>而无一人能识其用，圣贤亦不复作，天下乃赖人之智力以维持，而道遂为不传之妙物，儒者又何从而得之，以尊其身而独立于天下？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283696_comment'></div>《六经》诸史，反复推究，以见天运人事流行参错之处，而识观象之妙，时措之宜，如长江大河，浑浑浩浩，尽收众流而万古不能尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283696_comment'></div>而后知人之职分，圣贤之所用心，而人心之危不可以一息而不操也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283696_comment'></div>苟有用心之地，则凡天下之学皆可因之以资吾之陟降上下焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283696_comment'></div>故易扩名曰廓而字叔因，以坚其共学之志，廓亦愿自奋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283696_comment'></div>廓于程文，亦姑以游戏云耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283696_comment'></div>癸卯之秋，与其侪辈试漕台，亦复得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283696_comment'></div>冬十有一月九日，乃死于龙窟山寺中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283696_comment'></div>其兄抑来，抚而哭之曰：「吾不信汝死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283696_comment'></div>汝死，是无天也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283696_comment'></div>遂取以去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283696_comment'></div>余哭之过时而悲，自伤其孑孑而莫我助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283696_comment'></div>甲辰之春，余亦颠倒于祸患，凡十年，而世亦无察其始末者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283696_comment'></div>某月某日，其兄始葬之其邑某乡某所之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283696_comment'></div>念欲揭廓之志以刻诸墓上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283696_comment'></div>其友淩坚数以趣余，曰：「是坚之责也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283696_comment'></div>廓少孤，其祖良臣日以老，兄抑实任家事，督廓以学，而一钱不以假之，旁观亦不能安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283696_comment'></div>廓曰：「兄爱我者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283696_comment'></div>人有言兄私自为计，则愤然责数之曰：「何为间我兄弟也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283696_comment'></div>兄必不尔，终不能动吾心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283696_comment'></div>钱物之到手有数，到，辄与朋友故旧，无分毫吝惜计较心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283696_comment'></div>尝以事为人绐钱三十万，仅得银十余两，置之行箧中；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283696_comment'></div>暮夜入邸舍，发箧而又失之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283696_comment'></div>人为廓叹息失声，廓笑曰：「是固已失之物也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283696_comment'></div>其于世故澹泊，孝友慈爱，出于天资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283696_comment'></div>使得共学以至于今，不但侪辈之不能及，固吾尊行之所共畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283696_comment'></div>尝与吾友瑞安叶适正则论后来学者，而有遗恨于廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283696_comment'></div>余尝铭廓父赞之墓，故略其世系，而系近世问学之离合，求正则书之，使来者有考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283696_comment'></div>余，永康陈亮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283696_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1283696'>三十而死，其志皎然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283696_comment'></div>有子曰颢，以听于天。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1283696_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　是岁，仍教书，贫病交加。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　写定《类次文中子序引》，作《书后》，并辑附录。作品：书文中附录后。<div id='poem_1283501' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283501' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283501?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书文中子附录后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1175年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283501")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283501_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283501'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283501'>《文中子世家》，阮氏本以为杜淹撰，龚氏本则曰福奖、福畤、福郊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283501_comment'></div>今虽不可考，而《世家》不可不录，故存其录而去其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283501_comment'></div>房、魏论礼乐事，出于福畤所录，虽其间语言不能无节，然参考太宗与诸公经营当时之事，宜必有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283501_comment'></div>今备存之，重去其旧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283501_comment'></div>以余观之，魏徵、杜淹之于文中子，盖尝有师友之义矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283501_comment'></div>如房、杜，直往来耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283501_comment'></div>故尝事文中子于河汾者，一切抄之，曰门人弟子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283501_comment'></div>其家子弟见诸公之盛也，又从而实之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283501_comment'></div>夫文中子之道，岂待诸公而后重哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283501_comment'></div>可谓不知其师其父者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283501_comment'></div>关子明之筮，同州府君实书而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283501_comment'></div>备其本末者，亦福畤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283501_comment'></div>世往往以其筮为怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283501_comment'></div>《易》有理有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283501_comment'></div>数，出于理者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283501_comment'></div>得其理足以知百世之变，明其数足以计<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1283501", 1283501, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>将来</span>之事，而又何怪焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283501_comment'></div>如子明之论人谋天命，有后世儒生之所不及知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283501_comment'></div>文中子家世之明王道，子明盖有助焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283501_comment'></div>龚氏安得以私意易之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283501_comment'></div>故存此三书，曰《文中子附录》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1283501_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　收复祖田二百亩。整治苑囿亭宇，种植花木，建燕坐、抱膝、小憩、房斋、赤水堂、独松堂等，致朱熹书欲求字。作品：答朱元晦秘书书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第61页。）</span><div id='poem_1283444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬寅答朱元晦秘书<span class='inlineComment2'>（熹）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283444")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283444'>山间获陪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>妙论</span>，往往尽出所闻之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283444_comment'></div>世途日狭，所赖以强人意者，惟秘书一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283444_comment'></div>平生有坐料人物世事之癖，今而后知其不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283444_comment'></div>别去惘然，如盲者之失杖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283444_comment'></div>意每有所不通，辄翘首东望，思欲飞动而未能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283444_comment'></div>方将专人问起居，乃承专翰之赐，蒙所以见念者甚至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283444_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>顽悖</span>为众所共弃，而嗜好之异乃有甚于伯恭者邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283444_comment'></div>既以自幸，深惧为门下知人不明之一累也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283444_comment'></div>惟时春事更深，按临有相，台候动止万福，慰甚不可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283444_comment'></div>某<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>顽钝</span>只如此，日逐且与后生寻行数墨，正如三四十岁丑女，更欲扎腰缚脚，不独可笑，亦良苦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283444_comment'></div>山妇过月始免身，以初四日巳时得一男，却幸母子完全，小下何足上劳尊念，愧感无已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283444_comment'></div>《战国策》、《论衡》、《日注》为贶，甚佳，敢不下拜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283444_comment'></div>《田说》读得一遍稍详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283444_comment'></div>若事体<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>全转</span>，所谓智者献其谋，其间可采取处亦多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283444_comment'></div>但谓有补于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>圆转</span>事体，则非某所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283444_comment'></div>居法度繁密之世，论事正不当如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283444_comment'></div>此亦一述朱耳，彼亦一述朱耳，欲以文书尽天下事情，此所以为荆扬之化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283444_comment'></div>度外之功，岂可以论说而致；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283444_comment'></div>百世之法，岂可以辏合而行乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283444_comment'></div>天下，大物也，须是自家气力可以斡得动，挟得转，则天下之智力无非吾之智力，形同趋而势同利，虽异类可使不约而从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283444_comment'></div>若只欲安坐而感动之，向来诸君子固已失之偏矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283444_comment'></div>今欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>斗饤</span>而发施之，后来诸君子无乃又失之碎乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283444_comment'></div>论理论事，若箍桶然，此某所不解也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283444_comment'></div>秘书<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>挺特</span>崇深，自拔于党类之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283444_comment'></div>岁晚庶得一快，方自委托，岂敢怀不尽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283444_comment'></div>意之所到，虽缕缕未止，有不然者，却望见教，某不任至望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1283444_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　为妻父何（恢）茂宏撰墓志铭。作品：何茂宏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283687' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283687' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283687?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何茂宏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span
