class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283687")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283687_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283687'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283687'>公姓何氏，讳恢，字茂宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283687_comment'></div>得姓所从来甚远，而婺之诸何为尤盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283687_comment'></div>居城之东，而散出永康、东阳、义乌者，其分合之详不可得而纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283687_comment'></div>然义乌之族，自公而上，其可数者六世，而公又有子有孙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283687_comment'></div>公之曾大父京，始葬其父祖于官塘之东西两偏，又营其地而居之，浚其塘至百馀亩，以尽有其四旁之壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283687_comment'></div>两子，其次讳先，是生公之父，讳矩，以志气自豪，尝欲奋于武事，得官河北之恩州，而公生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283687_comment'></div>故公状貌端厚，意象<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1283687", 1283687, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>轩耸</span>，而胸次疏豁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283687_comment'></div>是非长短，人得以望而知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283687_comment'></div>读书为文，亦不肯过为巧丽，取于适用而已，大略似北人者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283687_comment'></div>岂其风土固如此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283687_comment'></div>公之父必欲其二子由科举自奋，公独以其馀力<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1283687", 1283687, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>助理</span>家事，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1283687", 1283687, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>积累</span>至巨万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283687_comment'></div>公弟恪茂恭，得以专于文学，庶几近世晁、张辈流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283687_comment'></div>尝与公同上礼部，茂恭得之，而公不利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283687_comment'></div>公忻然曰：「是足以报吾父矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283687_comment'></div>时公父已死数岁，家事一毫已上不使茂恭关心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283687_comment'></div>茂恭奉其母汤药惟谨，不问钱物为何事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283687_comment'></div>而公之临财，虽鬼神不欺也，兄弟相与为一体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283687_comment'></div>至其论文，小不合辄争辩，以致辞色俱厉，僮仆往往相语以为笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283687_comment'></div>茂恭未及为时用而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283687_comment'></div>公年且五十，方俯首笔砚，务合时好，以与后生辈较寸晷于春官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283687_comment'></div>伛偻奉汤药如茂恭在时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283687_comment'></div>暇则从容园池，以小诗自娱，皆清切有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1283687", 1283687, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>雅致</span>，而家事一切付茂恭之子大受，懵若素不解者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283687_comment'></div>进退伸缩，古之君子无以远过矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283687_comment'></div>娶同邑叶氏，子男三人：大辩、大雅、大猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283687_comment'></div>女六人，唐仲义、陈亮、宗楷、陈大同、俞袤，其婿也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283687_comment'></div>幼未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283687_comment'></div>仲义与茂恭同年进士，以邵武之光泽丞上铨曹关升矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283687_comment'></div>孙男二人：兰孙、玉孙；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283687_comment'></div>女二人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283687_comment'></div>得年五十有九，以淳熙癸卯七月三十日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283687_comment'></div>始公无恙时，尝欲营地于源深亭之上，曰：「东望吾父，西望吾弟，其他可勿问也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283687_comment'></div>既而策杖于野堂之西，桂林之旁，徘徊顾望曰：「是亦足以藏其身矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283687_comment'></div>日者独以黄顺堂之山为最吉，曰：「是回鸾舞凤之势也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283687_comment'></div>诸孤欲遵先志，稍近野堂之东，而日者又以净明之东山为吉，寺僧欣然从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283687_comment'></div>用功力至费百馀万，将以乙巳之正月某日葬焉，而有为口语，使寺僧牵连改动，以迁延其葬者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283687_comment'></div>诸孤竟以正月乙酉葬公于官塘之前山，使亮书其石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283687_comment'></div>昔亮尝见朱晦庵论广汉张敬夫「不惑于阴阳卜筮，虽奉其亲以葬，苟有地焉，无适而不可也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283687_comment'></div>天下之决者何以过之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283687_comment'></div>知公之三子固自为可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283687_comment'></div>于是永康陈亮再拜而书曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1283687'>生不求全于人，死不求全于地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283687_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283687_comment'></div>以此遗子孙足矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_41_1283687_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　与朱熹复为汉唐之辨，陈君举调停。作品：答朱元晦秘书书。<div id='poem_1283444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬寅答朱元晦秘书<span class='inlineComment2'>（熹）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283444")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283444'>山间获陪<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>妙论</span>，往往尽出所闻之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283444_comment'></div>世途日狭，所赖以强人意者，惟秘书一人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283444_comment'></div>平生有坐料人物世事之癖，今而后知其不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283444_comment'></div>别去惘然，如盲者之失杖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283444_comment'></div>意每有所不通，辄翘首东望，思欲飞动而未能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283444_comment'></div>方将专人问起居，乃承专翰之赐，蒙所以见念者甚至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283444_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>顽悖</span>为众所共弃，而嗜好之异乃有甚于伯恭者邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283444_comment'></div>既以自幸，深惧为门下知人不明之一累也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283444_comment'></div>惟时春事更深，按临有相，台候动止万福，慰甚不可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283444_comment'></div>某<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>顽钝</span>只如此，日逐且与后生寻行数墨，正如三四十岁丑女，更欲扎腰缚脚，不独可笑，亦良苦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283444_comment'></div>山妇过月始免身，以初四日巳时得一男，却幸母子完全，小下何足上劳尊念，愧感无已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283444_comment'></div>《战国策》、《论衡》、《日注》为贶，甚佳，敢不下拜！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283444_comment'></div>《田说》读得一遍稍详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283444_comment'></div>若事体<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>全转</span>，所谓智者献其谋，其间可采取处亦多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283444_comment'></div>但谓有补于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>圆转</span>事体，则非某所知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283444_comment'></div>居法度繁密之世，论事正不当如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283444_comment'></div>此亦一述朱耳，彼亦一述朱耳，欲以文书尽天下事情，此所以为荆扬之化也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283444_comment'></div>度外之功，岂可以论说而致；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283444_comment'></div>百世之法，岂可以辏合而行乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283444_comment'></div>天下，大物也，须是自家气力可以斡得动，挟得转，则天下之智力无非吾之智力，形同趋而势同利，虽异类可使不约而从也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283444_comment'></div>若只欲安坐而感动之，向来诸君子固已失之偏矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283444_comment'></div>今欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>斗饤</span>而发施之，后来诸君子无乃又失之碎乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283444_comment'></div>论理论事，若箍桶然，此某所不解也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283444_comment'></div>秘书<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1283444", 1283444, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>挺特</span>崇深，自拔于党类之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283444_comment'></div>岁晚庶得一快，方自委托，岂敢怀不尽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283444_comment'></div>意之所到，虽缕缕未止，有不然者，却望见教，某不任至望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1283444_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　秋，为朱熹寿，结束汉唐之辨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　丞相王淮素赏陈亮，有书致淮，论秦桧主和之失，欲激其恢复中原之心。作品：与王丞相淮书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第61页。）</span><div id='poem_1283422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与王季海丞相<span class='inlineComment2'>（淮）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283422")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283422'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283422'>亮窃惟大丞相首秉国钧，士之归心门下者，岂但诚服德谊，要亦不能无利于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283422_comment'></div>天下之士，其无求于世者固少，而吾之权又足以奔走天下之人，则其势固然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283422_comment'></div>独亮之于门下，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>心悦诚服</span>而未尝自言，丞相亦不得而知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283422_comment'></div>岁杪尝欲略布诚悃，而迫归仓卒，又成自外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283422_comment'></div>入春以来，贫病交攻，更无一日好况，虽欲拜一书以叙其本末，亦复因循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283422_comment'></div>私切自念：向者丞相于客退之后，促膝而命之坐，使得款语良久，且忧其无用于时，欲使得一试，恩意恳恳，虽父兄之于子弟不是过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283422_comment'></div>亮而自外于门下，是曾犬马之不若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283422_comment'></div>故尝愿自献其愚忠，惟丞相审听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283422_comment'></div>圣上天日之表，本非苟安于无事，而又英明<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>夐绝</span>古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283422_comment'></div>前后任相，非一人矣，盖亦有所甚属意者，而倚权以行其私，上亦终厌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283422_comment'></div>独丞相布诚心，开公道，进退则采之舆论，废置则付之准绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283422_comment'></div>事上之日久，而上亦察其无他也，故确然信用而不疑，久任而不拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283422_comment'></div>章圣皇帝所谓「王旦事朕之日久，而朕亦察之熟矣，卿等有事但与王旦商量」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283422_comment'></div>故在中书十四五年，而上不以为疑、下不以为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283422_comment'></div>丞相今日真有祖风矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283422_comment'></div>甚盛甚休，非馀人所可望其阃域也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283422_comment'></div>亮独有所甚忧者，秦丞相主和，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>薰炙</span>天地，身享不过十五年，又六年而和败，通止二十一年耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283422_comment'></div>近者乙酉、丙戌之和，本非有一定之计，而今亦二十一年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283422_comment'></div>此其势恐不能久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283422_comment'></div>南北分裂，于今六十年，此天数之当复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283422_comment'></div>阿骨打之兴，于今近八十年，正胡运之当衰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283422_comment'></div>天下一统，犹不能以五六十年无事于其间，必有水旱盗贼乘时窃发之变，况南北之势而欲三十年苟安，盖亦甚难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283422_comment'></div>天下无事，上之所以信任宰相者，他人所不得而间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283422_comment'></div>一旦缓急，丞相能保上之终任我乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283422_comment'></div>奉身而退，在丞相本非难事，然平时之觖望于我者，能保其不以我为奇货乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283422_comment'></div>无事则我享其福，有事则人当其难，此又非丞相之素心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283422_comment'></div>抱不哭之孩儿则当之而不辞，肩千钧之重负则赧然而自退，此又丞相之所当耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283422_comment'></div>亦尝以区区<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>管见</span>窥测圣意，缓急之所用，决非今日之所用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283422_comment'></div>一辈无赖，平居大言以诳人，交结以自鬻，盖亦有许其真能办事者，上安得不疑其可用乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283422_comment'></div>布之边徼，付之繁剧，人亦往往指目之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283422_comment'></div>异时误国，识者当议丞相之不早计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283422_comment'></div>丞相今日纵未能尽收召天下之人才，当一一知其姓名，某人可当何任，某人可办何事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283422_comment'></div>四方之将帅，当一一察其能否，某人可当一面，某人可临一阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283422_comment'></div>边陲之急慢，粮草之虚实，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/114/Comments/0")'>兵卒</span>之强弱，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>城壁</span>之坚脆，历然在目，朗然在心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283422_comment'></div>一旦缓急，则从容为上言之，使上有知人未尽之叹，天下有事故难量之识，虽其号有才力者，亦固在吾驱使间耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283422_comment'></div>一辈无赖不得群起而误国，其为天下国家之福，岂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>浅浅</span>哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283422_comment'></div>丞相虽长秉国钧，公论当不以为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283422_comment'></div>范文正公所谓「身安而后国家可保」者，于丞相见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283422_comment'></div>愿丞相详入思虑，以幸斯世，非亮一人之私言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283422_comment'></div>丞相苟以为然，则亮又将有裨千虑之一得者，继此以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283422_comment'></div>亮向尝言叶适之文学与其为人，此众所共知，丞相亦尝首肯之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283422_comment'></div>此人极有思虑，又心事和平，不肯随时翻覆，既有时名，又取甲科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283422_comment'></div>今一任回，改官，于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>格例</span>极易拈掇，丞相若拔擢而用之，必将有为报效者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283422_comment'></div>但秀才要索事分，若使之随例久候于逆旅，恐非其所能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283422_comment'></div>今已馀两月，丞相若于半月间那辍一差遣与之，徐议拔擢，亦无不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283422_comment'></div>薛叔似文学虽不及适，然识虑精密，心事和平，盖亦不减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283422_comment'></div>向因面对，上亦意其可用，丞相盖已将顺上意矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283422_comment'></div>若并收此人，更与一迁，而适代之，上必不以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283422_comment'></div>是丞相一举而得两士，亦足以厌满天下之公论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283422_comment'></div>亮当以五十口保任其终始可信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283422_comment'></div>其次如陈谦之文学识虑，施迈之心事和平，亦不宜久在掌故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283422_comment'></div>亮固愿使多士尽出门下，岂敢以一时之私，妄有所论荐，此亦效忠之一事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283422_comment'></div>事之所当言、心之所欲言者无限，今直未敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/179/Comments/0")'>缕缕</span>耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1283422_comment'></div>丞相苟察其忠诚，则我决不敢于此遂已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1283422_comment'></div>惓惓之心，伏冀钧恕，幸甚，幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1283422_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　撰谢教授墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283689' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283689' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283689?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢教授墓碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283689")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283689_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283689'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283689'>淳熙三四年间，三山林颖秀实之作邑永康，强敏有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283689", 1283689, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>干略</span>，一邑不劳而办，父老以为三十年所罕有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283689_comment'></div>刘仲光茂实为其丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283689_comment'></div>茂实，永嘉人，尝从一世士君子游，以器识自负，不以细故变其所守，实之疑其好异，而茂实不顾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283689_comment'></div>余游二君间，每为曲畅其情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283689_comment'></div>邑尉谢景安，独恬然无所适莫，二君亦安之如一家，邑人实赖焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283689_comment'></div>及赵伯彬德全来莅邑事，风采焕发，而一丞失其姓名，外缓中忮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283689_comment'></div>赵以忧去，丞欲掇拾其事而文致之，卒愧景安而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283689_comment'></div>使当两雄不相下时，景安居其间，所以阴消人意者，其所能庇赖必多，而区区一尉，效见止此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283689_comment'></div>及诸司交章论荐，于吏文少参差，景安一不以介意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283689_comment'></div>去为贺州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283689_comment'></div>贺在极南，人士无几何，景安独不鄙夷其人，请诸州将及诸司，愈欲赡给其徒而致之学，不幸而景安死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283689_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283689_comment'></div>国家以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1283689", 1283689, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>科目</span>取士，以格法而进退之，权奇磊瑰者固于今世无所合，虽复小合，旋亦弃去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283689_comment'></div>以景安之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283689", 1283689, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>静厚</span>笃实，亦复不偶如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283689_comment'></div>士之欲以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1283689", 1283689, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>科目</span>自奋者，虽既得之，要皆未可必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283689_comment'></div>景安，姓谢氏，名达，字景安，福之长溪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283689_comment'></div>曾大父某，大父某，父某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283689_comment'></div>先室王氏，继邵氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283689_comment'></div>子男三人：宜之、进之、谓老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283689_comment'></div>女三人，长适士人陈表之，馀幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283689_comment'></div>以淳熙甲辰五月二十三日卒，得年六十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283689_comment'></div>以致仕恩得承事郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283689_comment'></div>宜之将以明年三月甲申，葬景安于吾邑之合德乡茅山之原，而以墓石为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283689_comment'></div>余雅知景安者，不能经纪其葬而敢爱其言乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283689_comment'></div>顾未知千年之后定如何耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283689_comment'></div>宜之能自力，足以脩父之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283689_comment'></div>吾友徐木子才、吴竽允成实相为终始之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283689_comment'></div>允成与景安同邑，于是方尉永康云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283689_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1283689'>生于闽，死于广，葬于越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283689_comment'></div>惟其平生所不欺者，不与此而俱灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283689_comment'></div>深藏厚覆，以观馀烈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1283689_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　作《义乌减酒额记》<div id='poem_1283659' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283659' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283659?labeling=true' target='_blank'>义乌县减酒额记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283659")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283659_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283659'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283659'>义乌尉赵君师日以书来曰：「邑之课额，惟酒为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283659_comment'></div>岁之二月至于八月，煮酒以四百石为率，为缗钱八千六百有奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283659_comment'></div>馀为清酒，犹四千八百缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283659_comment'></div>乾道初，有宰驱八乡牙匮列之市肆，商贾争来，𨢜酤倍入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283659_comment'></div>既贡其馀于郡，又增岁额一百石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283659_comment'></div>及市易者交病，而官听其便，独酒额如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283659_comment'></div>逋负岁积，以至于不可计，官不得脱，而吏就黥者相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283659_comment'></div>淳熙十有二载，今资政殿大学士李公之镇是邦也，究心民隐，诸邑之利病莫不毕达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283659_comment'></div>师日实具本末以告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283659_comment'></div>公恻然曰：『民何以堪乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283659_comment'></div>吾尝备数政地，日接玉音，未尝一日不在民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283659_comment'></div>使一县至此而若不闻，吾为负其上矣』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283659_comment'></div>立命减煮酒额一百石，每石为减旧额一缗，清酒月减二百缗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283659_comment'></div>又蠲其旧逋几万缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283659_comment'></div>一邑自是获苏，官逃其责而民安焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283659_comment'></div>酒额岁不亏一钱，而郡县交便之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283659_comment'></div>公之盛德在民为甚深，邑民将立公生祠于星祠之东而朝暮奉事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283659_comment'></div>师日在邑僚之底而获于大惠，不勒其事于石，乌保异时之额不增，非所以相我公之惠于无穷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283659_comment'></div>愿属笔于吾子，以谂来者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283659_comment'></div>亮窃叹𨢜酤之兴，本以佐军旅之用，而其实则使民不得自便于酒，犹未戾于古者禁民饮之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283659_comment'></div>其后设计巧取，而始专于利矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283659_comment'></div>今郡县之利括之殆尽，能者无所用其力，惟酒为可措手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283659_comment'></div>而一县之计实在焉，又从而括之，则县不可为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283659_comment'></div>剥床及肤，其忧岂不在民乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283659_comment'></div>今天子之于民，独公为深知之，而吾州最为受其赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283659_comment'></div>蠲诸邑之逋，吝公帑之出，而一以与民，凡民苗米之不及斗、帛不及尺、绵不及两者，悉代输之，仁声载路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283659_comment'></div>是固所以宣天子之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1283659", 1283659, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>德意</span>，而入民之骨髓也，宁酒而已乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283659_comment'></div>上方图任旧德，与之共政，即日旋归，吾州不得久私其惠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283659_comment'></div>虽使世之名能文者，不能执笔以尽公之美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283659_comment'></div>顾以属诸陆沈无所比数之人，颠倒脱落，无以满邑民之望，不将归其咎于君乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283659_comment'></div>师日曰：「不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283659_comment'></div>吾二人皆将牵连托公以自见者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283659_comment'></div>亮又奚辞！</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1283659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　致书勾熙载。作品：与勾熙载书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　致章德茂书。作品：与章德茂侍郎书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1185&endYear=1185')">1185年</a>　送章德茂大卿使虏，作《水调歌头》（不见南师久）<div id='poem_157217' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157217' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157217?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头 送章德茂大卿使虏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157217")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157217_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157217'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157217'>不见南师久，漫说<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_157217", 157217, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>北群空</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157217'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_157217", 157217, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>当场</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_157217", 157217, "Clauses/2/Comments/1")'>只手</span>，毕竟还我万夫雄。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157217'>自笑堂堂汉使，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_157217", 157217, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>得似</span>洋洋河水，依旧只流东。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157217'>且复穹庐拜，会向藁街逢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157217_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157217'>尧之都，舜之壤，禹之封。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157217'>于中应有，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_157217", 157217, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>一个半个</span>耻臣戎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157217'>万里腥膻如许，千古英灵安在，磅礴几时通。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157217'>胡运何须问，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_157217", 157217, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>赫日</span>自当中。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157217_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_157217'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　七月十五日寿内，作《天仙子》（一夜秋光先著柳）<span class='inlineComment2'>（该词系年难辨。以末数语观之，子女至少已有二三人十余岁，且同甫似方遭诬陷得解，据此，推测为淳熙十一年至十三年之间，姑附于此。）</span><div id='poem_157211' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157211' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157211?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天仙子 七月十五日寿内</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157211")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157211_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157211'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157211'>一夜秋光先著柳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157211'>暑力平明羞失守。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157211'>西风不放入<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_157211", 157211, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>帘帏</span>，饶永昼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157211'>沉烟透。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157211'>半月十朝秋定否。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157211_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157211'>指点芙渠凝伫久。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157211'>高处成莲深处藕。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157211'>百年长共月团圆，女进酒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_157211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_157211'>男称寿。<div id='poem_sentence_8_157211_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_157211'>一点浮云人似旧。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_157211_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　秋，寿朱元晦。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　汉唐之辨余波，与朱熹书信往来。欲与朱熹讲切，求定论。陈傅良见二人争之太烈，出面劝解。作品：丙午复朱元晦秘书书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第63页。）</span><div id='poem_1283451' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283451' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283451?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙午复朱元晦秘书书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283451")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283451_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283451'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283451'>不获拜起居之问，又一年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283451_comment'></div>七八月之交，子约处递到所惠书，备纫存念不忘之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283451_comment'></div>陆沈至此，如门下之着眼者几人，遥望门墙，每欲飞动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283451_comment'></div>即日秋高气清，伏惟茂对令辰，天人显相，台候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283451_comment'></div>千里之远，竟未能酬奉觞为寿之愿，雪梨甜榴四十颗，今岁乡间遭大风，梨绝难得，极大者仅如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283451_comment'></div>章德茂得蜀隔织一缣，疏不甚佳，只堪粗裘用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283451_comment'></div>苏笺一百，鄙词一阕，薄致祝赞之诚，不敢失每岁常礼尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283451_comment'></div>无佳物自效，切幸笑留！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283451_comment'></div>向来往还数书，非敢与门下争辩，聊以明不敢自屈其说以自附和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283451_comment'></div>以亮之畸穷不肖，本应得罪于一世大贤君子，秘书独怜其穷，不忍弃绝之，亮亦因不敢自外于门下尔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283451_comment'></div>世以相附和为党而欲加之罪者，非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283451_comment'></div>此数书亦欲为免死之计，见世之有力者亦使一读之，而秀才门见其怪甚，相与传说流布，非有意流传之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283451_comment'></div>亮平生不曾会与人讲论，独伯恭于空闲时喜相往复，亮亦感其相知，不知其言语之尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283451_comment'></div>伯恭既死，此事尽废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283451_comment'></div>子约、叔昌卒岁一番相见，不过寒温常谈，而安得有所谓讲切者哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283451_comment'></div>来书问「有何讲论」者，犹以亮为喜与人语乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283451_comment'></div>兼之浙间议论，自始至末，亮并不晓一句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283451_comment'></div>道之在天下，至公而已矣，屈曲琐碎皆私意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283451_comment'></div>天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1283451", 1283451, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>情伪</span>，岂一人之智虑所能尽防哉，就能防之，亦非圣人所愿为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283451_comment'></div>《礼》曰：「人藏其心，不可测度也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283451_comment'></div>美恶皆在其心，不见其色也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283451_comment'></div>欲一以穷之，舍礼何以哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283451_comment'></div>惟其止于理，则彼此皆可知尔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283451_comment'></div>若各用其智，则迭相上下而岂有穷乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283451_comment'></div>圣人之于天下，时行而已矣，逆计、预防，皆私意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283451_comment'></div>天运之无穷，岂一人之私智所能曲周哉，就能周之，亦非圣人之所愿为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283451_comment'></div>《易》有太极而生两仪，两仪生四象，四象生八卦，八卦定吉凶，吉凶生大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283451_comment'></div>故圣人先天而天弗违，后天以奉天时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283451_comment'></div>先天者所以开此理也，岂逆计、预防之云乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283451_comment'></div>世疑《周礼》为六国阴谋之书，不知汉儒说《周礼》之过尔，非周公之本旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283451_comment'></div>老庄之所以深诮孔子者，岂非欲以一人之智虑而周天下乎，不知其本于至公而时行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283451_comment'></div>秘书之学，至公而时行之学也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283451_comment'></div>秘书之为人，扫尽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1283451", 1283451, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>情伪</span>而一于至公者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283451_comment'></div>世儒之论，皆有官不容针私通车马之意，皆亮之所不晓；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283451_comment'></div>故独归心于门下者，直以此耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283451_comment'></div>有公则无私，私则不复有公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283451_comment'></div>王霸可以杂用，则天理人欲可以并行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283451_comment'></div>亮所以为缕缕者，不欲更添一条路，所以开拓大中，张皇幽眇，而助秘书之正学也，岂好为异说而求出于秘书之外乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283451_comment'></div>不深察其心，则今可止矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283451_comment'></div>比见陈一之国录，说张体仁太博为门下士，每读亮与门下书，则怒发冲冠，以为异说；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283451_comment'></div>每见亮来，则以为怪人，辄舍去不与共坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283451_comment'></div>由此言之，此数书未能免罪于世俗，而得罪于门下士多矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283451_comment'></div>不止，则楚人又将钳我于市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283451_comment'></div>进退维谷，可以一笑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283451_comment'></div>甚欲走武夷为旬日之款，而近来亦自多病，眼前衮衮，更摆脱不暇，且看冬仲如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283451_comment'></div>如闻生理亦颇费力，叶正则独以为「秘书不求容于世，吾人不当为姑息之爱以相累」，此言良有理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283451_comment'></div>天下之事岂人智所可妆做而辏合哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283451_comment'></div>要之，今世学者终是信命不及，尚未暇其安于义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283451_comment'></div>如亮之谬戾颠倒，分与世违而无所恤，则又别论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283451_comment'></div>定叟智出于父兄之外，而卒不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283451_comment'></div>虎狼、蝼蚁，正未易择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283451_comment'></div>亮方学为治圃之事，亦欲治一二亭子，力所未能者甚多，其可及者又为风撤去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283451_comment'></div>「洛阳亭馆是何人」，吾人真瓶中见粟之人尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1283451_comment'></div>连书求作《抱膝吟》，非求秘书妆撰而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_53_1283451", 1283451, "Clauses/161/Comments/0")'>排连</span>也，只欲写眼前景物，道今昔之变，一为和平之音，一为慷慨悲歌，以娱其索居野处耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1283451_comment'></div>信手直写，便自抑扬顿挫，何必过于思虑以相玩哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1283451_comment'></div>去奴留待几日尽不妨，愿试作意而为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1283451_comment'></div>入秋脚气殊作梗，意绪极不佳，欲作一书，数日方能下笔，又不成语言，遣仆遂以蹉跎，秘书必察其非敢慢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1283451_comment'></div>寿之宣教侍旁，为学日粹，失子之戚今能置之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1283451_comment'></div>台眷长少均庆！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1283451_comment'></div>荆妇儿女附拜再四起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1283451_comment'></div>未承晤间，千万为世道崇护，亮不任区区之祷！</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1283451_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　患脚气病。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　为元宝观重建大殿撰文。作品：元宝观重建大殿记。<div id='poem_1283664' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283664' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283664?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元宝观重建大殿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283664")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283664_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283664'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283664'>东阳县之南四十里，有观曰元宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283664_comment'></div>世传齐人陈元宝舍宅为之，因以名云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283664_comment'></div>宣和剧盗之火，观为煨烬，则其里陈君严始建所谓北极殿者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283664_comment'></div>大夫徐君端记其事颇异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283664_comment'></div>大夫名下一字，实吾先祖之讳，今不复具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283664_comment'></div>严弟仕澄，字彦清，自力家事，积赀殆且巨万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283664_comment'></div>志不在于积也，而泄之里闾亲旧之惠为未足，乃泄之观焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283664_comment'></div>三清有殿，殿有庑，合以三门，而观俨然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283664_comment'></div>皆彦清之为，而绍兴之二十一年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283664_comment'></div>未几，殿蠹于蚁，彦清之子德佐过而动心焉，思与诸弟协力成之，使其父之志与殿俱存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283664_comment'></div>而主观事葛元度并以风其诸子曰：「先志今何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283664_comment'></div>欣然损金合百万先之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283664_comment'></div>元度先建道藏一所，为民祈福，祷请如响，其积亦颇夥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283664_comment'></div>并倾私囊、募众缘以建其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283664_comment'></div>殿未成而元度死，其徒胡大云继之，犹藉德佐之弟德先、德高以自助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283664_comment'></div>用财合一千万，役人之力凡万五千，经始于淳熙辛丑之春，落成于甲辰之冬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283664_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283664", 1283664, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>宏壮</span>伟丽，一切视彦清在时，远近合睹，起敬增叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283664_comment'></div>道家之有殿以奉三清，其教然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283664_comment'></div>三教之兴废有时，而本末宏阔，源流深长，非百世圣人不能定，则脩旧起废，固其徒之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283664_comment'></div>彦清兄弟皆有财力，可以自驰骋于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283664_comment'></div>而本朝出仕惟两涂，故其才独自豪于乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283664_comment'></div>其明效大验，亦不遗馀力，而乃见所谓两殿者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283664_comment'></div>殿之随废，又藉元度以起之，亦可叹也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283664_comment'></div>元度善自兴其教者，而敢爱其力而自纳于废弃！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283664_comment'></div>殿成而胡大云亦死，相与成就其殿之凡役，彦清幼子疆亦从而相之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283664_comment'></div>旁观多陈氏，其详虽不可考，宜其为元宝不可知孙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283664_comment'></div>一念之烈，泄于七八百年之后者犹如此，天下事其有不成于志念之烈者乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283664_comment'></div>疆与道士合辞以记为请，诺之阅二年矣，因以寓余之所感云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1283664_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　春，上礼部，复不中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　二月十三日，庶弟昭甫死。冬葬之，作墓志铭。作品：庶弟昭甫墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第64页。）</span><div id='poem_1283691' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283691' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283691?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庶弟昭甫墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283691")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283691_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283691'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283691'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283691_comment'></div>昔我先人实生汝而弃汝于他人，力未足以活汝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283691_comment'></div>我兄弟欲活汝于我家之旁，念汝之似吾先人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283691_comment'></div>活汝未成而弃我以去，岂以我为不足赖乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283691_comment'></div>我不能不念其子，而不念吾先人之子则无以自别于禽兽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283691_comment'></div>我之心既不欺于鬼神，而汝犹有疑乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283691_comment'></div>无乃汝既知之，而命之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1283691", 1283691, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>脩短</span>非汝之所能自制乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283691_comment'></div>不然，则我之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283691", 1283691, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>衰困</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283691", 1283691, "Clauses/14/Comments/1")'>颠倒</span>，获罪于天者既多，而并以累汝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283691_comment'></div>嗟乎冤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283691_comment'></div>畴昔之年，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1283691", 1283691, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>当路</span>欲置我于死地，病馀而继以囚系，坐天狱如坐井，虽生能几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283691_comment'></div>扶持左右，始末惟汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283691_comment'></div>未几，为小盗要而欲杀之于路，卒能使薄正其罪，独汝为有奔走之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283691_comment'></div>汝之于我，既无负矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283691_comment'></div>生死之变，俄然至此，得疾之端，又复由我，而我之所以处汝者，今虽百喙自言，人谁信之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283691_comment'></div>觞酒酹汝，而诸子列拜于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283691_comment'></div>汝魂未定，尚听我语：衣衾棺椁，我皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1283691", 1283691, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>主办</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283691_comment'></div>岁时祭享，汝终归享于陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283691_comment'></div>我当敕其子孙以无忘吾先人之骨肉，庶几异时有以见汝于地下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283691_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283691_comment'></div>此龙川陈亮志其庶弟之墓者如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283691_comment'></div>先人讳次尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283691_comment'></div>庶弟名明，字昭甫，行八三，而所养之父则张锐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283691_comment'></div>生甫百馀日，归张氏，其复归则十有七矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283691_comment'></div>又十一年而死，实淳熙丁未二月二十三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283691_comment'></div>其冬十二月十七日，葬之先茔之支垄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283691_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1283691'>汝父汝兄，相从在此，子孙敢曰，非陈氏子！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283691_comment'></div>灵其有知，共食千祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283691_comment'></div>此石昭然，其来未已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1283691_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　入夏，脚气复作梗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　策问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　秋，陈亮寿，陈傅良寄诗相贺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　朱熹寿，陈亮作《洞仙歌》词为贺。（秋容一洗）<div id='poem_157239' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157239' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157239?labeling=true' target='_blank'>洞仙歌 丁未寿朱元晦</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157239")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157239_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157239'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157239'>秋容一洗。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157239'>不受凡尘涴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157239'>许大乾坤这回大。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157239'>向上头、些子是，雕鹗抟空，篱底下，只有黄花几朵。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157239_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157239'>骑鲸汗漫，那得人同坐，赤手丹心扑不破。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157239'>问唐虞、禹汤武，多少功名，犹自是、一点浮云铲过。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157239_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157239'>且烧却、一瓣海南沉，任拈取、千年陆沉奇货。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_157239_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a246af9ea8c5479fa01b941003f6f3c3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a246af9ea8c5479fa01b941003f6f3c3");'><span id='a246af9ea8c5479fa01b941003f6f3c3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>，45岁</div><div id='a246af9ea8c5479fa01b941003f6f3c3' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>与章德茂侍郎书，并有小词数阕请章评阅。作品：与章德茂侍郎又书。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>冬，撰何夫人杜氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283711' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283711' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283711?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何夫人杜氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283711")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283711_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283711'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283711'>始余闻东阳何君坚才善为家，积资至巨万，乡之长者皆自以为才智莫能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283711_comment'></div>然坚才方端居深念，平生为学之志于是不酬矣，遣其子逮从一世士君子游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283711_comment'></div>又招至邵康似之，使造、适、遇、述从之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283711_comment'></div>似之有声学校中，及为甲辰礼部榜首，世多知其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283711_comment'></div>似之亦善称其四子，谓足以如坚才志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283711_comment'></div>而坚才死，逮实主家事，帅其四弟以奉母夫人杜氏惟谨，而门户纲纪，一切听之逮，如坚才在时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283711_comment'></div>人往往言逮才有父风，或曰：「是四弟为学之验也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283711_comment'></div>余独心知杜夫人之有异于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283711_comment'></div>夫母主于爱，爱之过则长幼必失其序，而家事莫适所主矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283711_comment'></div>今父死而五子以次听命，余虽不及知夫人处家之详，而其大略固足为寡居者之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283711_comment'></div>夫人姓杜氏，世为东阳儒家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283711_comment'></div>曾大父义，大父伯忻，父杉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283711_comment'></div>夫人年十九归何君松，坚才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283711_comment'></div>以淳熙丙午闰月二十五日卒，享年五十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283711_comment'></div>子男五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283711_comment'></div>女四人：长适同邑郭江，江兄弟为东方学者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283711_comment'></div>次适从政郎淮西江东总领军马钱粮所准备差遣巩嵘，寻卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283711_comment'></div>馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283711_comment'></div>孙男三人：存、摅、恬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283711_comment'></div>诸孤将以丁未十月二十九日合葬夫人于松山乡宝山原坚才之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283711_comment'></div>先事，逮跣行以见永康陈亮而哭曰：「葬日迫矣，闺门之懿将随葬而泯灭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283711_comment'></div>吾母早奉其姑勤甚，晚岁复迎外王母以归养，示诸子以孝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283711_comment'></div>吾父死而我兄弟居丧，不使一日废学，示诸子以无忘先志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283711_comment'></div>衣食足矣，而机杼之事虽老不置，示诸子以不忘本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283711_comment'></div>使令具矣，而鞭扑虽有不用，示诸子以尚宽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283711_comment'></div>至于平生妯娌之无间言，乡闾亲戚之有恩意，人人类能言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283711_comment'></div>吾子盍为逮图其所以永久者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283711_comment'></div>亮语之曰：「子之言皆是也，而我又有以知君之母，惜乎吾文之不逮也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283711_comment'></div>于是与之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1283711'>家政归一，如父在时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283711_comment'></div>非子之能，惟母之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283711_comment'></div>死则同穴，厚以培之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283711_comment'></div>后千百年，铭其庶几。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1283711_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>撰刘夫人何氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283712?labeling=true' target='_blank'>凌夫人何氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283712")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283712_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283712'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283712'>绍兴之季，余客临安凡三岁，父母愿其有室而命之归也，义乌何茂恭欲妻以其兄之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283712_comment'></div>于是义乌之富言何氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283712_comment'></div>茂恭兄弟俱能文，而茂恭声问尤伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283712_comment'></div>余贫甚，惧不得当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283712_comment'></div>诸凡茂恭姻党皆以为不然，独武义刘君叔向力赞其说，且语吾父趣纳币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283712_comment'></div>又明年，乾道改元，余往就姻焉，姻党咸在，而叔向之妻，茂恭之女弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283712_comment'></div>于是茂恭之母年七十馀，两子一女，相与为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283712_comment'></div>门户方张，和气充满，入其门者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283712", 1283712, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>油然</span>生敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283712_comment'></div>爱诸孙女如女，然而尤念吾妻为类己，以故刘氏姑视之特好，而叔向于余亦加厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283712_comment'></div>茂恭罢官吉之永新，诸公争知其才，旁观者亦以横飞直上为不难也，而壬辰之春，一日无疾而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283712_comment'></div>又三四年，母亦下世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283712_comment'></div>叔向与其妻会葬，而叔向死焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283712_comment'></div>茂恭之妻未几亦死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283712_comment'></div>吾妻之父以淳熙癸卯七月之晦，其死如茂恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283712_comment'></div>独刘氏姑与吾外姑尚无恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283712_comment'></div>丙午之春，俱集于外氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283712_comment'></div>刘氏姑语余曰：「我生于七月二十八日，岁烦遣礼而不一顾我，如不遣也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283712_comment'></div>余笑曰：「是固其初心，今当偿之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283712_comment'></div>及期而往，出门迎笑，大会亲族，劝酬达旦，而意殊无已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283712_comment'></div>是夜，将继之以乐，杯未行而举手扶头曰病，余往视之，则死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283712_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283712_comment'></div>盛衰相寻，本不足计，而生死之际，其谁为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283712_comment'></div>乃使其兄弟之死如一人，余亦不自知其哭之恸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283712_comment'></div>二十馀年之间，为月凡几，为日凡几，何氏刘氏其变如此之亟，而余穷盖如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283712_comment'></div>变通之道，独至于余而遂息耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283712_comment'></div>是又可叹已矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283712_comment'></div>夫人姓何氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283712_comment'></div>曾大父京，大父先，父矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283712_comment'></div>年十七归刘氏，死时五十三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283712_comment'></div>子男三人：三复，监衢州北较务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283712_comment'></div>三友，三进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283712_comment'></div>女三人：嫁黄华、黄述古，皆佳子弟，而述古尝以国子上礼部；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283712_comment'></div>幼未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283712_comment'></div>孙男三人，女三人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283712_comment'></div>夫人志意疏豁，语言明朗，遇亲族上下，不问贫富贵贱皆有恩纪，大略似其父而不类妇人女子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283712_comment'></div>然乐人之饮而不自饮，终日言笑而无可择之言，闺门懿行虽处子不能过，岂其得阴之正德而无其幽吝之气耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283712_comment'></div>此亦妇人之杰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283712_comment'></div>始，叔向之葬，在家傍五里金塘之东原，诸孤将以丁未十一月二十三日合葬，而谓亮：「何以使吾母虽死而不亡乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283712_comment'></div>亮固力不足者，将藉友朋以自助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283712_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1283712'>志念豁然，赍之以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283712_comment'></div>葬从其夫，畀尔孙子。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1283712_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>撰陈元嘉墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283690' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283690' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283690?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈元嘉墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283690")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283690_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283690'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283690'>缙云陈君元嘉，以其读书之馀，凡山经、地志、<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283690", 1283690, "Clauses/2/Comments/3")'>医卜</span>、方技之书，黄帝岐伯之所答问，郭璞吕才之所论注，无不熟复而究切之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283690_comment'></div>下至弈棋，亦入能品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283690_comment'></div>动息自遂，与物无忤，从容暇豫人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283690_comment'></div>元嘉娶章氏，故吏部侍郎讳服之女弟也，于是士大夫亦多知其名；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283690_comment'></div>闻其死，无不恻然伤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283690_comment'></div>其子桧，尝从予游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283690_comment'></div>幼子猛，有豪志，尝欲问余以古人之大体，方进而未已也，奉其诸兄之命而问铭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283690_comment'></div>乃见其乡之长老言曰：「甲戌之旱，所在摇动，乡之郭君集义兵以卫其境，元嘉亦散家赀，募少年之有武勇者，什什而伍伍之，参错能否，牵连远近，而人固不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283690_comment'></div>会郭君之徒有谋叛者，郭窘甚，夜走乡先生胡经仲之庐，则语元嘉，命队首击锣鸣鼓，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283690", 1283690, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>整布</span>队伍，更出迭入，压郭氏之门而过焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283690_comment'></div>时邑令方循行四隅，以督赈粜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283690_comment'></div>元嘉令伪为县牒，起义兵自卫，微使郭氏之徒闻之，而元嘉之兵先集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283690_comment'></div>未几，邑令亦来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283690_comment'></div>其徒震动，然犹自诡以献武艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283690_comment'></div>元嘉命翼开左右使献之，叛者卒不能逞而止」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283690_comment'></div>以元嘉之才，小小自见，已能如此，而余独知其为乡之善士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283690_comment'></div>盖人才因事乃见，而元嘉亦不愿以才自驰骋于世，非直余之浅于知人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283690_comment'></div>元嘉姓陈氏，讳昌运，元嘉其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283690_comment'></div>其先繇永嘉徙缙云，为乡之大姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283690_comment'></div>曾大父捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283690_comment'></div>大父梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283690_comment'></div>父师尹迪功郎，潭州善化主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283690_comment'></div>子男五人：椿、桧、槐、枢、猛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283690_comment'></div>女六人，适周翊、何坦、沈集、王元德；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283690_comment'></div>坦监处州石堰银场；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283690_comment'></div>馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283690_comment'></div>孙男五人：日新、日益、日宣、日严、日勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283690_comment'></div>元嘉以淳熙八年四月十日死，死时六十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283690_comment'></div>而其葬在其邑之仙都乡深渡之原，实十四年十一月五日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283690_comment'></div>于是永康陈亮为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1283690'>才足用世而为乡善士，非其命也，亦其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283690_comment'></div>山夷谷堙而来者不坠，非其志也，固其义也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1283690_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='61877bcf73364deb80777b3e62cc8bb3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("61877bcf73364deb80777b3e62cc8bb3");'><span id='61877bcf73364deb80777b3e62cc8bb3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1189')">1188-1189年</a>，46-47岁</div><div id='61877bcf73364deb80777b3e62cc8bb3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　与尤延之侍郎书，言仲冬将有京口之行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　撰姚汉英母夫人墓志铭，汉英乃陈亮太学同舎生。<div id='poem_1283713' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283713' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283713?labeling=true' target='_blank'>姚汉英母夫人沈氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1188年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283713")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283713_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283713'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283713'>余世居永康之村落间，雅不喜游城市，遇友朋在焉，则过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283713_comment'></div>一日，遇同舍生姚怡顺道于阛阓中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283713_comment'></div>其门桑柘环合，一径幽长，如幽人逸士之居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283713_comment'></div>升堂而拜其父，则风貌淳古，语言质实，使人失其所以欲富欲贵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283713_comment'></div>竹床瓦器，品具精洁，闺门济济，又若不待礼法而自合者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283713_comment'></div>余虽不及请拜其母，而心知其阃内之懿矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283713_comment'></div>久之，而怡之母夫人死，死后乃知其为故吏部尚书陈良祐之外兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283713_comment'></div>盖其夫妻安贫，不以亲戚之贵达而有赖焉，虽其友之子不得而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283713_comment'></div>夫人从子徐君之茂，登科从仕，日月有闻，而怡之友林君大中、徐君木亦浸浸有列于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283713_comment'></div>独怡蹭蹬太学，夫人亦不以是而愧其子，徒欲其学业之久且不怠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283713_comment'></div>夫人姓沈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283713_comment'></div>曾祖某，祖某，父某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283713_comment'></div>婺之金华人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283713_comment'></div>年若干，归永康姚君某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283713_comment'></div>子男一人，怡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283713_comment'></div>女若干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283713_comment'></div>孙男若干；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283713_comment'></div>女若干，适某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283713_comment'></div>夫人以怡入太学，遇高宗皇帝庆寿覃恩，得封孺人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283713_comment'></div>嫁之若干年，卒于某月某日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283713_comment'></div>越一年，当淳熙戊申冬十一月十有八日，葬于邑之承训乡马义弄之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283713_comment'></div>而以铭属其友陈亮，辞不获，则叙其略如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283713_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1283713'>不使其夫有赖于人，不使其子有羡于人，此其德之深且厚者，故所以宜其后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283713_comment'></div>铭以昭德，独可非其人乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1283713_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　撰陈春坊墓志铭。作品：陈春坊墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（一说《陈春坊墓志铭》作于淳熙十六年（1189），参见颜虚心《宋陈龙川先生亮年谱》第121页。）</span><div id='poem_1283692' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283692' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283692?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈春坊墓碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1188年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283692")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283692_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283692'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283692'>始余出国北门，弥望沮洳之地而带以一水，岸行不足以容车马，湖泊往往随在而有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283692_comment'></div>舟至松江，风涛汹涌，虽余亦惧而登焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283692_comment'></div>小立垂虹之上，四顾而欢曰：「是岂戎马驱驰之所乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283692_comment'></div>昔陈公思恭提兵数千，以小舟匿伏湖中，欲要兀术而擒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283692_comment'></div>扣舷相应，战士尽起，而兀术以轻舠遁去，众遂惊溃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283692_comment'></div>韩世忠复扼之江上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283692_comment'></div>虏自是不复南顾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283692_comment'></div>酌酒吊古，以酹陈公之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283692_comment'></div>其孙均，及以喻侃、何仲光之书来，求铭春坊之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283692_comment'></div>阅其家世，则陈公之子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283692_comment'></div>而陈公又为晋公恕之玄孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283692_comment'></div>晋公当太宗真宗时，为国计臣，寇忠悯诸公之所敬惮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283692_comment'></div>其子恭公执中，实相仁宗以大阐陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283692_comment'></div>恭公之弟执古，生殿中丞世昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283692_comment'></div>殿丞生赠武翼郎晏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283692_comment'></div>武翼以国学举人数上春官而无所遇，是生少师名思恭，卒由行伍自奋，为神武后军统制以困兀术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283692_comment'></div>其事有慨于余心，虽欲却均之请，而心知其可以张大陈公之功，亦一时之良会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283692_comment'></div>而均之请，阅一岁不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283692_comment'></div>春坊名龟年，字寿卿，其先熙州狄道人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283692_comment'></div>高宗南渡，少师扈从，转战至杭，因家焉，故今为杭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283692_comment'></div>春坊以少师致仕恩补保义郎，为閤门祗候，提辖制造御前军器所，干办军头引见司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283692_comment'></div>丁母崇国夫人柴氏忧，服除，差镇江府都统司主管机宜文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283692_comment'></div>未上，改差皇太子宫主管左右春坊事，为閤门宣赞舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283692_comment'></div>寻除武卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283692_comment'></div>御札曰：「陈龟年，名将之子也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283692_comment'></div>转右领军卫将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283692_comment'></div>特旨以「久在东宫，服勤不懈」，带文州刺史，除成州团练使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283692_comment'></div>为皇孙平阳郡王伴读有劳，授和州防御使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283692_comment'></div>少师一子，以南北既定，不复见诸武事，而独为东宫信臣，以身任怨，至死而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283692_comment'></div>尝以馆北客宴射玉津园，选善射者与虏并射，莫能中，春坊挟二矢以兴，平立睨的，一发中之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283692_comment'></div>使当多事时，吴江之遗恨犹有属也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283692_comment'></div>春坊须眉如画，而面目严冷，出入宫庭，不以色假人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283692_comment'></div>整齐事务，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1283692", 1283692, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>摧抑</span>侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283692_comment'></div>取前代储君事，钞成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1283692", 1283692, "Clauses/95/Comments/0")'>小集</span>，暇日从容献之，听知所择，以为东宫德业之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283692_comment'></div>和章作字，必以寓区区之意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283692_comment'></div>吾友王光化自中尝为其客，为余道其事如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283692_comment'></div>今所载者其略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283692_comment'></div>未几而春坊坐裴良珣事谪居信州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283692_comment'></div>复官，得提举台州崇道观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283692_comment'></div>以淳熙十五年四月癸酉卒于家，得年五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283692_comment'></div>以五月甲寅葬于馀杭县蔡家之坞，夫人赵氏祔，赠太师密之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283692_comment'></div>子男二人：均，承节郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283692_comment'></div>垓，以致仕恩上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283692_comment'></div>女八人：长适忠翊郎婺州准备将刘帱，次适从事郎隆兴府进贤县尉朱熙续，次适宣教郎两浙东路提举茶盐司干办公事魏宝慈，次适秉义郎裴良珣，次适吴衍，馀未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283692_comment'></div>男孙一人，小顽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283692_comment'></div>甲辰之春，余以药人之诬，就逮棘寺，更七八十日而不得脱，狱卒犹能言春坊之事始末，盖其受诬颇相类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283692_comment'></div>狱稍宽，欲往访春坊问计，而春坊病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283692_comment'></div>狱之相去才一二年间，而诬人药人亦可以例推耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283692_comment'></div>天下适安定，才者能者无不坎𡒄于世，宛转少能自致，至于受诬且死而世莫之察，未死者可不为死者一言乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283692_comment'></div>余非能言者也，二百年之间，陈氏之变故起伏亦数矣，均方与人士相角逐以自见，而垓亦将求世其家者，故再至垂虹，卒如其请，而书诸墓上曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1283692'>今天子龙飞之六十日，草莽之臣陈亮，实表故春坊陈龟年之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283692_comment'></div>叙载家世，感念事功，而卒归之命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283692_comment'></div>非人谁为，非命谁使？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283692_comment'></div>且以识死，且以起死。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1283692_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　九月十（八）日作《卜算子》寿徐子才。（悄静菊花天）<span class='inlineComment2'>（该词作年无考。末二句暗寓徐子才晚年仕进有展，证其经历，或作于淳熙末年，即1188年前后，附于此。）</span><div id='poem_157206' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157206' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157206?labeling=true' target='_blank'>卜算子 九月十八日寿徐子才</a><span class='authorDate'>（1188年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157206")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157206_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157206'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157206'>悄静菊花天，洗尽梧桐雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157206'>倍九周遭烂漫开，祝寿当头取。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157206_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157206'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_157206", 157206, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>顶戴</span>御袍黄，叠秀金棱吐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157206'>仙种花容晚节香，人愿争先睹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157206_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157206'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_157206_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　酬辛幼安，再用《贺新郎》韵见寄。（离乱从头说）<div id='poem_157253' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157253' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157253?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎 酬辛幼安再用韵见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_1_157253'>爱吾民、金缯不爱，蔓藤累葛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157253'>壮气尽消人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_157253", 157253, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>脆好</span>，冠盖阴山观雪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157253'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_157253", 157253, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>亏杀</span>我、一星星发。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157253'>涕出女吴成倒转，问鲁为、齐弱何年月。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157253'>丘也幸，由之瑟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157253_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157253'>斩新换出旗麾别。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157253'>把当时、一桩大义，拆开收合。<div id='poem_sentence_7_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_157253'>据地一呼吾往矣，万里摇肢动骨。<div id='poem_sentence_8_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_157253'>这话把、只成痴绝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_157253'>天地洪炉谁扇鞴，算于中、安得长坚铁。<div id='poem_sentence_10_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_157253'>淝水破，关东裂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_157253_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_157253'><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_157251'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157251'>话杀浑閒说。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157251'>不成教、齐民也解，为伊为葛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157251'>尊酒相逢成二老，却忆去年风雪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157251'>新著了、几茎华发。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157251'>百世寻人犹接踵，叹只今、两地<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_157251", 157251, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>三人月</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157251'>写旧恨，向谁瑟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157251_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157251'>男儿何用伤离别。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157251_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157251'>况古来、几番际会，风从云合。<div gray;'>▪</span>五月，自金陵归，正则来宿一日而行。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>送徐子宜赴新安知徽州时作《谒金门》（新雨足）<div id='poem_472898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_472898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/472898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒金门 送徐子宜如新安</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_472898'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_472898'>新雨足。洗尽山城<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_472898", 472898, id='poem_sentence_1_472898_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_472898'>四海英游追逐。事业相时伸缩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_472898_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年7月</a>　七月大病，几死。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　上皇帝《鉴成箴》，不报。作品：上光宗皇帝鉴成箴。<span class='inlineComment2'>（一说伏阙上《鉴成箴》在绍熙元年（1190），参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第67页。）</span><div id='poem_1283665' class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283665")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1283665_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283665'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283665'>五闰失驭，伪主<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>僭窃</span>，纲常丝棼，宇县<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>瓜裂</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1283665'>干戈日寻，汤沸火热，元元憔悴，无所存活。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1283665'>艺祖勃兴，天为民设。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1283665'>受命之日，兵刃不血。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1283665'>痛兹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>版图</span>，尚尔割截，丙夜不安，往就普说。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1283665'>独立门外，冲冒风雪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1283665'>谋定戈指，莫我敢遏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1283665'>首往扬州，重进诛殛；<div id='poem_sentence_7_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1283665'>旋征泽潞，李筠就杀。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1283665'>复掩湖南，保权力屈；<div id='poem_sentence_9_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1283665'>爰取荆南，继冲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>悚慑</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1283665'>一鼓孟昶，蜀城斯拔；<div id='poem_sentence_11_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1283665'>徂征岭南，刘鋹面缚。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1283665'>驰使江南，李煜踧踖；<div id='poem_sentence_13_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1283665'>传檄吴越，钱俶纳国。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1283665'>十馀年间，忧虑危慄，头若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>蓬葆</span>，雨沐风栉。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1283665'>东征西伐，天下始一。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1283665'>解兵脩贡，降王在列。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1283665'>施裤麻鞋，缘布衣褐。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1283665'>训练六军，法度陛级。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1283665'>太宗继之，乾乾夕惕。<div id='poem_sentence_20_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1283665'>亲征河东，督励士卒，人百其勇，城无全堞。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1283665'>下诏宽赦，继元乃伏；<div id='poem_sentence_22_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1283665'>收复漳泉，洪进<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>屏息</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1283665'>真宗嗣之，二祖是法。<div id='poem_sentence_24_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1283665'>契丹来寇，人心业业。<div id='poem_sentence_25_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1283665'>决意亲征，俯从准策。<div id='poem_sentence_26_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1283665'>亲御鞍马，躬秉黄钺。<div id='poem_sentence_27_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1283665'>白旄一麾，王师奋发。<div id='poem_sentence_28_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_1283665'>我气既盈，虏气斯竭。<div id='poem_sentence_29_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1283665'>稽首请和，干戈载戢。<div id='poem_sentence_30_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1283665'>譬以祸福，实赖臣弼。<div id='poem_sentence_31_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1283665'>于皇仁祖，善继善述。<div id='poem_sentence_32_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1283665'>未几元昊，在西复悖。<div id='poem_sentence_33_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1283665'>谋臣勇将，连年讨伐。<div id='poem_sentence_34_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_1283665'>边民既困，国用亦乏。<div id='poem_sentence_35_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1283665'>厥后智高，忽尔猖獗。<div id='poem_sentence_36_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_1283665'>南岭东西，扰扰数月。<div id='poem_sentence_37_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1283665'>以时讨平，狄青之力。<div id='poem_sentence_38_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1283665'>靖康之难，言之汗浃！<div id='poem_sentence_39_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1283665'>二帝北巡，狼窠熊窟。<div id='poem_sentence_40_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1283665'>沙漠万里，风霜冽冽，胡尘扑面，惊弦惨骨。<div id='poem_sentence_41_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_1283665'>国祚若旒，孰任其责！<div id='poem_sentence_42_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_1283665'>赖有高宗，克绍前烈。<div id='poem_sentence_43_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_1283665'>匆遽渡江，心胆欲折。<div id='poem_sentence_44_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1283665'>皇天降监，风涛安帖。<div id='poem_sentence_45_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1283665'>所至成市，暂都于浙。<div id='poem_sentence_46_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_1283665'>颜亮凶燄，震撼六合。<div id='poem_sentence_47_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1283665'>投箠采石，意谓无越。<div id='poem_sentence_48_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1283665'>幸而倒戈，自取夷灭。<div id='poem_sentence_49_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_1283665'>寿皇履位，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/113/Comments/0")'>求贤如渴</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_50_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_1283665'>崇事高宗，孝心尤切。<div id='poem_sentence_51_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1283665'>二十八载，终始无缺。<div id='poem_sentence_52_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_1283665'>高宗上仙，哀号哽咽。<div id='poem_sentence_53_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_1283665'>四方来观，其容惨怛。<div id='poem_sentence_54_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1283665'>王业艰难，坦然明白。<div id='poem_sentence_55_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1283665'>今王嗣位，祖宗是则。<div id='poem_sentence_56_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1283665'>无湎于酒，无沈于色：色能荒人之心，酒能败人之德。<div id='poem_sentence_57_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_1283665'>以宰相为腹心，以台谏为耳目；<div id='poem_sentence_58_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_1283665'>以将帅为爪牙，以尚书为喉舌。<div id='poem_sentence_59_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_1283665'>登崇俊良，斥退奸蘖。<div id='poem_sentence_60_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_1283665'>勿谓天高，常若对越；<div id='poem_sentence_61_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_1283665'>勿谓民弱，实关治忽；<div id='poem_sentence_62_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_1283665'>勿俾祸起于萧墙，勿使患生于仓卒；<div id='poem_sentence_63_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_1283665'>勿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/142/Comments/0")'>私赏</span>以格公议，勿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/143/Comments/0")'>私刑</span>以亏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/143/Comments/1")'>国律</span>；<div id='poem_sentence_64_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1283665'>勿侮老成之人，勿贵无益之物；<div id='poem_sentence_65_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_1283665'>勿妄费生灵之财，勿妄兴土木之役；<div id='poem_sentence_66_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_1283665'>勿谓嚬笑之微而莫我知，勿谓号令之严而莫我逆。<div id='poem_sentence_67_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_1283665'>尽孝乃明主之治，论相乃人主之职。<div id='poem_sentence_68_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1283665'>圣言不可侮，人心不可咈。<div id='poem_sentence_69_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_1283665'>倾耳乎公卿之言，游心乎帝王之术。<div id='poem_sentence_70_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_1283665'>勿谓和议已成而不虑乎远图；<div id='poem_sentence_71_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_1283665'>勿谓大位已得而不恤乎小失。<div id='poem_sentence_72_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_1283665'>当效禹王，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/159/Comments/0")'>寸阴</span>是惜；<div id='poem_sentence_73_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_1283665'>当效文王，日昃不食。<div id='poem_sentence_74_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_1283665'>勿效夏桀，瑶台琼室；<div id='poem_sentence_75_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_1283665'>勿效商纣，斮涉剖直。<div id='poem_sentence_76_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_1283665'>如履薄冰，深虞没溺；<div id='poem_sentence_77_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_1283665'>如驭六马，切虞奔轶。<div id='poem_sentence_78_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_1283665'>勿谓微过，当绝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/171/Comments/0")'>芽蘖</span>；<div
