id='poem_sentence_79_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_1283665'>勿谓小患，当窒孔穴。<div id='poem_sentence_80_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_1283665'>左右前后，当用贤哲。<div id='poem_sentence_81_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_1283665'>王惟戒兹，民罔不悦。<div id='poem_sentence_82_1283665_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_83_1283665'>草茅作箴，敢告<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1283665", 1283665, "Clauses/179/Comments/0")'>司阙</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_83_1283665_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　秋，复陆伯寿书，贺其中选，并述近况。<div id='poem_1283437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复陆伯寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283437")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283437'>五月末间，竟以雨甚，不能遂湖上之集，兼又新得罪于人，意况不佳，虽欲陪款语而归心如飞，破雨东渡，但剧怅仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283437_comment'></div>伏辱台翰，恭审即日晚秋喜晴，拜命之馀，神人共相，台候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283437_comment'></div>舍试揭榜，伏承遂释褐于崇化堂前，众望所归，此选增重，凡在友朋之列者，意气为之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283437", 1283437, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>光鲜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283437_comment'></div>寿皇在位二十七年，与此选者六人：自明夭折，纯叟中废，何以强人意！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283437_comment'></div>新天子龙飞，而兄首膺此选，遂使新政有光，甚盛甚盛！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283437_comment'></div>方图专驰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1283437", 1283437, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>尺楮</span>上庆，遂成先辱，惶恐不可言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283437_comment'></div>时事日以新，天意未易测度，但看人事对副何如耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283437_comment'></div>泛泛君子不足以承当好运，犹庸庸小人不足以究竟向阴之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283437_comment'></div>「好恶只看屋下郎」，此乃观时运真法门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283437_comment'></div>今之专靠天者自不肯信耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283437_comment'></div>兄以为如何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283437_comment'></div>英杰满朝，无为丑虏所欺，若其叔侄兄弟犹相衔持，尚可偷旦夕之安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283437_comment'></div>不尔，则虏情未可测也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283437_comment'></div>亮自七月二十五日，一病不知人者两月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283437_comment'></div>自此日里不能吃饭，夜间不能上床，凡二十馀日，方渐渐较可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283437_comment'></div>入九月，吃饭打睡始能自齿于平人，然未至五更便睡不著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283437_comment'></div>望见暮景已自如此，不如早与一死为快脆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283437_comment'></div>自馀皆非所宜言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283437_comment'></div>托契之厚，不觉狂态又发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283437_comment'></div>勿使他人见之，幸甚，幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1283437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　三山吴允成曾作尉永康三年，陈亮是年冬补作序以送之。作品：送吴允成运干序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作吴元成，参见颜虚心《宋陈龙川先生亮年谱》第122页。）</span><div id='poem_1283486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送吴允成运干序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283486")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283486'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283486'>往三十年时，亮初有识知，犹记为士者必以文章行义自名，居官者必以政事书判自显，各务其实而极其所至，人各有能有不能，卒亦不敢强也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283486_comment'></div>自道德性命之说一兴，而寻常烂熟无所能解之人自托于其间，以端悫静深为体，以徐行缓语为用，务为不可穷测以盖其所无，一艺一能皆以为不足自通于圣人之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283486_comment'></div>于是天下之士始丧其所有，而不知适从矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283486_comment'></div>为士者耻言文章、行义，而曰「尽心知性」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283486_comment'></div>居官者耻言政事、书判，而曰「学道爱人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283486_comment'></div>相蒙相欺以尽废天下之实，则亦终于百事不理而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283486_comment'></div>及其徒既衰，而异时熟视不平者合力共攻之，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1283486", 1283486, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>无须之祸</span>，滥及平人，固其所自取者，而出反之惨乃至此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283486_comment'></div>三山吴允成，少以气自豪，出手取<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283486", 1283486, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>科目</span>，随辄得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283486_comment'></div>来尉永康，遇事风生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283486_comment'></div>一日，枉车过余，讲客主之礼，若见所畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283486_comment'></div>且语余：「子所交皆一世老苍，至等辈已是第三四行人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283486_comment'></div>叶同年为我言如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283486_comment'></div>我家世以官为家者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283486_comment'></div>我父自力于官事，而与世为忤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283486_comment'></div>子盍为我诵数前闻，而言其所以致此者」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283486_comment'></div>余惘然失叹，意以为虽知所从来而不敢言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283486_comment'></div>自是相与往来如旧故，纵谀其所长以暴白于一时，虽老于吏道者亦知敬其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283486_comment'></div>文章、行义，政事、书判，并举兼能而不可掩，而道德性命之说政自不相妨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283486_comment'></div>于其中间，余受<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1283486", 1283486, "Clauses/56/Comments/0")'>无须之祸</span>尤惨，而允成亦深察余心，左右扶持，虽惨不至于极，以此犹相欢而无间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283486_comment'></div>及其去永康，余将叙其本末以累其行李，而多病因循，念之耿耿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283486_comment'></div>后三年，始克为之，盖新天子龙飞之十二月九日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283486_comment'></div>而允成方俛首于将漕糟丘之职，若新为吏者，其志向岂有穷哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1283486_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　冬，为金华金元卿撰墓志铭，其子潚从学陈亮。作品：金元卿墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283693?labeling=true' target='_blank'>金元卿墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283693")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283693'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283693'>君讳大亨，字元卿，姓金氏，世居婺之金华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283693_comment'></div>曾大父赐，大父肇，父从政，皆不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283693_comment'></div>娶陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283693_comment'></div>子男三人：海、潚、泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283693_comment'></div>女三人：于松年、孙之本，其婿也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283693_comment'></div>幼未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283693_comment'></div>孙女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283693_comment'></div>以淳熙己酉二月丁亥卒于家，享年五十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283693_comment'></div>是岁十二月丙申，诸孤奉君葬于其邑赤松乡塘里原，君在时所营也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283693_comment'></div>而问铭于永康陈亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283693_comment'></div>潚尝从余游，君之于余甚谨，以故习知其家事，而得君之为人亦甚详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283693_comment'></div>君读书为士有绳尺，不求苟异于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283693_comment'></div>内行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1283693", 1283693, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>洁整</span>，于声色淡然，而不求人之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283693_comment'></div>及其为家也，以俭勤自将，铢积寸累，迄用有成，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283693", 1283693, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>豪取智笼</span>之术一切置不用，故无怨恶于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283693_comment'></div>晚岁治其室稍华，将以娱其亲之老也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283693_comment'></div>诸子皆使之学，而必欲知辛勤起家之不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283693_comment'></div>独使潚从四方师友游，劳费皆所不问，而不责其近功也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283693_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283693_comment'></div>使天下之人皆知人有常分，事有常程，安平之效，几计有馀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283693_comment'></div>撼动之力，时移难恃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283693_comment'></div>则郡县可以无条令而治，家道虽传之百世可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283693_comment'></div>而世常不足以知之，何哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283693_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1283693'>富，人所欲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283693_comment'></div>善，吾所独欲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283693_comment'></div>公之独也同之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283693_comment'></div>遗之以此，开之于彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283693_comment'></div>铭之深长，尚有以也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1283693_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　怀韩彦古作《满江红》（曾洗乾坤）<div id='poem_157267' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157267' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157267?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红 怀韩子师尚书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157267")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157267_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157267'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157267'>曾洗乾坤，问何事、雄图顿屈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157267'>试著眼、阶除当下，又添英物。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157267'>北向争衡幽愤在，南来遗恨狂酋失。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157267'>算凄凉、部曲几人存，三之一。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157267_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157267'>诸老尽，郎君出。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157267'>恩未报，家何恤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157267'>念横飞直上，有时还戢。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157267'>笑我只知存饱煖，感君元不论阶级。<div id='poem_sentence_7_157267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_157267'>休更上、百尺旧家楼，尘侵帙。<div id='poem_sentence_8_157267_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_157267'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_157267_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　撰陈思正墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283694' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283694' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283694?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陈思正墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283694")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283694_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283694'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283694'>思正，姓陈氏，讳端中，思正其字也，世为婺之永康人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283694_comment'></div>曾祖博，祖回，父子茂，皆不显于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283694_comment'></div>余尝铭陈性之之墓，叙永康之陈凡七族，而思正盖出于龙山之陈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283694_comment'></div>思正娶刘氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283694_comment'></div>子男四人：藻、棻、葵、蕃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283694_comment'></div>女六人，葛汝舟，刘景脩、刘祉、周确、胡汝济、胡楷，其婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283694_comment'></div>景脩甲辰进士，今为脩职郎、临安府富阳县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283694_comment'></div>孙男女八人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283694_comment'></div>以淳熙十六年九月二十六日卒于家，享年六十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283694_comment'></div>是年十一月壬申葬于横塘之原，祖茔之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283694_comment'></div>思正以意气自豪，视钱物如粪土，不为分毫后日计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283694_comment'></div>平生不欲其乡有不平之事、其人有不满之意，虽以此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1283694", 1283694, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>遭踬</span>而不悔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283694_comment'></div>族人尝小忿争，至反眼不相视，思正病且亟矣，呼而语之曰：「兄弟不当至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283694_comment'></div>我死，谁当为汝解之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283694_comment'></div>各为我饮一杯，还兄弟骨肉之旧，以此送我死，足矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283694_comment'></div>其人皆释然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283694_comment'></div>及其将绝也，语诸子曰：「吾意之所向不在人后，而家事如此，累汝曹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283694_comment'></div>我死，会客宜如礼，求一文以铭吾墓，毕我一身，任汝曹所欲为也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283694_comment'></div>其子衰绖踵门，与其同宗人亮言其事如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283694_comment'></div>余悲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283694_comment'></div>以思正之才智，知所缓急先后，而行之以义，宜何所不可，而动辄龃龉，可以言命矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283694_comment'></div>死又无传，则仁人君子之所不忍，而求之余则非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283694_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1283694'>将死犹欲人之无争，死后犹欲身之不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283694_comment'></div>嗟逝者之如斯，与草木而共尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283694_comment'></div>于其中间，圣贤为准。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283694_comment'></div>我独何人，铭以相殉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1283694_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　致书范东叔。作品：与范东叔龙图书。<div id='poem_1283463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283463?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与范东叔龙图<span class='inlineComment2'>（仲艺）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283463")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283463_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283463'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283463'>亮自顷一望台光，蒙所以温接奖与之意厚甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283463_comment'></div>连岁到行都，自顾踪迹日以陆沈，无颜数诣台屏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283463_comment'></div>但时与令侄少约问讯启处之详，慰此尊仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283463_comment'></div>初夏尝一到金陵，与章丈侍郎甚款，相羊泉石间，每玩所留字，必相与咏颂怅望良久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283463_comment'></div>章丈亦言右司甚迟其来，失此良款，尤用怏悒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283463_comment'></div>亮自七八月之交，一病垂死，今幸苟存残喘，百念皆已灰灭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283463_comment'></div>但尊敬大贤君子，耿然犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283463_comment'></div>亮窃惟提刑右司，西州人物之英，一朝簪绅之表，文章议论为时宗工，道德风流在王左右，禁林两地，汉廷莫之或先，翻然而去，不可复驻，虽高节懔然，而徘徊恋主之义尚有可思者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283463_comment'></div>持节湖外，彼民何其幸也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283463_comment'></div>族兄君举遂获同寮，托契至厚，今兹游处其间，乐当不可涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283463_comment'></div>使轺联翩得贤，仁言仁闻交发并见，无从一游其间，睹此盛事，怅仰而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283463_comment'></div>时事反覆无常，天运所至，亦看人事对副如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283463_comment'></div>泛泛君子不足承当好运，犹庸庸小人不足以究竟向阴之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283463_comment'></div>人不自力而一委之天，岂不殆哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283463_comment'></div>亮一亲戚梁锐为郴阳判官，道出麾下，义当伏谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283463_comment'></div>渠虽北人，今与亮为邻且三四十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283463_comment'></div>亮非敢以一书为之先容，倘赐温颜垂接，孤寒小官，生死万幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283463_comment'></div>渠蹉跎选调，不善俯仰，莅官十四五考，而举者只一二人，生硬自信，可为一笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283463_comment'></div>右司加意怜之，固其所愿而不敢望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283463_comment'></div>亮开岁又随众一到春宫，包羞至此，只欲为遮拦门户计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283463_comment'></div>若更不遂，且当浮沈里闬，与田夫野老为伍，无所复望于今世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283463_comment'></div>新天子龙飞，寤寐英贤，决非湖外所能久留，纶涣一下，锋车鼎来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283463_comment'></div>更冀崇护寝餗，终为四海一出素蕴，不胜千万之祷！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1283463_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　再度致书范东叔。作品：与范东叔龙图又书。<div id='poem_1283463' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283463' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283463?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与范东叔龙图<span class='inlineComment2'>（仲艺）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283463")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283463_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283463'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283463'>亮自顷一望台光，蒙所以温接奖与之意厚甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283463_comment'></div>连岁到行都，自顾踪迹日以陆沈，无颜数诣台屏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283463_comment'></div>但时与令侄少约问讯启处之详，慰此尊仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283463_comment'></div>初夏尝一到金陵，与章丈侍郎甚款，相羊泉石间，每玩所留字，必相与咏颂怅望良久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283463_comment'></div>章丈亦言右司甚迟其来，失此良款，尤用怏悒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283463_comment'></div>亮自七八月之交，一病垂死，今幸苟存残喘，百念皆已灰灭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283463_comment'></div>但尊敬大贤君子，耿然犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283463_comment'></div>亮窃惟提刑右司，西州人物之英，一朝簪绅之表，文章议论为时宗工，道德风流在王左右，禁林两地，汉廷莫之或先，翻然而去，不可复驻，虽高节懔然，而徘徊恋主之义尚有可思者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283463_comment'></div>持节湖外，彼民何其幸也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283463_comment'></div>族兄君举遂获同寮，托契至厚，今兹游处其间，乐当不可涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283463_comment'></div>使轺联翩得贤，仁言仁闻交发并见，无从一游其间，睹此盛事，怅仰而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283463_comment'></div>时事反覆无常，天运所至，亦看人事对副如何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283463_comment'></div>泛泛君子不足承当好运，犹庸庸小人不足以究竟向阴之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283463_comment'></div>人不自力而一委之天，岂不殆哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283463_comment'></div>亮一亲戚梁锐为郴阳判官，道出麾下，义当伏谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283463_comment'></div>渠虽北人，今与亮为邻且三四十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283463_comment'></div>亮非敢以一书为之先容，倘赐温颜垂接，孤寒小官，生死万幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283463_comment'></div>渠蹉跎选调，不善俯仰，莅官十四五考，而举者只一二人，生硬自信，可为一笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283463_comment'></div>右司加意怜之，固其所愿而不敢望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283463_comment'></div>亮开岁又随众一到春宫，包羞至此，只欲为遮拦门户计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283463_comment'></div>若更不遂，且当浮沈里闬，与田夫野老为伍，无所复望于今世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283463_comment'></div>新天子龙飞，寤寐英贤，决非湖外所能久留，纶涣一下，锋车鼎来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283463_comment'></div>更冀崇护寝餗，终为四海一出素蕴，不胜千万之祷！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1283463_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>　复楼大防郎中书。<div id='poem_1283436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283436' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283436?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复楼大防郎中<span class='inlineComment2'>（钥）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283436")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283436_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283436'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283436'>亮病中昏倒，虽领台翰，初不晓只从门前过，将谓取道永康邑中，西望第剧怅然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283436_comment'></div>若知犹宿留界牌，固将忍死抬出，以求一见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283436_comment'></div>重蒙诲劄之赐，今已就安，方悟向来初不必追逐于双溪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283436_comment'></div>尊仰愈不自胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283436_comment'></div>恭审即日晚秋，晴雨不定，郎署多暇，天人叶相，台候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283436_comment'></div>温诏趣还，犹从郎署，殊未厌舆望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283436_comment'></div>台端谏省，非公其孰宜之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283436_comment'></div>庆福当需此时，今不足为门下道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283436_comment'></div>亮平生百事并在人后，只有一健耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283436_comment'></div>望见暮景，天已与夺之，憔悴病苦，反以求死为快脆，其他尚复何说！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283436_comment'></div>汉朝公卿皆伟人，而英俊尽布朝列，虏情叵测，深恐为其所侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283436_comment'></div>若其叔侄兄弟犹相衔持，尚可偷一日之安；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283436_comment'></div>不尔，无使患起虑表，有辜上下动色相庆之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283436_comment'></div>私布下悃，勿令重得罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283436_comment'></div>亮更不别布台闳问福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283436_comment'></div>有可驱委者，愿听约束。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1283436_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　跋朱熹《送写照郭秀才序》后。作品：跋朱晦庵送写照郭秀才序后。<div id='poem_1283506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋朱晦庵送写照郭秀才序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283506")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283506'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283506'>往时广汉张敬夫、东莱吕伯恭，于天下之义理自谓极其精微，而世亦以是推之，虽前一辈亦心知其莫能先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283506_comment'></div>余犹及见二人者，听其讲论，亦稍详其精深纡馀，若于物情无所不致其尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283506_comment'></div>而世所谓阴阳卜筮，书画伎术，及凡世间可动心娱目之事，皆斥去弗顾，若将浼我者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283506_comment'></div>晚得从新安朱元晦游，见其论古圣贤之用心，平易简直，欲尽摆后世讲师相授、流俗相传、既已入于人心而未易解之说，以径趋圣贤心地而发挥其妙，以与一世人共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283506_comment'></div>其不得见于世，则圣贤之命脉犹在，而人心终有时而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1283506", 1283506, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>开明</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283506_comment'></div>其于经文，稍不平易简直则置而不论，以为是非圣贤之本旨，若欲刊而去之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283506_comment'></div>余为之感慨于天地之大义，而抱大不满于秦、汉以来诸君子，思欲解其沈痼以从新安之志，而未能也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283506_comment'></div>然而于阴阳卜筮，书画伎术，凡世所有而未易去者，皆存而信之，乃与张、吕异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283506_comment'></div>其于郭叔瞻之能，尤爱而喜之不厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283506_comment'></div>岂悦物而不留于物者固若此乎，抑世所谓画师之能，皆未能窥叔瞻之心地而不可弃乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283506_comment'></div>故余于叔瞻无旧故，而为诸公道其所长不容已，亦因以见秦汉以来诸君子犹烦新安之刮剔，而后圣贤之心事可得而尽白也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283506_comment'></div>叔瞻力求余跋，因叙其本末如此，试以呈似新安云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1283506_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　书赵永丰训之行录后。<div id='poem_1283517' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283517' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283517?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书赵永丰训之行录后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283517")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283517_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283517'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283517'>太史公论婢妾之引决，出于计画无理之甚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283517_comment'></div>而英雄俯仰以全一死者，将以有为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283517_comment'></div>而孟子论义有重于死，虽圣贤不得而避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283517_comment'></div>人固难于一死，而一死之难又如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283517_comment'></div>国家遭阳九之厄，能以死拒虏者固自有数，而禁卒内溃，人不知义极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283517_comment'></div>身为宗室以当百里之寄，不爱一死以明大义，此圣贤所不得而避者，其死岂不壮哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283517_comment'></div>方天下太平，天子有事边功，使守在四夷，而公独知其为祸乱之萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283517_comment'></div>及金虏剪中国如枯槁，公又欲率<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283517", 1283517, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>义师</span>以沮遏其锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283517_comment'></div>推公之志而揆公之才，固非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283517", 1283517, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>自分</span>于一死者，义之所在，不约而自隐其中之所存耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283517_comment'></div>此天下之所知，而人之所以尚其子孙者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283517_comment'></div>张巡之死义，岂不明甚，而犹有待于韩李之秉笔者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283517_comment'></div>朝廷之旌死节不踰时，岂待人言而后明哉，殆未请耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283517_comment'></div>天人报应，尚堕渺茫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283517_comment'></div>上下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283517", 1283517, "Clauses/36/Comments/0")'>融合</span>，实关激劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283517_comment'></div>天下士固不少为赵公设也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283517_comment'></div>公之孙彦橚出其始末以示亮，因书以归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283517_comment'></div>新天子龙飞之十日也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1283517_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年6月11日</a>　六月十一日送叶正则如江陵，作《祝英台近》（驾扁舟）<div id='poem_157246' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157246' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157246?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祝英台近 六月十一日送叶正则如江陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年6月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157246")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157246_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157246'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157246'>驾扁舟，冲剧暑，千里江上去。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157246'>夜宿晨兴，一一旧时路。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157246'>百年忘了旬头，被人钻破，故纸里、是争雄处。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157246_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157246'>怎生诉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157246'>欲待细与分疏，其如有凭据。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157246'>包裹生鱼，活底怎遭遇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157246_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157246'>相逢樽酒何时，征衫容易，君去也、自家须住。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_157246_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年7月</a>　七月送丘宗卿使虏，作《三部乐》词。（小屈穹庐）<div id='poem_157207' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157207' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157207?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三部乐 七月送丘宗卿使北</a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157207")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157207_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157207'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157207'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_157207", 157207, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>小屈</span>穹庐，但<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_157207", 157207, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>二满三平</span>，共劳均佚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157207'>人中龙虎，本为明时而出。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157207'>只合是、端坐王朝，看指挥整办，扫荡飘忽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157207'>也持汉节，聊过旧家宫室。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157207_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157207'>西风又还带暑，把征衫著上，有时披拂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157207'>休将看花泪眼，闻弦病骨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157207'>对遗民、有如皎日。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157207'>行万里、依然故物。<div id='poem_sentence_7_157207_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_157207'>入奏几策，天下里、终定于一。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_157207_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　冬，妻弟何少嘉死，后有祭文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　十月十六，作《彩凤飞》词寿钱伯同。（人立玉）<span class='inlineComment2'>（此阕当作于淳熙末、绍熙初，约1188至1190年前后，附于此。）</span><div id='poem_157260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157260?labeling=true' target='_blank'>彩凤舞 十月十六日寿钱伯同</a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157260")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157260'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157260'>人立玉，天如水，特地如何撰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157260'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_157260", 157260, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>海南沈</span>烧著，欲寒犹暖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157260'>算从头，有多少、厚德阴功，人家上，一一旧时香案。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157260_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157260'>㬠经惯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157260'>小驻吾州才尔，依然欢声满。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157260'>莫也教、公子王孙眼见。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157260'>这些儿、颖脱处，高出书卷。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157260'>经纶自入手，不了判断。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157260_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年12月</a>　十二月，狱事再急。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　撰凌夫人何氏墓志铭，夫人子坚，从陈亮学。作品：凌夫人何氏墓志铭。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第68页。）</span><div id='poem_1283712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283712?labeling=true' target='_blank'>凌夫人何氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283712")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283712_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283712'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283712'>绍兴之季，余客临安凡三岁，父母愿其有室而命之归也，义乌何茂恭欲妻以其兄之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283712_comment'></div>于是义乌之富言何氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283712_comment'></div>茂恭兄弟俱能文，而茂恭声问尤伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283712_comment'></div>余贫甚，惧不得当也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283712_comment'></div>诸凡茂恭姻党皆以为不然，独武义刘君叔向力赞其说，且语吾父趣纳币。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283712_comment'></div>又明年，乾道改元，余往就姻焉，姻党咸在，而叔向之妻，茂恭之女弟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283712_comment'></div>于是茂恭之母年七十馀，两子一女，相与为命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283712_comment'></div>门户方张，和气充满，入其门者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283712", 1283712, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>油然</span>生敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283712_comment'></div>爱诸孙女如女，然而尤念吾妻为类己，以故刘氏姑视之特好，而叔向于余亦加厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283712_comment'></div>茂恭罢官吉之永新，诸公争知其才，旁观者亦以横飞直上为不难也，而壬辰之春，一日无疾而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283712_comment'></div>又三四年，母亦下世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283712_comment'></div>叔向与其妻会葬，而叔向死焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283712_comment'></div>茂恭之妻未几亦死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283712_comment'></div>吾妻之父以淳熙癸卯七月之晦，其死如茂恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283712_comment'></div>独刘氏姑与吾外姑尚无恙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283712_comment'></div>丙午之春，俱集于外氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283712_comment'></div>刘氏姑语余曰：「我生于七月二十八日，岁烦遣礼而不一顾我，如不遣也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283712_comment'></div>余笑曰：「是固其初心，今当偿之耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283712_comment'></div>及期而往，出门迎笑，大会亲族，劝酬达旦，而意殊无已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283712_comment'></div>是夜，将继之以乐，杯未行而举手扶头曰病，余往视之，则死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283712_comment'></div>嗟夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283712_comment'></div>盛衰相寻，本不足计，而生死之际，其谁为之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283712_comment'></div>乃使其兄弟之死如一人，余亦不自知其哭之恸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283712_comment'></div>二十馀年之间，为月凡几，为日凡几，何氏刘氏其变如此之亟，而余穷盖如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283712_comment'></div>变通之道，独至于余而遂息耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283712_comment'></div>是又可叹已矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283712_comment'></div>夫人姓何氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283712_comment'></div>曾大父京，大父先，父矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283712_comment'></div>年十七归刘氏，死时五十三矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283712_comment'></div>子男三人：三复，监衢州北较务；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283712_comment'></div>三友，三进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283712_comment'></div>女三人：嫁黄华、黄述古，皆佳子弟，而述古尝以国子上礼部；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283712_comment'></div>幼未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283712_comment'></div>孙男三人，女三人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283712_comment'></div>夫人志意疏豁，语言明朗，遇亲族上下，不问贫富贵贱皆有恩纪，大略似其父而不类妇人女子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283712_comment'></div>然乐人之饮而不自饮，终日言笑而无可择之言，闺门懿行虽处子不能过，岂其得阴之正德而无其幽吝之气耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283712_comment'></div>此亦妇人之杰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283712_comment'></div>始，叔向之葬，在家傍五里金塘之东原，诸孤将以丁未十一月二十三日合葬，而谓亮：「何以使吾母虽死而不亡乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283712_comment'></div>亮固力不足者，将藉友朋以自助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283712_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_1283712'>志念豁然，赍之以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283712_comment'></div>葬从其夫，畀尔孙子。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1283712_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　三次入狱，作书与章德茂，言朱熹、辛弃疾相念甚至，无时不相闻。作品：与章德茂侍郎书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年2月</a>　春二月，出狱。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　作谢陈同知启。<div id='poem_1283412' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283412' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283412?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢陈同知启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283412")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283412_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283412'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283412'>鹿非产于庖厨，系惟其命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283412_comment'></div>盆岂干于日月，戴掩其明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283412_comment'></div>嗟哉平人，有此奇祸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283412_comment'></div>肯茹冤于圣世，必白事于群公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283412_comment'></div>卒以微生，自归洪造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283412_comment'></div>敢缘雅故，妄出等夷！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283412_comment'></div>伏念某少览古书，恐遂流于无用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283412_comment'></div>晚更世故，始渐见于难通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283412_comment'></div>岂求田问舍之是专，亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283412", 1283412, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>闭门造车</span>之可验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283412_comment'></div>一毫以上，通缓急于里闾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283412_comment'></div>终岁之间，仅饱煖其妻子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283412_comment'></div>怨之所在，明者不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283412_comment'></div>苟有邪心，虽路人亦甘于就絷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283412_comment'></div>至遭毒手，盖坐客尽知其为冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283412_comment'></div>第以当路之见憎，况复旁观之共谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283412_comment'></div>怨家白撰于其外，狱吏文致于其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283412_comment'></div>俨然凶人，无一可免；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283412_comment'></div>置之诏狱，凡百谓何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283412_comment'></div>诘其来繇，可为惊骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283412_comment'></div>逮风波之既定，亦事状之皦然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283412_comment'></div>多取天地之虚名，所宜受罚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283412_comment'></div>犹有鬼神之明證，终赖持平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283412_comment'></div>国有人焉，事无冤者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283412_comment'></div>此盖伏遇枢密相公：英姿不世，学力绝人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283412_comment'></div>无遗憾于天，不求同于俗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283412_comment'></div>古心古貌，读前辈未见之书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283412_comment'></div>先觉先知，得累圣不传之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283412_comment'></div>虽泊然于世念，岂得已于时须！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283412_comment'></div>刑名度数之诸家，源流具涉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283412_comment'></div>规矩准绳之大器，本末兼通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283412_comment'></div>以典民彝，以断国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283412_comment'></div>方求万事之合律，不忍一夫之纳沟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283412_comment'></div>畴昔少年，许其托契；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283412_comment'></div>晚节末路，不啻如新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283412_comment'></div>岂敢以冤而自言，固已无简而不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283412_comment'></div>恍如一梦，尽忘井邑之故吾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283412_comment'></div>愿以馀年，自附门墙之小物。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1283412_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　作谢罗尚书启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　作谢郑侍郎启。<div id='poem_1283417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢郑侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283417")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283417'>文致诋欺之法，久矣不行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283417_comment'></div>生死肉骨之恩，今焉创见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283417_comment'></div>事实关于国体，道允惬于人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283417_comment'></div>曾是馀年，无非大造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283417_comment'></div>伏念某少尝有志于当世，晚乃自安于一廛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283417_comment'></div>身名俱沈，置而不论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283417_comment'></div>衣食才足，示以无求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283417_comment'></div>人真谓其有馀，心固疑其克取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283417_comment'></div>而况奴仆射日生之利，子弟为岁晏之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283417_comment'></div>怨有所归，谓可从于勿恤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283417_comment'></div>内常无歉，岂自意其难明！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283417_comment'></div>俄而积世之冤，端若从天而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283417_comment'></div>涂人相杀，罪及异乡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283417_comment'></div>当路见憎，勘从旁郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283417_comment'></div>恟恟之势可畏，炎炎之焰若何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283417_comment'></div>一死一生，足累久长之福；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283417_comment'></div>十目十手，具知来历之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283417_comment'></div>莫弭人言，爰兴诏狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283417_comment'></div>是非错出，真伪相淆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283417_comment'></div>不以大公而并观，孰从众證而细考？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283417_comment'></div>附法以杀，虽百喙以何言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283417_comment'></div>出意而行，恐单词而无据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283417_comment'></div>念天下之有冤士，盖古人之所用心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283417_comment'></div>坦然周道之平，翕若汉庭之允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283417_comment'></div>悉归绳尺，犹有鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283417_comment'></div>此盖伏遇判部侍郎，以独见之明，持甚平之论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283417_comment'></div>学期圣秘，肯姑徇于俗传；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283417_comment'></div>心与天通，宁曲从于世好！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283417_comment'></div>正色不挠，以法自将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283417_comment'></div>念曾子之慨然，昔闻斯勇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283417_comment'></div>使宣尼而尚在，今见其刚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283417_comment'></div>纯意国家，不遗微小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283417_comment'></div>拯匹夫于焚溺，惧损万分；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283417_comment'></div>办大事于从容，可观一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283417_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1283417", 1283417, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>弥纶</span>妙手，经济长才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283417_comment'></div>古道今时，合为全体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283417_comment'></div>正人端士，朗在下风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283417_comment'></div>萃之微躯，昭厥来世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283417_comment'></div>阖门六十口，分无免矣之期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283417_comment'></div>行法二百年，未有若斯之懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283417_comment'></div>自今以始，制命知归。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1283417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　作谢何正言启。<div id='poem_1283419' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283419' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283419?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢何正言启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283419")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283419_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283419'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283419'>肃此台纲，无非体国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283419_comment'></div>求其情实，要岂容心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283419_comment'></div>方物论之正胜，匪诏狱而莫定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283419_comment'></div>持平以听，惟是之归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283419_comment'></div>死则匪伊，活之造次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283419_comment'></div>伏念某徒有凌高厉空之志，本无应时适用之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283419_comment'></div>同故旧之戚休，乃名「任侠」；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283419_comment'></div>通里闾之缓急，见谓「豪强」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283419_comment'></div>欲为饱暖之谋，自速摧残之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283419_comment'></div>谤出事情之外，百喙莫明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283419_comment'></div>变生意料之馀，三肱并折。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283419_comment'></div>友朋私忧其身后，儿女环泣于生前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283419_comment'></div>吾道非邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283419_comment'></div>一穷至此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283419_comment'></div>男儿死尔，正命谓何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283419_comment'></div>台评欲付之大公，天定竟还于无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283419_comment'></div>国是所系，恩私有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283419_comment'></div>此盖伏遇正言执事，挺特性资，屹然山立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283419_comment'></div>优游心事，湛若镜平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283419_comment'></div>尽洗<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1283419", 1283419, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>偏阿</span>，具知情伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283419_comment'></div>举一世之端人正士，莫之或先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283419_comment'></div>合二百年之忠言嘉谟，于斯并建。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283419_comment'></div>故虽小小，亦使昭昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283419_comment'></div>况蝼蚁之微生，系天地之一命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283419_comment'></div>苟私意皆可致人于死，则圣朝容有倚法之威！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283419_comment'></div>欲民无冤，为国远虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283419_comment'></div>周道有小人之视，各使适平；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283419_comment'></div>汉纲无吏治之奸，本非过察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283419_comment'></div>怅馀年之何用，合四体以为公。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1283419_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　作谢王丞相书。<div id='poem_1283422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与王季海丞相<span class='inlineComment2'>（淮）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283422")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283422'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283422'>亮窃惟大丞相首秉国钧，士之归心门下者，岂但诚服德谊，要亦不能无利于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283422_comment'></div>天下之士，其无求于世者固少，而吾之权又足以奔走天下之人，则其势固然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283422_comment'></div>独亮之于门下，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>心悦诚服</span>而未尝自言，丞相亦不得而知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283422_comment'></div>岁杪尝欲略布诚悃，而迫归仓卒，又成自外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283422_comment'></div>入春以来，贫病交攻，更无一日好况，虽欲拜一书以叙其本末，亦复因循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283422_comment'></div>私切自念：向者丞相于客退之后，促膝而命之坐，使得款语良久，且忧其无用于时，欲使得一试，恩意恳恳，虽父兄之于子弟不是过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283422_comment'></div>亮而自外于门下，是曾犬马之不若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283422_comment'></div>故尝愿自献其愚忠，惟丞相审听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283422_comment'></div>圣上天日之表，本非苟安于无事，而又英明<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>夐绝</span>古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283422_comment'></div>前后任相，非一人矣，盖亦有所甚属意者，而倚权以行其私，上亦终厌之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283422_comment'></div>独丞相布诚心，开公道，进退则采之舆论，废置则付之准绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283422_comment'></div>事上之日久，而上亦察其无他也，故确然信用而不疑，久任而不拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283422_comment'></div>章圣皇帝所谓「王旦事朕之日久，而朕亦察之熟矣，卿等有事但与王旦商量」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283422_comment'></div>故在中书十四五年，而上不以为疑、下不以为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283422_comment'></div>丞相今日真有祖风矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283422_comment'></div>甚盛甚休，非馀人所可望其阃域也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283422_comment'></div>亮独有所甚忧者，秦丞相主和，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>薰炙</span>天地，身享不过十五年，又六年而和败，通止二十一年耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283422_comment'></div>近者乙酉、丙戌之和，本非有一定之计，而今亦二十一年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283422_comment'></div>此其势恐不能久也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283422_comment'></div>南北分裂，于今六十年，此天数之当复也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283422_comment'></div>阿骨打之兴，于今近八十年，正胡运之当衰也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283422_comment'></div>天下一统，犹不能以五六十年无事于其间，必有水旱盗贼乘时窃发之变，况南北之势而欲三十年苟安，盖亦甚难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283422_comment'></div>天下无事，上之所以信任宰相者，他人所不得而间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283422_comment'></div>一旦缓急，丞相能保上之终任我乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283422_comment'></div>奉身而退，在丞相本非难事，然平时之觖望于我者，能保其不以我为奇货乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283422_comment'></div>无事则我享其福，有事则人当其难，此又非丞相之素心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283422_comment'></div>抱不哭之孩儿则当之而不辞，肩千钧之重负则赧然而自退，此又丞相之所当耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283422_comment'></div>亦尝以区区<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>管见</span>窥测圣意，缓急之所用，决非今日之所用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283422_comment'></div>一辈无赖，平居大言以诳人，交结以自鬻，盖亦有许其真能办事者，上安得不疑其可用乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283422_comment'></div>布之边徼，付之繁剧，人亦往往指目之矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283422_comment'></div>异时误国，识者当议丞相之不早计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283422_comment'></div>丞相今日纵未能尽收召天下之人才，当一一知其姓名，某人可当何任，某人可办何事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283422_comment'></div>四方之将帅，当一一察其能否，某人可当一面，某人可临一阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283422_comment'></div>边陲之急慢，粮草之虚实，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/114/Comments/0")'>兵卒</span>之强弱，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>城壁</span>之坚脆，历然在目，朗然在心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283422_comment'></div>一旦缓急，则从容为上言之，使上有知人未尽之叹，天下有事故难量之识，虽其号有才力者，亦固在吾驱使间耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283422_comment'></div>一辈无赖不得群起而误国，其为天下国家之福，岂<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/126/Comments/0")'>浅浅</span>哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283422_comment'></div>丞相虽长秉国钧，公论当不以为过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283422_comment'></div>范文正公所谓「身安而后国家可保」者，于丞相见之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283422_comment'></div>愿丞相详入思虑，以幸斯世，非亮一人之私言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283422_comment'></div>丞相苟以为然，则亮又将有裨千虑之一得者，继此以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283422_comment'></div>亮向尝言叶适之文学与其为人，此众所共知，丞相亦尝首肯之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283422_comment'></div>此人极有思虑，又心事和平，不肯随时翻覆，既有时名，又取甲科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283422_comment'></div>今一任回，改官，于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>格例</span>极易拈掇，丞相若拔擢而用之，必将有为报效者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283422_comment'></div>但秀才要索事分，若使之随例久候于逆旅，恐非其所能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283422_comment'></div>今已馀两月，丞相若于半月间那辍一差遣与之，徐议拔擢，亦无不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283422_comment'></div>薛叔似文学虽不及适，然识虑精密，心事和平，盖亦不减。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283422_comment'></div>向因面对，上亦意其可用，丞相盖已将顺上意矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283422_comment'></div>若并收此人，更与一迁，而适代之，上必不以为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283422_comment'></div>是丞相一举而得两士，亦足以厌满天下之公论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283422_comment'></div>亮当以五十口保任其终始可信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283422_comment'></div>其次如陈谦之文学识虑，施迈之心事和平，亦不宜久在掌故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283422_comment'></div>亮固愿使多士尽出门下，岂敢以一时之私，妄有所论荐，此亦效忠之一事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283422_comment'></div>事之所当言、心之所欲言者无限，今直未敢<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_52_1283422", 1283422, "Clauses/179/Comments/0")'>缕缕</span>耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1283422_comment'></div>丞相苟察其忠诚，则我决不敢于此遂已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1283422_comment'></div>惓惓之心，伏冀钧恕，幸甚，幸甚！</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1283422_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　作谢留丞相启。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　作谢葛知院启。<div id='poem_1283410' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283410' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283410?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢葛知院启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283410")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283410_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283410'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283410'>人小有才，未知死所，世皆欲杀，要岂公心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283410_comment'></div>惟爱士出于至诚，则恤刑视其大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283410_comment'></div>门墙旧物，蝼蚁微生，鸣其积冤，纳之洪造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283410_comment'></div>伏念某少时跌宕，久遂阔疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283410_comment'></div>学剑何止不成，徒存逸想；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283410_comment'></div>读书非求甚解，第采高标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283410_comment'></div>谩曰古心，不入俗眼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283410_comment'></div>既置身于无用，宜取祸以难明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283410_comment'></div>下流而致缙绅之见推，从何自取？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283410_comment'></div>穷居而使衣食之粗足，似若无因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283410_comment'></div>谓其豪强，处以任侠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283410_comment'></div>加虚谤于实事，入信语于疑心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283410_comment'></div>内揣甚安，誉不为喜而毁不为沮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283410_comment'></div>外传大甚，恶欲其死而爱欲其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283410_comment'></div>酝在平时，合成奇祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283410_comment'></div>重以当涂之立意，加之众怨之凿空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283410_comment'></div>人与千金，未能半信；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283410_comment'></div>家置一喙，犹有后言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283410_comment'></div>遂烦诏狱之兴，允谓事情之审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283410_comment'></div>不胜谗者，尚及今兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283410_comment'></div>非庙论之至平，盖残生之永已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283410_comment'></div>此盖伏遇知院相公，以绝人之量，涵盖世之英；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283410_comment'></div>阖辟往来，归之无事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283410_comment'></div>是非好恶，泯于不争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283410_comment'></div>方其为韦布之时，固已有公辅之器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283410_comment'></div>较艺轶出，肯矜衒于己能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283410_comment'></div>奕世嗣兴，况践更于时变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283410_comment'></div>收天下之小以为大，合人情之异以为同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283410_comment'></div>扬历班行，从容廊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283410_comment'></div>饥溺关于禹、稷，指挥定于萧、曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283410_comment'></div>对众一言，群吏耸闻而加审；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283410_comment'></div>从旁四顾，同列熟视以生嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283410_comment'></div>兴言有识之知几，安得无故而杀士？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283410_comment'></div>为国远虑，欲民无冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283410_comment'></div>当二三大臣之同心，何往非福；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283410_comment'></div>使亿万斯年之受祜，有庆惟刑！</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1283410_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　作谢胡参政启。<div id='poem_1283411' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283411' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283411?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢胡参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283411")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283411_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283411'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283411'>并建豪英，获际不冤之世；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283411_comment'></div>苟全性命，颇思当痛之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283411_comment'></div>虽以自怜，敢不知幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283411_comment'></div>伏念某立志虽广，受才则疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283411_comment'></div>少不如人，所向墙壁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283411_comment'></div>老之将至，乃挂网罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283411_comment'></div>苟有一迹之可疑，岂逃十目之所指！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283411_comment'></div>自嗟命薄，适值途穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283411_comment'></div>一口传虚，絷路人而为罪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283411_comment'></div>三年置对，任狱吏之便文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283411_comment'></div>不思讼者之谓谁，但使仇人之逞志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283411_comment'></div>鞠之又鞠，疑于无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283411_comment'></div>杀一不辜，惧损奕世无疆之福；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283411_comment'></div>凡百君子，易生私忧过计之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283411_comment'></div>欲究尽于物情，终上干于庙论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283411_comment'></div>此盖伏遇参政相公，为国远虑，作时孚先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283411_comment'></div>称物平施，出一代经纶之手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283411_comment'></div>议狱缓死，佐九重断制之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283411_comment'></div>欲使民瞑目以无言，必自我平心而取决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283411_comment'></div>拾一生于九死，宁勿药无妄之灾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283411_comment'></div>付万事于大公，岂施恩不报之所！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283411_comment'></div>有来私谢，未泯常情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1283411_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d2b694de65484f049e259473f9aac82e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d2b694de65484f049e259473f9aac82e");'><span id='d2b694de65484f049e259473f9aac82e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1194')">1193-1194年</a>，51-52岁</div><div id='d2b694de65484f049e259473f9aac82e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年7月</a>　七月，家祭，有告高、曾祖文。作品：告高曾祖文。<div id='poem_1283799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283799' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283799?labeling=true' target='_blank'>告高曾祖文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283799")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283799_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283799'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283799'>维绍熙四年岁次癸丑，秋七月乙丑朔，十有三日丁丑，孝玄孙承事郎新签书建康军节度判官厅公事陈亮，同妻何氏，男沆、瀹、沃、涣、涵，女缪、缯，谨以家殽常馔致奠于我高祖考贺公、高祖妣李氏安人、曾祖考知元公、曾祖妣吕氏安人之灵，而言曰：我高祖蚤世，高祖妣以盛年守一子而克有立，丙午、丁未之间赴京城守御，随大将刘延庆死于固子门外，不复归骨于乡井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283799_comment'></div>故我高祖妣与曾祖妣妇姑相依，为陈氏再世之墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283799_comment'></div>我叔祖高安府君每以此墓必福陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283799_comment'></div>高安由特奏名主筠之高安簿，则指墓而语亮曰：「是必为福，福其在汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283799_comment'></div>是其为墓也十有二年而后生汝，此非人力，其殆天乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283799_comment'></div>亮皇恐再拜而不敢与闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283799_comment'></div>高安既殁，十年之间，亮两以罪系棘寺，实为我祖先之羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283799_comment'></div>绍熙癸丑之夏，天子亲阅礼部进士于庭，拔一卷子于众中，许以渊源而寘诸选首，拆其号，则亮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283799_comment'></div>亮之不肖，安能欺上圣之耳目，岂亦有天乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283799_comment'></div>墓真能为福乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283799_comment'></div>再世不能自有其墓，而集其遗泽于亮身乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283799_comment'></div>心所不安，推其所自，高祖之魂，随祷而至，伉俪同食，飨于乃位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283799_comment'></div>异时亮荣，视所招至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283799_comment'></div>孙祖绵眇，先绪恐坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283799_comment'></div>履冰之敬，非以为伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283799_comment'></div>水陆之品，岂不欲备，力所未能，则再三四。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1283799_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年7月</a>　七月，家祭，有告祖、考文。作品：告祖考文。<div id='poem_1283800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>告祖考文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283800")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283800'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283800'>维绍熙四年岁次癸丑，秋七月乙丑朔，十有四日戊寅，孝孙承事郎新签书建康军节度判官厅公事陈亮，同妻何氏，男沆、瀹、沃、涣、涵，女缪、缯等，谨以家殽常馔致奠于我皇祖三六承节、皇祖妣黄氏八孺人、皇考四二府君、皇妣黄氏七八孺人之墓，而言曰：昔皇妣之生我，年才十有四，皇祖、皇祖妣鞠我而教以学，冀其必有立于斯世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283800_comment'></div>而谓其必能魁多士也，故尝形诸梦寐，状元为童汝能，以为此吾孙也，少则名亮以汝能，而字以同甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283800_comment'></div>惓惓恳恳之意，虽取笑于乡人而不恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283800_comment'></div>及亮年二十有六，易名曰亮，而首贡于乡，而皇祖下世已十阅月，皇祖妣盖整一年又三月矣，皇妣且四年而未葬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283800_comment'></div>越二十六年，始见录于礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283800_comment'></div>及对策大廷，天子拔诸众中而置之首选，曾弗涉于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283800_comment'></div>上恩深厚，兢惧无地自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283800_comment'></div>我皇祖之梦至是始验，而不知所谓童汝能者果何祥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283800_comment'></div>我先人弃不肖孤而去，亦整二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283800_comment'></div>被天子之命服而不能归荣其先，得罪于天，其来既久，茕然一身，又将谁咎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283800_comment'></div>天地无穷，顶踵蒙恩，没身论报，恐死无门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283800_comment'></div>归告诸墓，指日为誓：亲不能报，报君勿替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283800_comment'></div>七十年间，大责有归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283800_comment'></div>非毕大事，心实耻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283800_comment'></div>惟我再世，忘其不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283800_comment'></div>尚想此心，愆或有在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283800_comment'></div>誊天子诏，焚诸九原，幽冥共相，溥博渊源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283800_comment'></div>我皇祖、皇祖妣、皇考、皇妣必不为此一饭之安也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1283800_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　送诸生赴补，有序。作品：送诸生赴补序。<div id='poem_1283479' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283479' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283479?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送诸生赴补序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283479")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283479_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283479'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283479'>今年夏，进士既题名，于是成均阙弟子员，有司将群四方之大而择其可者，而从余游告余以行者四人耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283479_comment'></div>问其不行者，则曰：「度无道以得之，往将何济」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283479_comment'></div>问其行者，则曰：「心知其不可得，直未能免俗耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283479_comment'></div>余以为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283479_comment'></div>古之君子，尽其在我者，以听其在命者，得失非吾事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283479_comment'></div>然既已应之矣，而谓无心于得，亦岂情也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283479_comment'></div>居者勉吾学，而非以畏失也，失亦何害，而吾则未至也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283479_comment'></div>行者竭吾力，而非以志得也，得之固佳，而吾不敢必也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283479_comment'></div>如是而居，如是而行，吾无憾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283479_comment'></div>皆曰：「不敢不勉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283479_comment'></div>已而行者曰：「行非居比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283479_comment'></div>行都英俊之薮，无非可学事者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283479_comment'></div>有如不得其门，则终日枵然，谁实食之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283479_comment'></div>其何以自视于居者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283479_comment'></div>余曰：「四方之英，余不得而究识也，有为临安校官石夫子者，吾友也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283479_comment'></div>子往拜之，虚往实归，吾待子于此矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283479_comment'></div>谓卢子曰：「子以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283479", 1283479, "Clauses/51/Comments/2")'>通爽</span>往」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283479_comment'></div>谓陈子曰：「子以惇谨往」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283479_comment'></div>谓何子曰：「子以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1283479", 1283479, "Clauses/55/Comments/1")'>开警</span>往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283479_comment'></div>此子之资而非学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283479_comment'></div>求学于夫子而不子告者，他日吾将问之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283479_comment'></div>小何子徐而进曰：「准独遗矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283479_comment'></div>余笑曰：「彼苟不遗夫二三子者，子则何忧！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283479_comment'></div>并以吾之所常言者而问其当否焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283479_comment'></div>彼如『唯唯』，则告之曰：『先生谓我：不得一言则勿已』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283479_comment'></div>五月之朔，书于妥斋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1283479_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　众祭孔子、颜子、孟子，作文。作品：告先圣文。告先师文。告邹国公文。<div id='poem_1283793' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283793' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283793?labeling=true' target='_blank'>告先圣文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283793")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283793_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283793'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283793'>天下之理具于《易》，治道之本末著之《洪范》，而《诗》之喜怒哀乐，盖学者所以用功于平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283793_comment'></div>举而措之之大端，而当时之学者载而为《论语》，后世之群儒终日讲论而不到其地，则未免于争者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283793_comment'></div>帝王继世之用，《书》载之明矣，而三王之损益，夏商文献之不足，而周道独详焉，夫子之所深叹，而《春秋》所以备四王之制，百世以俟圣人而不惑者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283793_comment'></div>人才短长高下之不齐，而学力浅深中否之或异，岂能出规矩准绳之外哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283793_comment'></div>秦、汉以来，世有所谓英雄豪杰者，自矜其智力于夫子之外，亦可叹也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283793_comment'></div>亮等于夫子之书，各知用其力而不能齐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283793_comment'></div>今天子各命以官，使得以夫子之书从事，浅深中否非他人所能与，俯而拜，仰而祝，敢有不尽其志以负天子之显休命者，夫子实鉴临之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1283793_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283794?labeling=true' target='_blank'>告先师文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283794")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283794_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283794'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283794'>陋巷箪瓢，有何可乐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283794_comment'></div>而吾先师实乐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283794_comment'></div>近世诸儒求其乐而不可得，而曾点之浴沂遂得因吾夫子以自进于此焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283794_comment'></div>四代之礼乐亦可端坐以待时命之行也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283794_comment'></div>亮等皆知有疑于此矣，然而何以异于漆雕开也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283794_comment'></div>服天子之命服以拜吾先师，而求其所以自进于此者，庶几可以无负，惟吾先师实启之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1283794_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1283795' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283795' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283795?labeling=true' target='_blank'>告邹国公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283795")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283795_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283795'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283795'>用力于四端之微，举而措之喜怒哀乐之大，较其极，至于与造化同功，而天下之治乱无不在其掌握者，此邹公所以自达于天子者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283795_comment'></div>事半古之人而功则倍之者，岂当时百家众说之所能知哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283795_comment'></div>亮等以随时科举之文，而窃国家之一命，冀得稍自见于斯世，非乞灵于邹公则平生之志荒矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1283795_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年9月</a>　九月，寿朱元晦。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年9月1日</a>　九月一日，作《祝英台近》词寿俞德载。（嫩寒天）<span class='inlineComment2'>（该词作年难考，据词义疑在绍熙四年（1193），附于此。）</span><div id='poem_157245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157245?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祝英台近 九月一日寿俞德载</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年9月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157245")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157245_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157245'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157245'>嫩寒天，金气雨，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_157245", 157245, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>搅断</span>一秋事。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157245'>仝样霏微，还作小晴意。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157245'>世间万宝都成，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_157245", 157245, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>些儿</span>无欠，只待与、黄花为地。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157245_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157245'>好招致。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157245'>对此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_157245", 157245, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>郁郁葱葱</span>，新篘未成醉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157245'>翻手为云，造物等儿戏。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157245'>也知富贵来时，一班呈露，便做出、人中祥瑞。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_157245_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年9月7日</a>　九月七日，作《垂钓丝》词自寿。（菊花细雨）<span class='inlineComment2'>（该词作年难考，就词中气象，岂绍熙四年（1193||）得第后作，附于此。）</span><div id='poem_157225' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157225' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157225?labeling=true' target='_blank'>垂丝钓 九月七日自寿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年9月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157225")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157225_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157225'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157225'>菊花细雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157225'>萧萧红蓼汀渚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157225'>景物渐幽，风致如许。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157225'>秋未暮。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157225'>又值吾初度。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157225'>看天宇。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157225'>正澄清欲往。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157225_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157225'>登高未也，红尘当面飞舞。<div id='poem_sentence_7_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_157225'>几人吊古。<div id='poem_sentence_8_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_157225'>乌帽牢收取。<div id='poem_sentence_9_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_157225'>短发还羞觑。<div id='poem_sentence_10_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_157225'>遐寿身。<div id='poem_sentence_11_157225_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_157225'>近五云深处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_157225_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年10月</a>　十月，作刘和卿墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>刘和卿墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283699")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283699'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283699'>金华刘范，十年前名渊，尝与二三子从予学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283699_comment'></div>居亡何，其母死，葬邑之庆云乡杉塘原，求予铭其墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283699_comment'></div>其后予久不见范，范能入太学为诸生，与一时英俊相先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283699_comment'></div>一日，其父和卿名大声访予宝婺观，为予道范近事，喜甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283699_comment'></div>今年夏秋之交，予得第东归，趋本郡谢，则闻君死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283699_comment'></div>入吊君丧，甚悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283699_comment'></div>未几，范衰绖跣行，以其同舍生袁州州学教授徐君正夫所述君行来告曰：「我父将以十月己酉合葬，往尝辱铭吾母矣，可不哀吾父乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283699_comment'></div>予自念投老蒙上误恩，擢先众俊，精神筋力往往尽矣，愧无以报称也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283699_comment'></div>将遗落世事，痛自啬养，以庶几万一焉，而敢费心思于文字间以重其羞！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283699_comment'></div>然闻范言，则拒之有所不忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283699_comment'></div>盖世有常言：「争名于朝，争利于市」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283699_comment'></div>金华距行都一水，水湍流时，舟昨发今日至，行都无试则已尔，有则金华之士必多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283699_comment'></div>君尝学为其文，而众中未尝有君之迹，孝友自将，祈无愧于乡党而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283699_comment'></div>君世居都城，乃傍城筑室瞰溪，而南山森列，一望甚远，纵横不过二三丈许，外未免于利名交关，而过数步则幽人逸士之居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283699_comment'></div>然君与人无甚交涉怨恶，亦以是取足而无他营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283699_comment'></div>晚始作大室天宁寺傍，亦取其不涉闹市耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283699_comment'></div>君气貌伟然，宜于世无所不可，而利名之场，宜至死不休也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283699_comment'></div>去朝密迩而不往争名，出入于市而不就争利，则其可书者众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283699_comment'></div>君卒于绍熙四年六月壬寅，得年五十有七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283699_comment'></div>曾大父赐，大父肇，父从政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283699_comment'></div>先娶陈氏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283699_comment'></div>继季氏，赠朝议大夫迤之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283699_comment'></div>子男三人：长箕，次范也，少简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283699_comment'></div>女三人，适杨颋、李召甫、夏焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283699_comment'></div>孙男四人，女一人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283699_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1283699'>人生何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283699_comment'></div>为其有欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283699_comment'></div>欲也必争，惟日不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283699_comment'></div>粗足而休，惟君也独。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283699_comment'></div>抱此入土，吉不必卜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1283699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　冬，为义乌黄子野妻楼氏撰墓志铭。作品：黄夫人楼氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283716' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283716' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283716?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄夫人楼氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283716")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283716_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283716'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283716'>义乌黄耕子野，以壬辰岁入太学，与其同舍一时豪俊角铢积寸累之功以登舍选，于余为同年进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283716_comment'></div>其入太学之四年，始娶同邑楼君若虚之女为妇，年才二十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283716_comment'></div>而子野孀亲在堂，不以违离自戚，亟欲为其亲一日之荣，时节不敢离学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283716_comment'></div>故楼夫人见子野之日常少，子野亦觊得一官以终配俪之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283716_comment'></div>有男一人，名初孙，而楼夫人以己酉十二月十五日死矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283716_comment'></div>绍熙四年夏，子野与余同试殿廷下，登甲第，每为余诵言其不满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283716_comment'></div>至十二月二十八日辛酉，葬楼夫人于邑之龙祈乡菱塘先茔之侧，求余书圹石以志其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283716_comment'></div>余，龙川陈亮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283716_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1283716'>三纲所在，人之至情。<div
