class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283716_comment'></div>事或夺之，本心自明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283716_comment'></div>是皦皦者，宁间死生！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283716_comment'></div>子野具石，余为其铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1283716_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　及第后，感妻叔何茂恭知遇，又为文祭之。作品：祭妻叔文。<div id='poem_1283725' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283725' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283725?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭妻叔文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283725")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283725_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283725'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283725'>昔公有意圣贤之学，而不为世俗之文，山立玉峙，地负海涵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283725_comment'></div>少年四举手取科目，曾不得小自试于时，而竟赍志以殁，识者无不为公惜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283725_comment'></div>而公之既第，尝以其兄之女归之同年矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283725_comment'></div>其次固不应属之寒士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283725_comment'></div>公得官于大江之西，将行，力谓其兄：「必以次女归亮，吾保其可依也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283725_comment'></div>兄犹疑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283725_comment'></div>一行二千里，有便必寄书，书必以亮为言：「吾惧失此士」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283725_comment'></div>兄亦奋然曰：「宁使吾女不自振，无宁异日不可以见吾弟」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283725_comment'></div>故次女卒归亮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283725_comment'></div>当是时，虽亮亦笑公与之非其人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283725_comment'></div>及冒荐于乡，公喜特甚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283725_comment'></div>翼折而归，则以为事终在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283725_comment'></div>其后公兄弟相继下世，亮亦坎𡒄穷困，至为囚于棘寺而未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283725_comment'></div>岁时或一归，则羞拜公之墓，自省累公知人之明也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283725_comment'></div>今年之夏，竟以累举见录于春官，使得奉大廷之对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283725_comment'></div>天子躐取于众中，许以渊源而寘之选首，众欢曰宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283725_comment'></div>岂敢徒以冠裳与公之侄女拜公之墓，而明公之知人哉，使其不遭，公之知人固在也，但可以开公兄弟之一笑于九原之上耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283725_comment'></div>酌酒酹公，英灵不昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283725_comment'></div>报公未也，其或有待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283725_comment'></div>公明则远，我心未艾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283725_comment'></div>尚其懋哉，众不可盖！</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1283725_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　祭周贤庐文。<div id='poem_1283740' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283740' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283740?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭周贤董文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283740")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283740_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283740'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283740'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283740_comment'></div>尊行亲戚，今垂尽也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283740_comment'></div>惟吾舅与君，屹然为一坐之镇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283740_comment'></div>方姨母在时，一再岁必一觐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283740_comment'></div>间者阔焉，而君惠顾不靳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283740_comment'></div>连岁有江上之役，欲为公寿而不果奔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283740_comment'></div>谓公之寿方兴未艾，而此心终未泯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283740_comment'></div>曾与吾担未及弛，而死生不能以一瞬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283740_comment'></div>思吾先人，不可得见，而行辈亦复不振也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283740_comment'></div>若余之所遭如此，而安得不为世所摈也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283740_comment'></div>天乎人乎，自今皆可勿问也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283740_comment'></div>寿大较不满六十，而余少君九岁亦凛凛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283740_comment'></div>岂生既有阙于君，而死乃为此恳恳也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283740_comment'></div>亦伤夫事变之亟，而可以自见者无使有遗恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283740_comment'></div>英灵如在，其亦举吾觞而满引也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1283740_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　撰何少嘉墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283698' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283698' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283698?labeling=true' target='_blank'>何少嘉墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283698")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283698_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283698'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283698'>少嘉，何氏，名大猷，少嘉其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283698_comment'></div>世为义乌著姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283698_comment'></div>初，少嘉之曾祖先既死，祖矩以武事强力起家以光其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283698_comment'></div>父恢茂宏，叔父恪茂恭，以文字自奋场屋，有声诸公间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283698_comment'></div>茂恭登庚辰进士第，未及为时用而死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283698_comment'></div>茂宏不上第亦死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283698_comment'></div>少嘉时年二十许岁，辅伯兄大辩以当家，而家事悉禀命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283698_comment'></div>仲兄大雅以疾不涉事，少嘉时其起居，使得徜佯以自养疾，门外之事，不问剧易，身悉自当之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283698_comment'></div>少嘉兄弟欲葬其父于旁家之净明寺，葬有日矣，而寺僧梗不得葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283698_comment'></div>少嘉慨然曰：「我岂无一地以葬！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283698_comment'></div>是少我也，家不可立矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283698_comment'></div>官为杖之而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283698_comment'></div>又杖一恶少之无故为梗者，而后门户为之少宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283698_comment'></div>少嘉处宗族以顺，待朋友以信，接乡党以礼，协亲戚以恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283698_comment'></div>教诏童仆，而随力使之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283698_comment'></div>视租户如家人，而恤其轻重有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283698_comment'></div>及其死也，无一人不为堕泪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283698_comment'></div>而快其死者，两僧及一恶少耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283698_comment'></div>内事则姑姊妹之既适人者，疾病而多方救疗之，缓急而奔走扶助之，公济其乏而私又不靳其所有；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283698_comment'></div>惟其无事则平处之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283698_comment'></div>或怨其不均，则曰：「兄弟姊妹，岂有两心乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283698_comment'></div>未适人者，坐起必曰：「嫁尔而不及父在时，是为死其父矣，尔伯兄必不然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283698_comment'></div>暇时，读书有常课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283698_comment'></div>暮夜欲慰暖其母，则卧榻之侧，几案之旁，道及闾阎碎事，姊妹笑语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283698_comment'></div>夜分母倦，始各散去，而母亦忘其为寡居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283698_comment'></div>倾心一世之贤者，见辄尊事之，虽未见知，而不怠愈虔，曰：「吾未知前辈所谓不传之学安在，而敢自弃乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283698_comment'></div>尝从余学，而其姊以为「吾弟何所求于子而汲汲若此，盍有以大慰其心」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283698_comment'></div>予笑谓其姊：「越鸡不能化鹄卵，惜吾之非鲁鸡也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283698_comment'></div>其姊曰：「我不解子书语，吾弟满意而去，则吾之愿也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283698_comment'></div>未几而当路欲以事见杀，少嘉自比于子弟，而营救不爱其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283698_comment'></div>浙江风涛之险，一日往复两涉之，几至覆舟，不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283698_comment'></div>绍熙改元，冬十有二月，狱事再急，月之六日，少嘉无疾而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283698_comment'></div>予为之惊呼曰：「我其不免于诏狱乎，少嘉死，是恶證也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283698_comment'></div>二年兴狱，而仅能以不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283698_comment'></div>其兄将以癸丑二月二十三日，葬其园之南山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283698_comment'></div>少嘉娶俞氏麟之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283698_comment'></div>麟一时名士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283698_comment'></div>得邑以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283698_comment'></div>少嘉年二十九岁，无子，爱其兄之少子已孙者，死以嗣其后，亦少嘉之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283698_comment'></div>于是龙川陈亮铭其墓，晋安吴竽为书之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283698_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_1283698'>兄之子，吾子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283698_comment'></div>百世之后，孰知其为彼为此也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283698_comment'></div>宅兆之卜，惟其安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283698_comment'></div>以吾身而为后日之计，则阴阳祸福之多端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283698_comment'></div>身无可择之行，而道有未尽之精微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283698_comment'></div>赍志地下，深藏而厚覆之，而鬼神莫之窥也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283698_comment'></div>化为堆土，溢为精英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283698_comment'></div>变动无时，其或尔克承。</div><div id='poem_sentence_47_1283698_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　祭俞德载知县文。<div id='poem_1283726' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283726' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283726?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭俞德载知县文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283726")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283726_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283726'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283726'>士患无才，铺张不易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283726_comment'></div>患无科名，掀腾可冀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283726_comment'></div>得之既艰，况也中弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283726_comment'></div>十常八九，不如意事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283726_comment'></div>我岂无友，嗟嗟德载！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283726_comment'></div>翼折方飞，舟弃半济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283726_comment'></div>未有如此，倏兴忽废，投老多感，恸且出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283726_comment'></div>德载之学，初期自遂；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283726_comment'></div>既见伟人，欲极其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283726_comment'></div>涉猎不休，经史百氏，开物成务，以发厥志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283726_comment'></div>德载之文，亹亹有制，徐务收敛，刔剔瑕翳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283726_comment'></div>谓古作者，谁不可继？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283726_comment'></div>如其不可，方脩愈锐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283726_comment'></div>至其为人，有胆有气，乐易无他，倜傥任意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283726_comment'></div>开口见心，视人如己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283726_comment'></div>人攻我短，如石投水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283726_comment'></div>及夫从政，吏奸不蔽，遇事洒落，宁尚苛细！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283726_comment'></div>诛强锄梗，若近严毅，约定保伍，一于岂弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283726_comment'></div>我生与君，岁月不异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283726_comment'></div>我不自菲，早识前辈，君时有急，弟昆之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283726_comment'></div>彼此才冠，冀为道地，由此往来，交情日契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283726_comment'></div>乡荐我先，而公先第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283726_comment'></div>年壮气盛，事方迢递，所可知者，期以勿替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283726_comment'></div>我困祸患，抬头不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283726_comment'></div>君于仕途，有功无罪，亦复摧折，晚方小试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283726_comment'></div>只手援我，累卵不坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283726_comment'></div>改秩作邑，岂必得计！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283726_comment'></div>我亦遭逢，唱首殿陛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283726_comment'></div>相看晚岁，云胡独逝！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283726_comment'></div>哭君无穷，传以一祭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1283726_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　撰俞德载墓志铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年2月</a>　作吕夫人夏氏墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283715?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吕夫人夏氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1194年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283715")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283715_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283715'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283715'>夫人夏氏，世居婺之永康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283715_comment'></div>曾大父恭，大父开，父琛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283715_comment'></div>年二十有七嫁同邑吕君师愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283715_comment'></div>吕君先娶夏氏，生一男一女而殁，盖夫人同族女兄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283715_comment'></div>夫人初归吕氏，家道未为甚裕，吕君不遗馀力，经理其家，至有田近数千亩，遂甲于永康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283715_comment'></div>夫人节啬于内，课女工甚悉，以辅成吕君之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283715_comment'></div>又赞吕君教其前母之子约，必使自见于士林，取其女若夫置屋傍，使能自昌其家，盖继为人母者之所难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283715_comment'></div>及夫人所生之子浩以赈济得官，夫人不为动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283715_comment'></div>及用是而获贡于漕台，乃始为之喜曰：「汝父本非私汝，直为今日尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283715_comment'></div>更能自力以明父之志，乃吾心也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283715_comment'></div>约为怨家所告，几陷不测，语连吕君，浩诣阙告哀，请以所得官赎父兄之罪，朝廷义而许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283715_comment'></div>里闾族党咸以浩年少不知事体，为人所戏弄；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283715_comment'></div>自丧失一官，浩亦惭见其母，母语之曰：「汝今日不怠，自力于学，已能明父之心矣，尚将何求」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283715_comment'></div>其后既许约居外以事生产，亦许浩自读书于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283715_comment'></div>独与少子源俱，曰：「汝历事未多，读书未广，自力家事以代父之劳，所得亦既多矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283715_comment'></div>妇人女子之不溺于爱，区处其子切于事情，而无违夫之志，若夫人者能几！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283715_comment'></div>而享年止于六十有四，以绍熙三年十二月二十七日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283715_comment'></div>五年二月二十七日，葬于赵侯祠南山之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283715_comment'></div>孙男五人：季鲁、季殊、季时、季怀、季恂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283715_comment'></div>女三人，尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283715_comment'></div>前事，约、浩、源扣予门而哭：「盍亦哀吾母而赐之铭，且吾父之志也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283715_comment'></div>余方叨被误恩，褒嘉之语，非所宜蒙，训诫之辞，不遑宁处，思所以休息暮年而报称天地之造者，惧未之逮，而敢言文乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283715_comment'></div>独欲使一世知予无所怨恶，而乡闾幽闺之微往往具知之，故勉从约、浩之请而系之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283715_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1283715'>妇贵于拙，拙不害成；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283715_comment'></div>母主于爱，爱惟其平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283715_comment'></div>彤管所书，幽闺曷称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283715_comment'></div>因所自见，庶几平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283715_comment'></div>在尔后之克绍，岂予言而后明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283715_comment'></div>一石易朽，遗志可凭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283715_comment'></div>深藏厚覆，莫之变更。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1283715_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1194&endYear=1194')">1194年</a>　授官，未至，病，一夕卒。葬家侧龙窟马铺山，叶适、辛弃疾等为文祭之。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州（临安）
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年</a>　客临安，受《中庸》、《大学》于周葵，道德性命之学渐开。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1163&endYear=1163')">1163年11月</a>　十一月，垂拱殿成，进赋颂德。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='069a24dc082c4b77825a50aa8f4f35bc_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年2月</a>　二月，婺州以解头荐，应试礼部，不中。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1169&endYear=1169')">1169年</a>　上策问。作品：策问。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参看童振福《陈亮年谱》第12页。）</span><div id='poem_1283522' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283522' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283522?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中兴论<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>中兴五论序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1169年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283522")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283522_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283522'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283522'>臣闻治国有大体，谋敌有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>大略</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283522_comment'></div>立大体而后纪纲正，定<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>大略</span>而后机变行，此不易之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283522_comment'></div>仰惟陛下以睿圣神武之资，充硕大光明之学，留神政事，励志恢复，罔敢自暇自逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283522_comment'></div>而大欲未遂，大业未济，意者大体之未立而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>大略</span>之未定欤！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283522_comment'></div>臣尝为陛下有忧于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283522_comment'></div>尝欲输肝胆，效情愫，上书于北阙之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283522_comment'></div>又念世俗道薄，献言之人动必有觊，心虽不然，迹或近似，相师成风，谁能不疑！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283522_comment'></div>既已疑矣，安能察其言而明其心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283522_comment'></div>此臣之所大惧而卒以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>自沮</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283522_comment'></div>今年春，随试礼部，侥倖一中，庶几俯伏殿陛，毕写区区之忠以彻天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283522_comment'></div>有司以为不肖，竟从黜落，不得进望清光以遂昔愿，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>索手</span>东归，杜门求志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283522_comment'></div>因以为功名之在人，犹在己也：怀愚负计，而不以裨上之万一，是忿世也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283522_comment'></div>有君如此而忠言之不进，是匿情也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283522_comment'></div>己无他心而防人之疑，是自信不笃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283522_comment'></div>故书其《中兴论》一千八百馀言，大体<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1283522", 1283522, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>大略</span>，于斯见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283522_comment'></div>并论开诚、执要、励臣、正体之道，合五篇，上干天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283522_comment'></div>惟陛下宽其万死，不以为草茅之言而留神财幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283522_comment'></div>是天下社稷之福也，于臣何有！</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1283522_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='29b9f0f70bb7474e90c795c39a073ab4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("29b9f0f70bb7474e90c795c39a073ab4");'><span id='29b9f0f70bb7474e90c795c39a073ab4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>，28岁</div><div id='29b9f0f70bb7474e90c795c39a073ab4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1170&endYear=1170')">1170年</a>　岁首，在太学，有《孟子提要》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='086a56d713b549018534884b446c9dc8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("086a56d713b549018534884b446c9dc8");'><span id='086a56d713b549018534884b446c9dc8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1178')">1177-1178年</a>，35-36岁</div><div id='086a56d713b549018534884b446c9dc8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　不满考试官，去太学。试南宫，何儋校其文而黜之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　吕祖谦有书安慰，陈亮复信。作品：与吕伯恭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　策问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1177&endYear=1177')">1177年</a>　弟子郎景明来学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　是岁，更名为同。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年1月19日</a>　正月十九日丁巳，诣阙上孝宗皇帝书。作品：上孝宗皇帝第一书。<div id='poem_1283386' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283386' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283386?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上孝宗皇帝第一书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年1月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283386")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283386_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283386'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283386'>臣窃惟：中国，天地之正气也，天命之所钟也，人心之所会也，衣冠礼乐之所萃也，百代帝王之所以相承也，岂天地之外夷狄邪气之所可奸哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283386_comment'></div>不幸而能奸之，至于挈中国衣冠礼乐而寓之偏方，虽天命人心犹有所系，然岂以是为可久安而无事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283386_comment'></div>使其君臣上下苟一朝之安而息心于一隅，凡其志虑之所经营，一切置中国于度外，如元气偏注一肢，其他肢体往往<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>萎枯</span>而不自觉矣，则其所谓一肢者，又何恃而能久存哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283386_comment'></div>天地之正气，郁遏于腥膻而久不得骋，必将有所发泄，而天命人心固非偏方之所可久系也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283386_comment'></div>东晋自元帝息心于一隅，而胡、羯、鲜卑、氐、羌迭起中国，中国无岁不寻干戈，而江左卒亦不得一日宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283386_comment'></div>然渊、勒遂无遗种，而悯、怀之痛犹有所诿以安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283386_comment'></div>晋之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>植根</span>，本无可言者，而江左诸臣若祖逖、周访、陶侃、庾翼之徒，皆有虎视河洛之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283386_comment'></div>而桓温之师西至灞上，东至枋头，又于其间修陵寝于洛阳，盖犹未尽置中国于度外也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283386_comment'></div>故刘裕竟能一平河洛，而后晋亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283386_comment'></div>百年之间，其事既已如此，而天地之正气，固将有所发泄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283386_comment'></div>元魏起而承之，孝文遂定都洛阳，以修中国之衣冠礼乐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283386_comment'></div>而江左衣冠礼乐之旧，非复天命人心之所系矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283386_comment'></div>是以一天下者，卒在西北而不在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>东南</span>，天人之际，岂不甚可畏哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283386_comment'></div>一日之苟安，数百年之大祸也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283386_comment'></div>恭惟我国家二百年太平之基，三代之所无也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283386_comment'></div>二圣北狩之痛，汉唐之所未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283386_comment'></div>堂堂中国，而蠢尔丑虏安坐而据之，以二帝三王之所都，而为五十年犬羊之渊薮，国家之耻不得雪，臣子之愤不得伸，天地之正气不得而发泄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283386_comment'></div>方南渡之初，君臣上下痛心疾首，誓不与虏俱生，卒能以奔败之馀而胜百战之虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283386_comment'></div>及秦桧倡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/69/Comments/0")'>邪议</span>以沮之，忠臣义士斥死南方，而天下之气惰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283386_comment'></div>三十年之馀，虽西北<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/73/Comments/0")'>流寓</span>皆抱孙长息于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/73/Comments/1")'>东南</span>，而君父之大雠，一切不复关念，自非逆亮送死淮南，亦不知兵戈之为何事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283386_comment'></div>况望其愤中国之腥膻，而相率北向以发一矢哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283386_comment'></div>丙午、丁未之变，距今尚以为远；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283386_comment'></div>而靖康皇帝之祸，盖陛下即位之前一年也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283386_comment'></div>独陛下奋不自顾，志在灭虏，而天下之人，安然如无事时，方口议腹非，以陛下为喜功名而不恤后患，虽陛下亦不能以崇高之势而独胜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283386_comment'></div>隐忍以至于今，又十有七年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283386_comment'></div>昔者春秋之时，君臣父子相戕杀之祸，举一世皆安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283386_comment'></div>而孔子独以为三纲既绝，则人道遂为禽兽夷狄，皇皇奔走，义不能以一朝安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283386_comment'></div>然卒于无所寓，而发其志于《春秋》之书，犹能以惧乱臣贼子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283386_comment'></div>今者举一世而忘君父之大雠，此岂人道之所可安乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283386_comment'></div>使学者知学孔子，当进陛下以有为，决不沮陛下以苟安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283386_comment'></div>南师之不出，于今几年矣，河洛腥膻，而天地之正气抑郁而不得泄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283386_comment'></div>岂以堂堂中国，而五十年之间无一豪杰之能自奋哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283386_comment'></div>其势必有时而发泄矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283386_comment'></div>苟国家不能起而承之，必将有承之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283386_comment'></div>不可恃衣冠礼乐之旧，祖宗积累之深，以为天命人心可以安坐而久系也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283386_comment'></div>「皇天无亲，惟德是辅；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283386_comment'></div>民心无常，惟惠之怀」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283386_comment'></div>自三代圣人皆知其为甚可畏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283386_comment'></div>春秋之末，齐、晋、秦、楚皆衰，诸侯往往困于陪臣而不自振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283386_comment'></div>当此之时，虽如鲁卫之邦，苟能举大义以正诸侯，则天下可以一指麾而定也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283386_comment'></div>孔子惓惓斯世，而卒莫能用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283386_comment'></div>吴越起于蛮夷之小邦，而举兵以临齐晋，如履无人之地，遂伯诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283386_comment'></div>黄池之会，孔子之所甚痛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283386_comment'></div>天地之气发泄于蛮夷之小邦，可以明中国之无人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283386_comment'></div>王通有言：「夷狄之德，黎民怀之，三才其舍诸」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283386_comment'></div>此今世儒者之所未讲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283386_comment'></div>今丑虏之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>植根</span>既久，不可以一举而遂灭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283386_comment'></div>国家之大势未张，不可以一朝而大举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283386_comment'></div>而人情皆便于通和者，劝陛下积财养兵以待时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283386_comment'></div>臣以为，通和者所以成上下之苟安，而为妄庸两售之地，宜其为人情之所甚便也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283386_comment'></div>自和好之成，十有馀年，凡今日之指画方略者，他日将用之以坐筹也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283386_comment'></div>今日之击毬射雕者，他日将用之以决胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283386_comment'></div>府库充满，无非财也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1283386_comment'></div>介胄鲜明，无非兵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1283386_comment'></div>使兵端一开，则其迹败矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1283386_comment'></div>何者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1283386_comment'></div>人才以用而见其能否，安坐而能者不足恃也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1283386_comment'></div>兵食以用而见其盈虚，安坐而盈者不足恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1283386_comment'></div>而朝廷方幸一旦之无事，庸愚龌龊之人，皆得以守格令，行文书，以奉陛下之使令，而陛下亦幸其易制而无他也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1283386_comment'></div>徒使度外之士，摈弃而不得骋，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_59_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/182/Comments/0")'>日月蹉跎</span>而老将至矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1283386_comment'></div>臣故曰：通和者所以成上下之苟安，而为妄庸两售之地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1283386_comment'></div>东晋百年之间，未尝与虏通和也，故其臣东西驰骋，而多可用之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1283386_comment'></div>今和好一不通，而朝野之论常如虏兵之在境，惟恐其不得和也，虽陛下亦不得而不和矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1283386_comment'></div>昔者虏人草居野处，往来无常，能使人不知所备，而兵无日不可出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1283386_comment'></div>今也城郭宫室，政教号令，一切不异于中国；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1283386_comment'></div>点兵聚粮，文移往返，动涉岁月；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1283386_comment'></div>一方有警，三边骚动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1283386_comment'></div>此岂能岁出师以扰我乎，是固不知势者之论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1283386_comment'></div>然使朝野常如虏兵之在境，乃国家之福，而英雄所用以争天下之机也，执事者胡为速和以惰其心乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1283386_comment'></div>晋楚之战于邲也，栾书以为楚自克庸以来，其君无日不讨国人而训之于民生之不易，祸至之无日，戒惧之不可以怠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1283386_comment'></div>在军，无日不讨军实而申儆之于胜之不可保，纣之百克而卒无后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1283386_comment'></div>晋楚之弭兵于宋也，子罕以为：「兵所以威不轨而昭文德也，圣人以兴，乱人以废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1283386_comment'></div>废兴存亡，昏明之术，皆兵之由也，而求去之，是以诬道蔽诸侯也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1283386_comment'></div>夫人心之不可惰，兵之不可废，故虽成康之太平，犹有所谓「四征不庭」、「张皇六师」者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1283386_comment'></div>此李沆之所以深不愿真宗皇帝之与虏和亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1283386_comment'></div>况南北角立之时，而废兵以惰人心，使之安于忘君父之大雠，而置中国于度外，徒以便妄庸之人，则执事者之失策亦甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1283386_comment'></div>陛下何不明大义而慨然与虏绝也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1283386_comment'></div>贬损乘舆，却御正殿，痛自克责，誓必复雠，以励群臣，以振天下之气，以动中原之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1283386_comment'></div>虽未出兵，而人心不敢惰矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1283386_comment'></div>东西驰骋，而人才出矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1283386_comment'></div>盈虚相补，而兵食见矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1283386_comment'></div>狂妄之辞不攻而自息，懦庸之夫不却而自退缩矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1283386_comment'></div>当有度外之士起而惟陛下之所欲用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1283386_comment'></div>是<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/258/Comments/0")'>云合响应</span>之势，而非可安坐而致也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1283386_comment'></div>臣请为陛下陈国家立国之本末，而开今日大有为之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1283386_comment'></div>论天下形势之消长，而决今日大有为之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1283386_comment'></div>伏惟陛下试幸听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1283386_comment'></div>唐自肃、代以后，上失其柄，而藩镇自相雄长，擅其土地人民，用其甲兵财赋，官爵惟其所命，而人才亦各尽心于其所事，卒以成君弱臣强、正统数易之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1283386_comment'></div>艺祖皇帝一兴，而四方次第平定，藩镇拱手以趋约束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1283386_comment'></div>使列郡各得自达于京师，以京官权知，三年一易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1283386_comment'></div>财归于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_90_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/279/Comments/0")'>漕司</span>，而兵各归于郡，朝廷以一纸下郡国，如臂之使指，无有留难，自管库微职，必命于朝廷，而天下之势一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1283386_comment'></div>故京师尝宿重兵以为固，而郡国亦各有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/288/Comments/0")'>禁军</span>，无非天子所以自守其地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1283386_comment'></div>兵皆天子之兵，财皆天子之财，官皆天子之官，民皆天子之民，纲纪总摄，法令明备，郡县不得以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/296/Comments/0")'>一事</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/296/Comments/1")'>自专</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1283386_comment'></div>士以尺度而取，官以资格而进，不求度外之奇才，不慕绝世之隽功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1283386_comment'></div>天子蚤夜忧勤于其上，以礼义廉耻婴士大夫之心，以仁义公恕厚斯民之生，举天下皆由于规矩准绳之中，而二百年太平之基从此而立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1283386_comment'></div>然夷狄遂得以猖狂恣睢，与中国抗衡，俨然为南北两朝，而头目手足混然无别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1283386_comment'></div>微澶渊一战，则中国之势浸微，根本虽厚而不可立矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1283386_comment'></div>故庆历增币之事，富弼以为朝廷之大耻，而终身不敢自论其劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1283386_comment'></div>盖夷狄征令，是主上之操也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1283386_comment'></div>天子供贡，是臣下之礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1283386_comment'></div>夷狄之所以卒胜中国者，其积有渐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1283386_comment'></div>立国之初，其势固必至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1283386_comment'></div>故我祖宗常严庙堂而尊大臣，宽郡县而重守令；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1283386_comment'></div>于文法之内未尝折困天下之富商巨室，于格律之外有以容奖天下之英伟奇杰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1283386_comment'></div>皆所以助立国之势，而为不虞之备也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1283386_comment'></div>庆历诸臣亦尝愤中国之势不振矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1283386_comment'></div>而其大要，则使群臣争进其说，更法易令，而庙堂轻矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1283386_comment'></div>严按察之权，邀功生事，而郡县又轻矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1283386_comment'></div>岂惟于立国之势无所助，又从而脧削之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1283386_comment'></div>虽微章得象、陈执中以排沮其事，亦安得而不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/341/Comments/0")'>自沮</span>哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1283386_comment'></div>独其破去旧例，以不次用人，而劝农桑，务宽大，为有合于因革之宜，而其大要已非矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1283386_comment'></div>此所以不能洗夷狄<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_111_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/348/Comments/0")'>平视</span>中国之耻，而卒发神宗皇帝之大愤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1283386_comment'></div>王安石以正法度之说，首合圣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1283386_comment'></div>而其实则欲籍天下之兵尽归于朝廷，别行教阅以为强也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1283386_comment'></div>括郡县之利尽入于朝廷，别行封桩以为富也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1283386_comment'></div>青苗之政，惟恐富民之不困也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1283386_comment'></div>均输之法，惟恐商贾之不折也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1283386_comment'></div>罪无大小，动辄兴狱，而士大夫缄口畏事矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1283386_comment'></div>西北两边，至使内臣经画，而豪杰耻于为役矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1283386_comment'></div>徒使神宗皇帝见兵财之数既多，锐然南征北伐，卒乖圣意，而天下之势实未尝振也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1283386_comment'></div>彼盖不知朝廷立国之势，正患文为之太密，事权之太分，郡县太轻于下而委琐不足恃，兵财太关于上而重迟不易举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1283386_comment'></div>祖宗惟用前四者以助其势，而安石竭之不遗馀力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1283386_comment'></div>不知立国之本末者，真不足以谋国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1283386_comment'></div>元祐、绍圣，一反一覆，而卒为夷狄侵侮之资，尚何望其振中国以威夷狄哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1283386_comment'></div>南渡以来，大抵遵祖宗之旧，虽微有因革增损，不足为轻重有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1283386_comment'></div>如赵鼎诸臣，固已不究变通之理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1283386_comment'></div>而况秦桧尽取而沮毁之，忍耻事雠，饰太平于一隅以为欺，其罪可胜诛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1283386_comment'></div>陛下愤王业之屈于一隅，励志复雠，而不免籍天下之兵以为强，括郡县之利以为富；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1283386_comment'></div>加惠百姓，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_128_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/398/Comments/0")'>富人</span>无五年之积；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1283386_comment'></div>不重征税，而大商无巨万之藏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1283386_comment'></div>国势日以困竭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1283386_comment'></div>臣恐尺籍之兵，府库之财，不足以支一旦之用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1283386_comment'></div>陛下早朝宴罢，以冀中兴日月之功，而以绳墨取人，以文法莅事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1283386_comment'></div>圣断裁制中外，而大臣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_133_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/410/Comments/0")'>充位</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1283386_comment'></div>胥吏坐行条令，而百司逃责；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1283386_comment'></div>人才日以阘茸，臣恐程文之士，资格之官，不足以当度外之用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1283386_comment'></div>艺祖皇帝经画天下之大略，太宗皇帝已不能尽用，臣不敢尽具之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_136_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/419/Comments/0")'>纸墨</span>，今其遗意岂无望于陛下也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1283386_comment'></div>陛下苟推原其意而行之，可以开社稷数百年之基，而况于复故物乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1283386_comment'></div>不然，维持之具既穷，臣恐祖宗之积累亦不足恃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1283386_comment'></div>陛下试幸令臣毕陈于前，则今日大有为之略必知所处矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1283386_comment'></div>夫吴、蜀天地之偏气也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1283386_comment'></div>钱塘又吴之一隅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1283386_comment'></div>当唐之衰，而钱镠以闾巷之雄起王其地，自以不能独立，常朝事中国以为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1283386_comment'></div>及我宋受命，俶以其家入京师而自献其土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1283386_comment'></div>故钱塘终始五代被兵最少，而二百年之间，人物日以繁盛，遂甲于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_144_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/440/Comments/0")'>东南</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1283386_comment'></div>及建炎、绍兴之间，为六飞所驻之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1283386_comment'></div>当时论者固已疑其不足以张形势而事恢复矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1283386_comment'></div>秦桧又从而备百司庶府以讲礼乐于其中，其风俗固已华靡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1283386_comment'></div>士大夫又从而治园囿台榭以乐其生于干戈之馀，上下宴安，而钱塘为乐国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1283386_comment'></div>一隙之地本不足以容万乘，而镇压且五十年，山川之气盖亦发泄而无馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1283386_comment'></div>故谷粟桑麻丝枲之利岁耗于一岁，禽兽鱼鳖草木之生日微于一日，而上下不以为异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1283386_comment'></div>公卿将相大抵多江、浙、闽、蜀之人，而人才亦日以凡下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1283386_comment'></div>场屋之士以十万数，而文墨小异已足以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_152_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/458/Comments/0")'>称雄</span>于其间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1283386_comment'></div>陛下据钱塘已耗之气，用闽、浙日衰之士，而欲鼓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_153_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/461/Comments/0")'>东南</span>习安脆弱之众北向以争中原，臣是以知其难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1283386_comment'></div>荆襄之地，在春秋时，楚用以虎视齐、晋，而齐晋不能屈也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1283386_comment'></div>及战国之际，独能与秦争帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1283386_comment'></div>其后三百馀年，而光武起于南阳，同时共事，往往多南阳故人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1283386_comment'></div>又二百馀年，遂为三国交据之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1283386_comment'></div>诸葛亮由此起辅先主，荆楚之士从之如云，而汉氏赖以复存于蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1283386_comment'></div>周瑜、鲁肃、吕蒙、陆逊、陆抗、邓艾、羊祜，皆以其地显名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1283386_comment'></div>又百馀年，而晋氏南渡，荆雍常雄于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_160_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/482/Comments/0")'>东南</span>，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_160_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/483/Comments/0")'>东南</span>往往倚以为强，梁竟以此代齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1283386_comment'></div>及其气发泄无馀，而隋唐以来遂为偏方下州；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1283386_comment'></div>五代之际，高氏独常臣事诸国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1283386_comment'></div>本朝二百年之间，降为荒落之邦，北连许汝，民居稀少，土产庳薄，人才之能通姓名于上国者，如晨星之相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1283386_comment'></div>况至于建炎、绍兴之际，群盗出没于其间，而被祸尤极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1283386_comment'></div>以迄于今，虽南北分画交据，往往又置于不足用，民食无所从出，而兵不可由此而进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1283386_comment'></div>议者或以为忧，而不知其势之足用也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1283386_comment'></div>其地虽要为偏方，然未有偏方之气五六百年而不发泄者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1283386_comment'></div>况其东通吴会，西连巴蜀，南极湖湘，北控关洛，左右伸缩，皆足为进取之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1283386_comment'></div>今诚能开垦其地，洗濯其人，以发泄其气而用之，使足以接关洛之气，则可以争衡于中国矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1283386_comment'></div>是亦形势消长之常数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1283386_comment'></div>陛下慨然移都建业，百司庶府，皆从草创，军国之仪，皆从简略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1283386_comment'></div>又作行宫于武昌，以示不敢宁居之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1283386_comment'></div>常以江淮之师为虏人侵轶之备，而精择一人之沈鸷有谋、开豁无他者，委以荆襄之任，宽其文法，听其废置，抚摩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_173_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/532/Comments/0")'>振厉</span>于三数年之间，则国家之势成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1283386_comment'></div>至于相时弛张以就形势者，有非书之所能尽载也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1283386_comment'></div>石晋失卢龙一道，以成开运之祸，盖丙午、丁未岁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1283386_comment'></div>明年，艺祖皇帝始从郭太祖征伐，卒以平定天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1283386_comment'></div>其后契丹以甲辰败于澶渊，而丁未、戊申之间，真宗皇帝东封西祀以告太平，盖本朝极盛之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1283386_comment'></div>又六十年而神宗皇帝实以丁未岁即位，国家之事于是一变矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1283386_comment'></div>又六十年而丙午、丁未，遂为靖康之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1283386_comment'></div>天独启陛下于是年，而又启陛下以北向复雠之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1283386_comment'></div>今者去丙午、丁未，近在十年间尔，天道六十年一变，陛下可不有以应其变乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1283386_comment'></div>此诚今日大有为之机，不可苟安以玩岁月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1283386_comment'></div>臣不佞，自少有驱驰四方之志，常欲求天下豪杰之士而与之论今日之大计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1283386_comment'></div>盖尝数至行都，而人物如林，其论皆不足以起人意，臣是以知陛下大有为之志孤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1283386_comment'></div>辛卯、壬辰之间，始退而穷天地造化之初，考古今沿革之变，以推极皇帝王伯之道，而得汉、魏、晋、唐长短之由，天人之际，昭昭然可察而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1283386_comment'></div>始悟今世之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_186_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/572/Comments/0")'>儒士</span>自以为得正心诚意之学者，皆风痹不知痛痒之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1283386_comment'></div>举一世安于君父之雠，而方低头拱手以谈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_187_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/575/Comments/0")'>性命</span>，不知何者谓之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_187_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/576/Comments/0")'>性命</span>乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1283386_comment'></div>陛下接之而不任以事，臣于是服陛下之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1283386_comment'></div>又悟今世之才臣自以为得富国强兵之术者，皆狂惑以肆叫呼之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1283386_comment'></div>不以暇时讲究立国之本末，而方扬眉伸气以论富强，不知何者谓之富强乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1283386_comment'></div>陛下察之而不敢尽用，臣于是服陛下之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1283386_comment'></div>陛下厉志复雠，足以对天命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1283386_comment'></div>笃于仁爱，足以结民心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1283386_comment'></div>而又仁明足以临照群臣一偏之论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1283386_comment'></div>此百代之英主也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1283386_comment'></div>今乃驱委庸人，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_196_1283386", 1283386, "Clauses/593/Comments/0")'>笼络</span>小儒，以迁延大有为之岁月，臣不胜愤悱，是以忘其贱而献其愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1283386_comment'></div>陛下诚令臣毕陈于前，岂惟臣区区之愿，将天地之神，祖宗之灵，实与闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1283386_comment'></div>干冒天威，罪当万死。</div><div id='poem_sentence_198_1283386_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　孝宗震动，欲榜朝堂，将擢用之。曾觌将见，亮耻之，逾垣而逃，觌不悦。大臣恶其无讳，交沮之。由是八日待命，未有闻焉。因再诣阙上书。作品：上孝宗第二书。<div id='poem_1283387' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283387' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283387?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上孝宗皇帝第二书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283387")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283387_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283387'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283387'>臣尝叹西周之末，犬戎之祸，盖天地之大变，国家之深耻，臣子之至痛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283387_comment'></div>平王东迁以来，使其痛内切于心，必将因臣子之愤，藉晋郑之势，以告哀于天下之诸侯，以大义责其兴师以奖王室，其不至者，天下共诛之，则可以扫荡犬戎，洗国家之耻而舒臣子之愤矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283387_comment'></div>然后正纪纲，修法度，亲鲁卫以和柔中国，命齐晋为方伯，以纠合天下之诸侯，文武之迹可寻，东周之业可兴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283387_comment'></div>今乃即安于洛邑，虽周民赖以粗安，宗祀赖以不绝，然使其臣子忘君父之大雠，而置天下之诸侯于度外，周之名号虽存，而其实则眇然一列国耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283387_comment'></div>当平王在位之时，世之君子尚意其犹有待也，及待之四十九年，而士君子之望亦衰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283387_comment'></div>天子之命令不足以制诸侯，则其互相吞灭，盖其势之所必至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283387_comment'></div>天下不明于复雠之义，则其君臣父子相贼杀，习以为常而不之怪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283387_comment'></div>孔子伤宗周之无主，痛人道之将绝，而作《春秋》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283387_comment'></div>其书天王之义严矣：书其出入之地者，示天王不可置中国于度外也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283387_comment'></div>书其有所求者，明天王之不可失其柄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283387_comment'></div>其书讨贼之义严矣：贼不讨不书葬者，明一国之无臣子也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283387_comment'></div>一人讨贼而以众书者，示夫人之皆可得而讨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283387_comment'></div>天子既不能以保天下之民，而一国各自有其民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283387_comment'></div>其君之有志于民而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283387", 1283387, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>闵雨</span>者必书，无志于民而不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1283387", 1283387, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>闵雨</span>者必书，土功必书，饥馑必书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283387_comment'></div>孔子之心，未尝不庶几天下之民一日之获瘳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283387_comment'></div>是君道之大端，而圣人望天下与来世者，可谓深切著明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283387_comment'></div>臣恭惟皇帝陛下厉志复雠，不肯即<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283387", 1283387, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>安于一隅</span>，是有大功于社稷也，而天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283387", 1283387, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>经生</span>学士讲先王之道者，反不足以明陛下之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283387_comment'></div>陛下笃意恤民，每遇水旱，忧见颜色，是有大德于天下也，而天下之才臣智士趋当世之务者，又不足以明陛下之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283387_comment'></div>论恢复则曰修德待时，论富强则曰节用爱人，论治则曰正心，论事则曰守法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283387_comment'></div>君以从谏务学为美，臣以识心见性为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283387_comment'></div>论安言计，动引圣人，举一世谓之正论，而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1283387", 1283387, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>经生</span>学士合为一辞，以摩切陛下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283387_comment'></div>夫岂知安一隅之地则不足以承天命，忘君父之雠则不足以立人道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283387_comment'></div>民穷兵疲而事不可已者，不可以常理论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283387_comment'></div>消息盈虚而与时偕行者，不可以常法拘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283387_comment'></div>为天下之正论而不足以明天下之大义，宜其取轻于陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283387_comment'></div>论恢复则曰精间谍，结豪望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283387_comment'></div>论富强则曰广招募，括隐漏：论治则曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1283387", 1283387, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>立志</span>，论事则曰从权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283387_comment'></div>君以驾驭笼络为明，臣以奋励驱驰为最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283387_comment'></div>察事见情，自许豪杰，举一世谓之奇论，而才臣智士合为一辞以撼动陛下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283387_comment'></div>夫岂知坐钱塘浮侈之隅以图中原，则非其地；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283387_comment'></div>用东南习安之众以行进取，则非其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283387_comment'></div>财止于府库，则不足以通天下之有无；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283387_comment'></div>兵止于尺籍，则不足以兼天下之勇智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283387_comment'></div>为天下之奇论而无取于办天下之大计，此所以取疑于陛下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283387_comment'></div>三光五岳之气分，而人才之高者止于如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283387_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1283387", 1283387, "Clauses/117/Comments/0")'>经生</span>学士既揆之以大义而取轻，才臣智士又权之以大计而取疑，陛下始不知所仗而有独运四海之意矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283387_comment'></div>故左右亲信之臣又得以窥意向而效<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_36_1283387", 1283387, "Clauses/120/Comments/0")'>忠款</span>，陛下喜其颐指如意，而士大夫亦喜其有言之易达也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283387_comment'></div>是以附会之风浸长，而陛下之大权移矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283387_comment'></div>寻常无过之人，安然坐庙堂而奉使令，陛下幸其易制无他，而天下之人亦幸其苟安而无事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283387_comment'></div>是以迁延之计遂行，而陛下大有为之志乖矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283387_comment'></div>陛下励志复雠，有大功于社稷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283387_comment'></div>笃意恤民，有大德于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283387_comment'></div>而卒不免笼络小儒，驱委庸人，以迁延大有为之岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283387_comment'></div>此臣之所以不胜忠愤，而斋沐裁书，择今者丁巳而献之阙下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283387_comment'></div>愿得望见颜色，陈国家立国之本末而开大有为之略，论天下形势之消长而决大有为之机，务合于艺祖皇帝经画天下之本旨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283387_comment'></div>然八日待命而未有闻焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283387_comment'></div>夫匹夫匹妇不获自尽，民主罔与成厥功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283387_comment'></div>使天下之言者越月踰时而后得报，在安平无事之时犹且不可；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283387_comment'></div>今者当陛下大有为之际，陈天下之大义，献天下之大计，而八日不得命焉，臣恐天下之豪杰得以测陛下之意向，而云合响应之势不得而成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283387_comment'></div>陛下积财养兵，志在灭虏，而不免与之通和以俟时，固已不足以动天下之心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283387_comment'></div>故既和而聚财，人反以为厉民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283387_comment'></div>既和而练兵，人反以为动众；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283387_comment'></div>举足造事，皆足以致人之疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1283387_comment'></div>议者惟其不明大义以示之，而后大计不可得而立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1283387_comment'></div>苟又无意于臣之言，则天下愈不知所向矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1283387_comment'></div>张浚始终任事，竟无一功可论；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1283387_comment'></div>而天下之童儿妇女不谋同辞，皆以为社稷之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1283387_comment'></div>彼其誓不与虏俱生，百败而不折者，诚有以合于天人之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1283387_comment'></div>秦桧专权二十馀年，东南赖以无事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1283387_comment'></div>而天下之童儿妇女不谋同辞，皆以为国之贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1283387_comment'></div>彼其忘君父之雠而置中国于度外者，其违天人之心亦甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1283387_comment'></div>陛下将以办天下之大计，而大义未足以震动天下，亦执事者之所当蚤正而预计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1283387_comment'></div>臣区区之心皆已具之前书，惟陛下财幸。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1283387_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　书既上，有都堂审察之命。宰相问所欲言，又不合。待命十日，再诣阙上书。作品：上孝宗皇帝第三书。<div id='poem_1283388' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283388' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283388?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上孝宗皇帝第三书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1178年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283388")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283388_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283388'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283388'>臣窃惟：艺祖皇帝经画天下之大略，盖将上承周、汉之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283388_comment'></div>太宗皇帝一切律之于规矩准绳之内，以立百五六十年太平之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283388_comment'></div>至于今日，而不思所以变而通之，则维持之具穷矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283388_comment'></div>举江、浙、闽、广之士，亡虑十四五万数，蜀不与焉，而龌龊拘挛，日甚于一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283388_comment'></div>选人之在铨者，殆以万计，而侥倖之源未有穷已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283388_comment'></div>财用之入倍于承平之时，而费于养兵者十之九，兵不足用，而民日以困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283388_comment'></div>非必道微俗薄而至此也，盖本朝维持之具，二百年之馀，其势固必至此，艺祖皇帝固已逆知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283388_comment'></div>使天下安平无事，犹将望陛下变而通之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283388_comment'></div>而况<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283388", 1283388, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>版舆</span>之地半入于夷狄，国家之耻未雪，臣子之痛未伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283388_comment'></div>天锡陛下以非常之智勇，而又启陛下以北向复雠之意，乃欲因今之势而有为焉，此所以十有七年之间，圣虑愈劳而取效愈远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283388_comment'></div>群臣既不足以望清光，而草茅贱士不胜忧国之心，私以为陛下春秋五十有二，经天下之事变为已多，阅天下之义理为已熟，举足造事，必不伤国家之大体，叩囊底之智，犹足以办此丑虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283388_comment'></div>六十以往，顾将望一日之安，而亦何忍遗患于后人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283388_comment'></div>臣以为拘挛龌龊之中，其势当有卓然自奋于草茅而开悟圣聪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283388_comment'></div>臣不自量其分之不足，而窃有志焉，是以具国家社稷之大计，质之天地鬼神而献之阙下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283388_comment'></div>陛下亦卓然拔之群言之中，特命大臣察其所欲言之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283388_comment'></div>臣妄意国家维持之具，至今日而穷，而艺祖皇帝经画天下之大指，犹可恃以长久，苟推原其意而变通之，则恢复不足为矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283388_comment'></div>然而变通之道有三：有可以迁延数十年之策，有可以为百五六十年之计，有可以复开数百年之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283388_comment'></div>事势昭然而效见殊绝，非陛下聪明度越百代，决不能一二以听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283388_comment'></div>臣不敢泄之大臣之前，而大臣拱手称旨以问，臣亦姑取其大体之可言者三事以答之，而草茅亦不自知其开口触讳也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283388_comment'></div>其一曰：二圣北狩之痛，盖国家之大耻，而天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1283388", 1283388, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>公愤</span>也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283388_comment'></div>五十年之馀，虽天下之气销铄颓惰，不复知雠耻之当念，正在主上与二三大臣振作其气以泄其愤，使人人如报私雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283388_comment'></div>此《春秋》书「卫人杀州吁」之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283388_comment'></div>若祇与一二臣为密，是以天下之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1283388", 1283388, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>公愤</span>而私自为计，恐不足以感动天人之心，恢复之事亦恐茫然未知攸济耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283388_comment'></div>其二曰：国家之规模，使天下奉规矩准绳以从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283388_comment'></div>群臣救过之不给，而何暇展布四体以求济度外之功哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283388_comment'></div>故其势必至于委靡而不振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283388_comment'></div>五代之际，兵财之柄倒持于下，艺祖皇帝束之于上以定祸乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283388_comment'></div>后世不原其意，束之不已，故郡县空虚而本末俱弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283388_comment'></div>今不变其势而求恢复，虽一旦得精兵数十万，得财数万万计，而恢复之期愈远，就使虏人尽举河南之地以还我，亦恐不能守耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283388_comment'></div>其三曰：艺祖皇帝用天下之士人以易武臣之任事者，而五代之乱不崇朝而定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283388_comment'></div>故本朝以儒立国，而儒道之振独优于前代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283388_comment'></div>今天下之士<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1283388", 1283388, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>烂熟</span>委靡，诚可厌恶，正在主上与二三大臣反其道以教之，作其气以养之，使临事不至乏才，随才皆足有用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283388_comment'></div>则立国之规模不至戾艺祖皇帝之本旨，而东西驰骋以定祸乱，不必专在武臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283388_comment'></div>前汉以军吏立国，而用儒辄败人事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283388_comment'></div>要之人各有家法，未易轻动，惟在变而通之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283388_comment'></div>天下大势之所趋，非人力之所能移也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283388_comment'></div>臣之所以为大臣论者，其大略如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283388_comment'></div>而所谓数十年之策，百五六十年之计，数百年之基，与夫恢复之形势，事大体重，苟未决之圣心，则不可泄之大臣之前也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283388_comment'></div>故止陈其大略之可言者三事以答之，二三大臣已相顾骇然，而臣亦皇恐而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283388_comment'></div>疏远草茅，宁复有路以望清光乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283388_comment'></div>马周，一时琐琐之才也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283388_comment'></div>太宗喜其为常何陈事，召使面对，未至之间，使者连数辈趣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283388_comment'></div>使有能为太宗开礼乐法度者，其召之当不容喘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283388_comment'></div>陛下聪明迈越太宗，而拔臣于群言混淆之中，孤立以行一意，卒不免泯没而止，其罪在臣之踪迹不明，有以误陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283388_comment'></div>臣本太学诸生，自忧制以来，退而读书者六七年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283388_comment'></div>虽蚤夜以求皇帝王伯之略，而科举之文不合于程度不止也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283388_comment'></div>去年一发其狂论于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1283388", 1283388, "Clauses/158/Comments/0")'>小试</span>之间，满学之士口语纷然，至腾谤以动朝路，数月而未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283388_comment'></div>而为之学官者，迄今进退未有据也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283388_comment'></div>臣自是始弃学校而决归耕之计矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283388_comment'></div>旋复自念：数年之间，所学云何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283388_comment'></div>而陛下之心，臣独又知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283388_comment'></div>苟徒恤一世之谤，而不为陛下一陈国家社稷之大计，将得罪于天地之神与艺祖皇帝在天之灵而不可解，是故昧于一来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283388_comment'></div>旧名已在学校之籍，于法不得以上书言事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1283388_comment'></div>使臣有一毫攫取爵禄之心，以臣所习科举之文更一二试，而考官又平心以考之，则亦随例得之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1283388_comment'></div>何忍假数百年社稷之大计，以为一日之侥倖，而徒以累陛下哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1283388_comment'></div>世固有却万钟之禄而不受者，亦有争一钱以至于相杀者，人情相去之远，何啻于十百千万也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1283388_comment'></div>而臣欲持空言以自明，亦浅矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1283388_comment'></div>然审察十日而不得自便之命，臣将无以自见于山林之士，徒以伤陛下招致天下豪杰之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1283388_comment'></div>臣今更待罪三日而后渡江，誓将终老田亩以弭群论，以报陛下拔臣言于众中之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1283388_comment'></div>故昧死拜书以辞于阙下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1283388_comment'></div>臣阖门数十口，去行都无四百里，当席稿私室，以听<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1283388", 1283388, "Clauses/199/Comments/0")'>雷霆之诛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1283388_comment'></div>干冒天威，罪当万死。</div><div id='poem_sentence_61_1283388_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='e7621a5fa4204095aa22625a28323f8f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e7621a5fa4204095aa22625a28323f8f");'><span id='e7621a5fa4204095aa22625a28323f8f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>，36岁</div><div id='e7621a5fa4204095aa22625a28323f8f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1178&endYear=1178')">1178年</a>　与辛弃疾有临安之聚。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c2aa7e40958744afacfbb2d4d7149a9f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c2aa7e40958744afacfbb2d4d7149a9f");'><span id='c2aa7e40958744afacfbb2d4d7149a9f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>，45岁</div><div id='c2aa7e40958744afacfbb2d4d7149a9f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年10月8日</a>　十月八日，入都。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　周必大为右丞相，以书贺周必大，并述晚景蹉跎，求一见。作品：与周丞相必大书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第65页。）</span><div id='poem_1283457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与周丞相<span class='inlineComment2'>（必大）</span>书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1187年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283457")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283457'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283457'>亮不获瞻望钧表，忽忽又复两载，崇仰之心，如水万折而必东也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283457_comment'></div>穷居野处，日与海内之人在陶冶之中，而独能知其所自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283457_comment'></div>今春以年免上礼部，本有进拜之便，临试一病狼狈，拖强魂入院，仅而不死，仓皇渡江，兄弟接之江头，携持抵家，更一月始能啖饭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283457_comment'></div>一庶弟竟染病以死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283457_comment'></div>更以妻孥番病，意绪惘惘，殆不知身世之足赖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283457_comment'></div>方困顿时，亦闻昭布大号，晋秉国钧，二十年海内所仰望而敬祝者，一旦遂满其愿，非独一夫欣幸而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283457_comment'></div>仰惟丞相以命世之才，得旷古之学，平生经纶老手，至是可以展布而无疑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283457_comment'></div>主上天日之表，本非苟安于无事者，皇天全畀之重，百年丘墟之责，则北向之志非可与好大喜功者同日而语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283457_comment'></div>丞相亦岂今日而忘念虑哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283457_comment'></div>亮忭甚至于起立，虽病未即安，喜慰无量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283457_comment'></div>亦尝撰为骈俪之语，欲遣一介驰献，因循至今，其意之皎然，尚赖丞相终察之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283457_comment'></div>今者又闻朝廷非复向来安静，庙堂当亦多事，何暇款读士子言语；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283457_comment'></div>念此意不可不达，故卒遣前，倘略赐钧览，不胜幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283457_comment'></div>亮蹉跎遂入晚景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283457_comment'></div>技成无用，重以多病，度非久于人世者，宜可一笔勾断；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283457_comment'></div>而耿耿者未易即灭，况在门墙之旧，岂便复缄口！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283457_comment'></div>又不敢缕缕为渎，虽叠楮之恭，亦以为丞相既厌之而不复出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283457_comment'></div>亮至节后，以小故一到浙西，取道行都，首当俯伏钧屏，以究其平生欲言而未敢者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283457_comment'></div>冒昧渎尊之罪，钧慈必有以照容之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283457_comment'></div>亮下情惶惧之至！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1283457_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ac0a5336893e43c9bf575810a83e6c24_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ac0a5336893e43c9bf575810a83e6c24");'><span id='ac0a5336893e43c9bf575810a83e6c24_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>，46岁</div><div id='ac0a5336893e43c9bf575810a83e6c24' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年4月</a>　夏四月丙戌，上孝宗皇帝书。孝宗将内禅，不报。在廷交怒，以为狂怪。留临安二十余日，始归。作品：戊申再上孝宗皇帝书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第65页。）</span><div id='poem_1283389' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283389' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283389?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戊申再上孝宗皇帝书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1188年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283389")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283389_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283389'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283389'>臣闻有非常之人，然后可以建非常之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283389_comment'></div>求非常之功而用常才、出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/2/Comments/2")'>常计</span>、举常事以应之者，不待智者而后知其不济也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283389_comment'></div>前史有言：「非常之原，黎民惧焉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283389_comment'></div>古之英豪岂乐于惊世骇俗哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283389_comment'></div>盖不有以新天下之耳目，易斯民之志虑，则吾之所求亦泛泛焉而已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283389_comment'></div>皇天全付予有家，而半没于夷狄，此君天下者之所当耻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283389_comment'></div>《春秋》许九世复雠，而再世则不问，此为人后嗣者之所当愤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283389_comment'></div>中国，圣贤之所建置，而悉沦于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>左衽</span>，此英雄豪杰之所当同以为病也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283389_comment'></div>秦桧以和误国二十馀年，而天下之气索然而无馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283389_comment'></div>陛下慨然有削平宇内之志，又二十馀年而天下之士始知所向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283389_comment'></div>其有功德于宗庙社稷者，非臣区区之所能诵说其万一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283389_comment'></div>高宗皇帝春秋既高，陛下不欲大举以惊动慈颜，抑心俯首以致色养，圣孝之盛，书册之所未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283389_comment'></div>今者高宗皇帝既已祔庙，天下之英雄豪杰皆仰首以观陛下之举动，陛下其忍使二十年间所以作天下之气者，一旦而复索然乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283389_comment'></div>天下不可以坐取也，兵不可以常胜也，驱驰运动又非年高德尊者之所宜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283389_comment'></div>东宫居曰监国，行曰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>抚军</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283389_comment'></div>陛下近者以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>宅忧</span>之故，特命东宫以监国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283389_comment'></div>天下之论，皆以为事有是非可否，而父子之际至难言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283389_comment'></div>东宫聪明睿知，而四十之年不必试以事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283389_comment'></div>故东宫不敢安而陛下亦知其难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283389_comment'></div>陛下何不于此时命东宫为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>抚军</span>大将军，岁巡建业，使之兼统诸司，尽护诸将，置长史司马以专其劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283389_comment'></div>而陛下于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>宅忧</span>之馀，运用人才，均调天下，以应无穷之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283389_comment'></div>此肃宗所以命广平王之故事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283389_comment'></div>兵虽未出，而圣意振动，天下之英雄豪杰靡然知所向矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283389_comment'></div>天下知所向，则吾之驰驱运动亦有所凭藉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283389_comment'></div>臣请为陛下论天下之形势，而后知江南之不必忧，和议之不必守，虏人之不足畏，而书生之论不足凭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283389_comment'></div>臣闻吴会者，晋人以为不可都，而钱镠据之以抗四邻，盖自毗陵而外不能有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283389_comment'></div>其地南有浙江，西有崇山峻岭，东北则有重湖沮洳，而松江、震泽横亘其前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283389_comment'></div>虽有戎马百万，何所用之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283389_comment'></div>此钱镠所恃以为安，而国家六十年都之而无外忧者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283389_comment'></div>独海道可以径达吴会；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283389_comment'></div>而海道之险，吴儿习舟楫者之所畏，虏人能以轻师而径至乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283389_comment'></div>破人家国而止可用其轻师乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283389_comment'></div>书生以为江南不易保者，是真儿女子之论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283389_comment'></div>臣尝疑书册不足凭，故尝一到京口、建业，登高四望，深识天地设险之意，而古今之论为未尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283389_comment'></div>京口连冈三面，而大江横陈，江傍极目千里，其势大略如虎之出穴，而非若穴之藏虎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283389_comment'></div>昔人以为京口酒可饮，兵可用，而北府之兵为天下雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283389_comment'></div>盖其地势当然，而人善用之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283389_comment'></div>臣虽不到采石，其地与京口股肱建业，必有据险临前之势，而非止于靳靳自守者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283389_comment'></div>天岂使南方自限于一江之表，而不使与中国通而为一哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283389_comment'></div>江傍极目千里，固将使谋夫勇士得以展布四体，以与中国争衡者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283389_comment'></div>韩世忠顿兵八万于山阳，如老罴之当道，而淮东赖以安寝，此守淮东之要法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283389_comment'></div>天下有变，则长驱而用之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283389_comment'></div>若一一欲堑而守之，分兵而据之，出奇设险，如兔之护窟，势分力弱，反以成戎马长驱之势耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283389_comment'></div>是以二十年间，纷纷献策以劳圣虑，而卒无一成，虽成亦不足恃者，不知所以用淮东之势者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283389_comment'></div>而书生便以为长淮不易守者，是亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/130/Comments/0")'>问道于盲</span>之类耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283389_comment'></div>自晋之永嘉，以迄于隋之开皇，其在南则定建业为都，更六姓，而天下分裂者三百馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283389_comment'></div>南师之谋北者不知其几，北师之谋南者盖亦有数，而南北通和之时则绝无而仅有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283389_comment'></div>未闻有如今日之岌岌然以北方为可畏，以南方为可忧，一日不和则君臣上下朝不能以谋夕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283389_comment'></div>罪在于书生之不识形势，并与夫逆顺曲直而忘之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283389_comment'></div>高宗皇帝于虏有父兄之仇，生不能以报之，则死必有望于子孙，何忍以升遐之哀告诸仇哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1283389_comment'></div>遗留报谢，三使继遣，金帛宝货，千两连发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1283389_comment'></div>而虏人仅以一使如临小邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1283389_comment'></div>闻诸道路，哀祭之辞寂寥简慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1283389_comment'></div>义士仁人，痛切心骨，岂以陛下之圣明智勇而能忍之乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1283389_comment'></div>意者执事之臣忧思万端，有以误陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1283389_comment'></div>南方之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_55_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/160/Comments/0")'>红女</span>积尺寸之功于机杼，岁以输虏人，固已不胜其痛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1283389_comment'></div>金宝之出于山泽者有限，而轮诸虏人者无穷，十数年后，岂不遂就尽哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1283389_comment'></div>陛下何不翻然思首足之倒置，寻即位之初心，大泄而一用之，以与天下更始乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1283389_comment'></div>未闻以数千里之地而畏人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1283389_comment'></div>刘渊、石勒、石虎、苻坚，皆夷虏之雄，曾不能以终其世，而阿骨打之兴于今近八十年，中原涂炭又六十年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1283389_comment'></div>父子相夷之祸，具在眼中，而方畏其为南方之患，岂不误哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1283389_comment'></div>陛下倘以大义为当正，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/182/Comments/0")'>抚军</span>之言为可行，则当先经理建业，而后使临之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1283389_comment'></div>今之建业，非昔之建业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1283389_comment'></div>臣尝登石头钟阜而望今城，直在沙嘴之傍耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1283389_comment'></div>钟阜之支陇隐隐而下，今行宫据其平处以临城市，城之前则逼山而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_64_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/191/Comments/0")'>斗绝</span>焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1283389_comment'></div>此必后世之读山经而相宅者之所定，江南李氏之所为，非有据高临下以乘王气而用之之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1283389_comment'></div>本朝以至仁平天下，不恃险以为固，而与天下共守之，故因而不废耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1283389_comment'></div>臣尝问之钟阜之僧，亦能言<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/200/Comments/0")'>台城</span>在钟阜之侧，大司马门适当在今马军新营之傍耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1283389_comment'></div>其地据高临下，东环平冈以为固，西城石头以为重，带元武湖以为险，拥秦淮、清溪以为阻，是以王气可乘，而运动如意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1283389_comment'></div>若如今城，则费侯景数日之力耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1283389_comment'></div>曹彬之登长干，兀术之上雨花台，皆俯瞰城市，虽一飞鸟不能逃也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1283389_comment'></div>臣又尝问之守臣，以为今城不必改作，若上有北方之志，则此直寄路焉耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1283389_comment'></div>臣疑其言虽大，而实未切也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1283389_comment'></div>据其地而命将出师以谋中国，不使之乘王气而有为，虽省目前经营之劳，乌知其异日不垂得而复失哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1283389_comment'></div>纵今岁未为北举之谋，而为经理建业之计，以震动天下而与虏绝，陛下即位之初志亦庶几于少伸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1283389_comment'></div>第非常之事非可与常人谋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1283389_comment'></div>陛下即位之初，喜怒哀乐，是非好恶，皦然如日月之在天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1283389_comment'></div>雷动风行，天下方如草之偃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1283389_comment'></div>惟其或失之太快，故书生得拘文执法以议其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1283389_comment'></div>而其真有志者，私自奋励以求称圣意之所在，则陛下或未之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1283389_comment'></div>陛下见天下之士皆不足以望清光，而书生拘文执法之说往往有验，而圣意亦少衰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1283389_comment'></div>故大事必集议，除授必资格；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1283389_comment'></div>才者以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/246/Comments/0")'>跅弛</span>而弃，不才者以平稳而用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1283389_comment'></div>正言以迂阔而废，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/249/Comments/0")'>巽言</span>以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/249/Comments/1")'>软美</span>而入；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1283389_comment'></div>奇论指为横议，庸论谓有典则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1283389_comment'></div>陛下以雄心英略，委曲上下于其间，机会在前而不敢为翻然之喜，隐忍事仇而不敢奋赫斯之怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1283389_comment'></div>朝得一才士，而暮以当路不便而逐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1283389_comment'></div>心知为庸人，而外以人言不至而留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1283389_comment'></div>泯其喜怒哀乐，杂其是非好恶，而用依违以为仁，戒喻以为义，牢笼以为礼，关防以为智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1283389_comment'></div>陛下聪明自天，英武盖世，而何事出此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1283389_comment'></div>天下非有豪猾不可制之奸，虏人非有方兴未艾之势，而何必用此哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1283389_comment'></div>夫喜怒哀乐爱恶，人主之所以鼓动天下而用之之具也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1283389_comment'></div>而皇极之所谓无作者，不使加私意于其间耳，岂欲如老、庄所谓槁木死灰，与天下为婴儿，而后为至治之极哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1283389_comment'></div>陛下二十七年之间，遵养时晦，示天下以乐其有亲，而天下归其孝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1283389_comment'></div>行三年之丧，一诚不变，示天下以哀而从礼，而天下服其义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1283389_comment'></div>陛下以一身之哀乐而鼓天下以从之，其验如影响矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1283389_comment'></div>乙巳、丙午之间，虏人非无变故，而陛下不独不形诸喜，而亦不泄诸机密之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1283389_comment'></div>近者非常之变，虏人略于奉慰，而陛下不独不形诸怒，而亦不密其简慢之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1283389_comment'></div>陛下不以喜示天下，而天下恶知机会之可乘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1283389_comment'></div>陛下不以怒示天下，而天下恶知雠敌之不可安！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1283389_comment'></div>弃其喜怒以动天下之机，而欲事功之自成，是闭目而欲行也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1283389_comment'></div>小臣之得对，陛下有卓然知其才者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1283389_comment'></div>外臣之奉公，陛下有隐然念其忠者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1283389_comment'></div>而已用者旋去，既去者无路以自进，是陛下不得而示天下以爱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1283389_comment'></div>大臣之弄权，陛下既知其有塞路者，议人之多私，陛下既知其有罔我者，而去之惟恐伤其意，发之惟恐其怅恨而不满，是陛下不得而示天下以恶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1283389_comment'></div>陛下翻然思即位之初心，岂知其今日至此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1283389_comment'></div>臣犹为陛下怅念于既往，而天生英雄，岂使其终老于不济乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1283389_comment'></div>长江大河，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_107_1283389", 1283389, "Clauses/324/Comments/0")'>一泻千里</span>，苟得非常之人以共之，则电扫六合，非难致之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1283389_comment'></div>本朝以儒道治天下，以格律守天下，而天下之人知经义之为常程，科举之为正路，法不得自议其私，人不得自用其智，而二百年之太平由此而出也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1283389_comment'></div>至于艰难变故之际，书生之智，知议论之当正而不知事功之为何物，知节义之当守而不知形势之为何用，宛转于文法之中，而无一人能自拔者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1283389_comment'></div>陛下虽欲得非常之人以共斯世，而天下其谁肯信乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1283389_comment'></div>臣于戊戌之春正月丁巳，尝极论宗庙社稷大计，陛下亦慨然有感于其言，而卒不得一望清光，以布露其区区之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1283389_comment'></div>非廷臣之尽皆见恶，亦其势然耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1283389_comment'></div>臣今者非以其言之小验而再冒万死以自陈，实以宗庙社稷之大计不得不决于斯时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1283389_comment'></div>陛下用其喜怒哀乐爱恶之权以鼓动天下，使如臣者，得借方寸之地以终前书之所言，而附寸名于竹帛之间，不使邓禹笑人寂寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1283389_comment'></div>而陛下得以发其雄心英略，以与四海才臣智士共之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1283389_comment'></div>天生英雄，殆不偶然，而帝王自有真，非区区小智所可附会也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1283389_comment'></div>干冒天威，罪当万死。</div><div id='poem_sentence_117_1283389_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='98610d9a96374cc2a3253fb0eee7dc13_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("98610d9a96374cc2a3253fb0eee7dc13");'><span id='98610d9a96374cc2a3253fb0eee7dc13_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年5月</a>　夏五月乙巳，光宗策进士，擢为第一。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　廷对。作品：廷对。<span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157193")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_157193_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157193'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157193'>皇朝锐意急英贤，虏据中原七十年。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157193'>际遇风云凡事别，积功日月壮心愆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157193'>管箫器小谁能识，孔孟人存用则传。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157193_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157193'>惭负寿皇勤教育，奏篇半彻冕旒前。<div id='poem_title_157192' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157192?labeling=true' target='_blank'>及第谢恩和御赐诗韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span
