id='poem_title_157192_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157192'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157192'>云汉昭回倬<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_157192", 157192, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>锦章</span>，烂然衣被九天光。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157192'>已将德雨平分布，更把仁风与奉扬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157192'>治道脩明当正宁，皇威震叠到遐方。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157192'>复雠自是平生志，勿谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_157192", 157192, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>儒臣</span>鬓发苍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157192'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_157192_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　作皇帝正谢表。作品：皇帝正谢表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第71页。）</span><div id='poem_1283390' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283390' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283390?labeling=true' target='_blank'>皇帝正谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283390")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283390_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283390'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283390'>伏以天之生才，实系国家之造；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283390_comment'></div>人之用世，亦关时运之兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283390_comment'></div>济济朋来，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1283390", 1283390, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>班班</span>颖脱，以须选择，不使弃遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283390_comment'></div>臣亮等恭惟皇帝陛下以圣人之大才，行天下之正道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283390_comment'></div>韬英武于盛际，对《易》之《需》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283390_comment'></div>据君师之至尊，为《书》之《范》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283390_comment'></div>眷言问寝，重于复雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283390_comment'></div>固将与时以偕行，讵有抚机而不发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283390_comment'></div>安静和平之福，用以宅心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283390_comment'></div>发扬蹈厉之功，期于得士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283390_comment'></div>臣亮等仰知圣意，俯诵謏闻，本末后先，宁无失策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283390_comment'></div>短长高下，孰有遁情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283390_comment'></div>悉俟圣裁，尽从官使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283390_comment'></div>自今以始，宁敢窃爵禄以苟岁时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283390_comment'></div>如日之升，或可依风云而效尺寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283390_comment'></div>臣亮等下情无任激切营屏之至，谨奉表称谢以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1283390_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　作重华宫正谢表。作品：重华宫正谢表。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第71页。）</span><div id='poem_1283391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重华宫正谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283391")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283391'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283391'>伏以教育之功，易世乃见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283391_comment'></div>选抡之道，惟时是逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283391_comment'></div>虽三岁之故常，而一日之特异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283391_comment'></div>无非自献，盖有从来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283391_comment'></div>臣亮等恭惟寿皇圣帝陛下，对越在天，倦勤与子，以不世出之资而归之澹泊，以大有为之志而宅以和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283391_comment'></div>昔者论天下大计之小臣，亦尝动圣人隐忧之良会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283391_comment'></div>一时排摈，十五载之多奇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283391_comment'></div>末路遭逢，四百人之自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283391_comment'></div>共幸奋身于今日，独知回首于当年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283391_comment'></div>不肖姓名，再关天听；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283391_comment'></div>已输忠款，尽出圣谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283391_comment'></div>载惟精一之传，无非正大之实，设科取士，虽旧贯之尚仍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283391_comment'></div>陈力复雠，亦大义之难废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283391_comment'></div>共兹一毂，合彼众材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283391_comment'></div>付托得人，爰上唐家之寿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283391_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1283391", 1283391, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>陟降</span>在帝，孰知文后之声！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283391_comment'></div>臣亮等下情无任激切营屏之至，谨奉表称谢以闻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1283391_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　又谢留丞相启。作品：谢留丞相启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第71页。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　又谢葛丞相启。作品：谢葛丞相启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第71页。）</span><div id='poem_1283395' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283395' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283395?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢葛丞相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283395")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283395_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283395'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283395'>平生险阻，宁一事之称心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283395_comment'></div>晚节遭逢，当上圣之信目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283395_comment'></div>况更新于爰立，方共耸于具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283395_comment'></div>适丁斯时，当有甚幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283395_comment'></div>敬惟大丞相国公：山立玉峙，地负海涵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283395_comment'></div>才非求奇，贵其可用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283395_comment'></div>事去已甚，取其适宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283395_comment'></div>不自知其同心，宁更防于异己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283395_comment'></div>是非毁誉，肯概于胸中！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283395_comment'></div>小大短长，自安于度外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283395_comment'></div>虽斡旋之功每极其妙，而归宿之地卒底于平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283395_comment'></div>士守常心，物无觖望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283395_comment'></div>百年旧典，当渐见于施行；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283395_comment'></div>一日俊功，宜不忧于震动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283395_comment'></div>共赞朝廷之拔士，亦令草莽之逢时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283395_comment'></div>亮少不自量，谓功名差易耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283395_comment'></div>晚更多难，虽性命其如何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283395_comment'></div>忽从死灰之中，腾上烈焰之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283395_comment'></div>栽培倾覆，天亦何心！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283395_comment'></div>嘘枯吹生，人焉有助！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283395_comment'></div>猥以门墙之旧物，加之场屋之陈人，忍使白头尚作如新之态，当令赤手曾微直上之嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283395_comment'></div>为知己而狂言，亦无心于任运。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1283395_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　又谢赵同知启。作品：谢赵同知启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第72页。）</span><div id='poem_1283397' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283397' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283397?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赵同知启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283397")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283397_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283397'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283397'>汲引人才，使相先后；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283397_comment'></div>倏经时变，宁问短长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283397_comment'></div>但有向者之虚名，庶几今兹之实用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283397_comment'></div>滥叨首选，徒激壮心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283397_comment'></div>自源徂流，探端知绪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283397_comment'></div>敬惟同知相公：蚤以文墨，自结主知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283397_comment'></div>出其才猷，遂为世用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283397_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1283397", 1283397, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>践更</span>多矣，声问伟然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283397_comment'></div>北向以复神州，固有无前之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283397_comment'></div>中立而行正道，姑从端本之谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283397_comment'></div>英流冀其相先，善类依以为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283397_comment'></div>公辅雅望，上所属心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283397_comment'></div>宥密本衷，国焉惟屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283397_comment'></div>官则见舜朝之逊，贤岂容尧野之遗！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283397_comment'></div>念昔少年，及见前辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283397_comment'></div>素所自喜，《兵法》《六韬》；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283397_comment'></div>已而饫闻，《中庸》、《大学》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283397_comment'></div>坐想百年之旧，疾趋一世之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283397_comment'></div>荏苒岁时，牵连祸患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283397_comment'></div>人皆欲杀，付微命于鸿毛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283397_comment'></div>公不我遗，脱残年于虎口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283397_comment'></div>况遇持于文柄，欲稍复于古初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283397_comment'></div>舍其旧而新是图，望之大而小可略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283397_comment'></div>使膺清问，尽致公言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283397_comment'></div>上亦念其论之平，竟以先此时之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283397_comment'></div>愿当圣世，合天下之异以为同；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283397_comment'></div>岂无厉阶，非斯人之徒而谁与！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283397_comment'></div>鼓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1283397", 1283397, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>同舟遇风</span>之势，成披云睹日之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283397_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1283397", 1283397, "Clauses/57/Comments/0")'>出尖</span>之才，百端并用；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283397_comment'></div>易世之怨，一洗而空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283397_comment'></div>伊我何心，惟公是望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283397_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1283397_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　又谢罗尚书启。作品：谢罗尚书启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第72页。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　谢曾察院启。作品：谢曾察院启。<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见童振福《陈亮年谱》第72页。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　谢陈参政启。<div id='poem_1283396' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283396' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283396?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢陈参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283396")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283396'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283396'>暮景<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1283396", 1283396, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>生涯</span>，恍如落日；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283396_comment'></div>少年梦事，旋若好风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283396_comment'></div>方大贤共秉国钧之时，而一介乃有遽掩时流之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283396_comment'></div>老之将至，人其谓何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283396_comment'></div>敬惟参政相公，究力古书，潜心正学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283396_comment'></div>质而有韵，判一言父子之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283396_comment'></div>博以逢原，当千载君臣之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283396_comment'></div>是膺大任，以展良图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283396_comment'></div>四海群贤，争先<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1283396", 1283396, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>攀附</span>；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283396_comment'></div>百年旧典，次第施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283396_comment'></div>方皇家陈善以闭邪，使天下回心而向道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283396_comment'></div>弥纶所至，不阙毫釐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283396_comment'></div>汲引而来，咸展尺寸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283396_comment'></div>萌新芽于枯木，燃烈焰于死灰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283396_comment'></div>亮祸患之馀，心志凋落；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283396_comment'></div>尘埃之底，笔墨荒疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283396_comment'></div>独有丹心，不渝白首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283396_comment'></div>自牗纳约，于焉开明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283396_comment'></div>盈缶有孚，所以发志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283396_comment'></div>不学近名之直，亦微慕利之谀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283396_comment'></div>上于二三之中，擢在第一之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283396_comment'></div>圣恩深厚，固非臣下所能知；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283396_comment'></div>众口会同，夫岂志力所可及！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283396_comment'></div>自天有命，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1283396", 1283396, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>无地自容</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283396_comment'></div>音韵琅琅，徒累巨公之读；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283396_comment'></div>风期隐隐，式关上哲之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283396_comment'></div>略转洪钧，悉成通路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283396_comment'></div>过此以往，未知所裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1283396_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　谢张侍御启。<div id='poem_1283400' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283400' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283400?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢张侍御启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283400")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283400_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283400'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283400'>主持公论，意独在于朴忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283400_comment'></div>叶正上心，理难施于巧智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283400_comment'></div>虽或从于亲擢，本亦备于先登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283400_comment'></div>推其闿端，何以论报！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283400_comment'></div>伏念亮脱身虎口，久矣讳穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283400_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1283400", 1283400, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>批逆龙鳞</span>，期于合理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283400_comment'></div>庶几一割之有用，安能百鍊而愈刚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283400_comment'></div>竞短争长，无复此梦：分多共少，冀度残生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283400_comment'></div>白首骎骎，丹心隐隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283400_comment'></div>言在此而意在彼，问之显而答之微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283400_comment'></div>第其度程，亦在<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1283400", 1283400, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>二三</span>之数；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283400_comment'></div>决于旒扆，竟成第一之传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283400_comment'></div>辱此误知，光夫末路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283400_comment'></div>此盖伏遇侍御执事，英姿沈毅，伟量洪深；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283400_comment'></div>国典朝章，固盛时之所习见；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283400_comment'></div>世科士版，亦素宦之所具宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283400_comment'></div>腾此英声，成夫厚德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283400_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1283400", 1283400, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>风宪</span>之地，执守是先；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283400_comment'></div>才智之渊，选抡不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283400_comment'></div>欲使从风而靡，要当如日之升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283400_comment'></div>献言因恶于近谀，矫枉亦防于过直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283400_comment'></div>少年勇决，记追逐于英游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283400_comment'></div>暮景安详，务归尊于独智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283400_comment'></div>并心一向，图补万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283400_comment'></div>正学以言，及明时而自献；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283400_comment'></div>导人使谏，开大义以相先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283400_comment'></div>公所欲为，谁敢不应！</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1283400_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　谢黄正言启。<div id='poem_1283401' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283401' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283401?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢黄正言启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283401")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283401_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283401'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283401'>文律持平，岂遽分于人品；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283401_comment'></div>论衡求是，亦务当于物情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283401_comment'></div>累藻鉴之至明，成冕旒之小误。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283401_comment'></div>足光晚景，以动壮怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283401_comment'></div>伏念亮剽锐何如，蹉跎至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283401_comment'></div>置身无所，方念昔非；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283401_comment'></div>回首亦疑，未知孰是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283401_comment'></div>岂有圣贤之学，乃为世俗所憎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283401_comment'></div>殆非其人，以招此祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283401_comment'></div>暮年前却，私窃自怜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283401_comment'></div>寸晷短长，虽争何用！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283401_comment'></div>遇执至公之柄，肯收近拙之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283401_comment'></div>使对大廷，褎然亲擢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283401_comment'></div>误先众隽，翕若诵言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283401_comment'></div>非出人谋，悉从天定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283401_comment'></div>此盖伏遇正言执事，英姿挺特，德性静渊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283401_comment'></div>学有源流，诚不惭于游夏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283401_comment'></div>文出机杼，盖取则于孟韩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283401_comment'></div>固非尧野之肯遗，抑亦汉庭之未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283401_comment'></div>竟从王邸，收备谏工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283401_comment'></div>遇事风生，辈流退缩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283401_comment'></div>责难山立，左右惊嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283401_comment'></div>持此血诚，效夫心膂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283401_comment'></div>不遗馀力，曲致弥缝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283401_comment'></div>犹有后忧，敢忘汲引！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283401_comment'></div>故虽某辈，亦及今兹，岂徒尔而激昂，盖闻之而兴起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283401_comment'></div>合天下为一体，非此为则彼为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283401_comment'></div>极治道无两端，苟君美而身美。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1283401_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　谢章司谏启。<div id='poem_1283402' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283402' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283402?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢章司谏启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283402")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283402_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283402'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283402'>讳穷久矣，世宁保其必遭！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283402_comment'></div>自视歉然，人岂容于彊附！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283402_comment'></div>苟不愧君子之论，斯足对上圣之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283402_comment'></div>赖此品题，几于遇合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283402_comment'></div>伏念某脱身虎口，欲求护命之符；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283402_comment'></div>妄意鸿冥，莫得游仙之枕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283402_comment'></div>进退不知所据，往来徒自于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283402_comment'></div>眷一试之随群，盖百思而无策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283402_comment'></div>庶其在此，不堪暮景之怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283402_comment'></div>幸而得之，敢作少年之爱！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283402_comment'></div>入当大对，曲尽寸心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283402_comment'></div>问所不该，言岂容于越次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283402_comment'></div>意虽独至，事亦谨于闿端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283402_comment'></div>故此区区，发其耿耿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283402_comment'></div>有司之所不快，越在二三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283402_comment'></div>当宁以为无他，俄从第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283402_comment'></div>侥倖至此，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1283402", 1283402, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>称塞</span>若何！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283402_comment'></div>此盖伏遇司谏执事，貌粹骨奇，神清气劲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283402_comment'></div>学传正派，以百圣为准绳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283402_comment'></div>文擅古风，以两汉为机杼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283402_comment'></div>鼓行场屋而无其对，惊动缙绅而为之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283402_comment'></div>岂止嘉猷足善王邸，遂膺睿眷以备谏工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283402_comment'></div>知无不言，成非所计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283402_comment'></div>海内人物，固自如林，古来忠诚，亦应有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283402_comment'></div>牵连咸在，汲引而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283402_comment'></div>识别分明，不虑人心之异，诸凡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1283402", 1283402, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>魁垒</span>，亦惟门下之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283402_comment'></div>上诚得人，公必知我。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1283402_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年6月11日</a>　谢杨解元启。<div id='poem_1283403' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283403' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283403?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢杨解元启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年6月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283403")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283403_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283403'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283403'>决得失于数人之目，有命者类能得之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283403_comment'></div>同毁誉于万口之辞，怀才者始克称此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283403_comment'></div>眷一时之偶幸，矧群议之喟然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283403_comment'></div>感惠有繇，抚躬知愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283403_comment'></div>窃以求贤而下间岁之诏，国有常经；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283403_comment'></div>糊名而收一日之长，士多苟得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283403_comment'></div>立制莫踰于今密，得人无复于古如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283403_comment'></div>盖昔者相知以心，此心达而此士至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283403_comment'></div>而后世相持以法，一法立而一弊生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283403_comment'></div>程度愈谨而豪杰之气渐以拘，禁防益密而旷达之人遭其辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283403_comment'></div>顾积弊之至此，岂创法之所期！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283403_comment'></div>故<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1283403", 1283403, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>庙朝</span>徒叹于乏才，而川泽岂闻于遗士！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283403_comment'></div>虽十九之乖意，庶千一之有人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283403_comment'></div>如某者才本不羁，誉俄过实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283403_comment'></div>虽本诸公之浪听，卒为十目之不容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283403_comment'></div>盖才者争之端，据其端而争日至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283403_comment'></div>而名者忌之府，趋其府而忌群兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283403_comment'></div>人其奈何，天亦随罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283403_comment'></div>忧患百罹而未艾，惊惶万状而莫支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283403_comment'></div>既荣辱之两忘，亦得丧之一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283403_comment'></div>一若龙而一若虎，习且不能；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283403_comment'></div>呼我马而呼我牛，惟其所谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283403_comment'></div>已分息心于世故，岂期获玷于贤书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283403_comment'></div>顾脱俗之无阶，谩随人而求举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283403_comment'></div>望不及此，得之若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283403_comment'></div>此盖伏遇判府先生，以恢廓之资，充硕大之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283403_comment'></div>百年忠骨，尚观慷慨之遗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283403_comment'></div>奕世义门，犹识薰陶之自。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283403_comment'></div>清望骤膺于圣眷，长才或耸于朝班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283403_comment'></div>入为持橐之华，出拥分符之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283403_comment'></div>狱讼日简，教化浸行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283403_comment'></div>致此无庸，亦叨首荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283403_comment'></div>某敢不勉其不逮，听以无心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283403_comment'></div>瓦注者巧而金注者惛，本何所系；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283403_comment'></div>适矢复沓而方矢复寓，庶造其精。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1283403_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　六月十一日，寿罗春伯作《瑞云浓慢》词。（蔗浆酪粉）<div id='poem_157268' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157268' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157268?labeling=true' target='_blank'>瑞云浓慢 六月十一日寿罗春伯</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157268")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157268_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157268'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157268'>蔗浆酪粉，玉壶冰醑，朝罢更闻宣赐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157268'>去天咫尺，下拜再三，幸今有母可遗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157268'>年年此日，共道是、月入怀中最贵。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157268'>向暑天，正风云会遇，有恁嘉瑞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157268_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157268'>鹤冲霄，鱼得水。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157268'>一超便、直入神仙地。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157268'>植根江表，开拓两河，做得黑头公未。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157268'>骑鲸赤手，问如何、长鞭尺箠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_157268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_157268'>算向来、数王谢风流，只今管是。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_157268_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年7月</a>　秋七月，授建康军节度判官厅公事。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
金华
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c93a29d4fab94567b95487825b0bc5bc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c93a29d4fab94567b95487825b0bc5bc");'><span id='c93a29d4fab94567b95487825b0bc5bc_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1172&endYear=1172')">1172年2月</a>　春二月，吕祖谦之父卒，亲赴金华吊唁，有祭文。作品：祭吕治先郎中文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（颜虚心《宋陈龙川先生亮年谱》第35页。）</span><div id='poem_1283719' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283719' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283719?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭吕治先郎中文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1172年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283719")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283719_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283719'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283719'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283719_comment'></div>公以东北世家之贤，来寓吾邦，是生贤子，以淑一邦之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283719_comment'></div>位不究其所蕴，而奄焉以没，使其贤子号天叫地，如不欲生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283719_comment'></div>西乡稽颡，以受一邦之吊，其为可哀，盖不论乎知公之与否也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283719_comment'></div>亮以晚生，不及拜公于堂，间获从公之子以游，诱之掖之，盖公之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283719_comment'></div>则今日之俯伏道傍，举觞一恸者，诚未敢径自附于知生之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283719_comment'></div>孰信而来，孰屈而往？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283719_comment'></div>此心昭然，庶几其飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1283719_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='4f4748b302b842b2988a8bc0d35ae2b2_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1181&endYear=1181')">1181年8月2日</a>　吕祖谦七月二十九日癸卯卒，越四日丙午，陈亮赴金华哭之。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
兰溪
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='abe246f2d3df4ca099b33c8ec492f521_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("abe246f2d3df4ca099b33c8ec492f521");'><span id='abe246f2d3df4ca099b33c8ec492f521_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1176&endYear=1176')">1176年</a>　会吕伯恭于长乐。行李至自永嘉。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4a8ea29a68d64036b77880e8a8a06ee8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4a8ea29a68d64036b77880e8a8a06ee8");'><span id='4a8ea29a68d64036b77880e8a8a06ee8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　和吴允成游灵洞韵，作《水调歌头》。吴竽（允成）于淳熙十一年至十三年任永康尉，该词当作于其间，附于此。（人爱新来景）<div id='poem_157216' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157216' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157216?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水调歌头 和吴允成游灵洞韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157216")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157216_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157216'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157216'>人爱新来景，龙认旧时湫。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157216'>不论三伏，小住便觉凛生秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157216'>我自醉眠其上，任是水流其下，湍激若为收。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157216'>世事如斯去，不去为谁留。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157216_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157216'>料得神仙窟穴，争似提封万里，大小几琉球。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157216_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157216'>但有君才具，何用问时流。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157216_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
温州（永嘉）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='cb493d2dccf7422cbe8c15376875aa41_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cb493d2dccf7422cbe8c15376875aa41");'><span id='cb493d2dccf7422cbe8c15376875aa41_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>，38岁</div><div id='cb493d2dccf7422cbe8c15376875aa41' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1180&endYear=1180')">1180年</a>　秋，有永嘉之行，与陈傅良、叶适等相聚论学，归时，诸子相饯，作《南乡子》致谢。（人物满东瓯）<div id='poem_157233' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157233' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157233?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南乡子 谢永嘉诸友相饯</a><span class='authorDate'>（1180年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157233")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157233_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157233'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157233'>人物满东瓯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157233'>别我江心识俊游。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157233'>北尽平芜南似画，中流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157233'>谁系龙骧万斛舟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157233_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157233'>去去几时休。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157233'>犹自潮来更上头。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157233'>醉墨淋漓人感旧，离愁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157233_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157233'>一夜西风似夏不。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157233_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
镇江（丹徒）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7fa2786051164f8881c6aedbaac55674_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7fa2786051164f8881c6aedbaac55674");'><span id='7fa2786051164f8881c6aedbaac55674_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1189&endYear=1189')">1189年</a>，47岁</div><div id='fbf7dfffad094d87981bbfe68d0c60ab' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>六月，往哭石天民。此行在京口购得屋子。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>登多景楼，作《念奴娇》（危楼还望）<span class='inlineComment2'>（姜书阁认为该词与《念奴娇》（江南春色）作于同一年，参见《陈亮龙川词笺注》第41页。）</span><div id='poem_157228' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157228' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157228?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇 登多景楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157228")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157228_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157228'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157228'>危楼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_157228", 157228, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>还望</span>，叹此意，今古几人曾会。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157228'>鬼设神施，浑认作、天限南疆北界。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157228'>一水横陈，连冈三面，做出争雄势。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157228'>六朝何事，只成门户私计。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157228_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157228'>因笑王谢诸人，登高怀远，也学英雄涕。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157228'>凭却江山管不到，河洛腥膻无际。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157228'>正好长驱，不须反顾，寻取中流誓。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157228'>小儿破贼，势成宁问彊对。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_157228'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(157228)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dd8aa9b324184b8a978bd75484aa664c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dd8aa9b324184b8a978bd75484aa664c");'><span id='dd8aa9b324184b8a978bd75484aa664c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>，50岁</div><div id='dd8aa9b324184b8a978bd75484aa664c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　避宅京口。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年4月</a>　春四月，永嘉郑伯英卒，为文以祭之。作品：祭郑景元提干文。<div id='poem_1283730' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283730' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283730?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭郑景元提干文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283730")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283730_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283730'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283730'>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283730_comment'></div>奇才异能，世资以为用，则何患于无路？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283730_comment'></div>高科显第，人资以自达，则何患于无时？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283730_comment'></div>兄弟炳乎其相辉，则何向不可恃？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283730_comment'></div>朋友蔚乎其相扶，则何志不可施？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283730_comment'></div>世惟恐无一焉于其间，又安得合四者而有之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283730_comment'></div>寿踰六十，非人命之难期；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283730_comment'></div>年历三纪，非世道之难移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283730_comment'></div>如兄之止于此，亦理之未易推。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283730_comment'></div>昔吾以兄为自锢，得非同病而后知？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283730_comment'></div>庙论亦察其不可，宪属且先其至微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283730_comment'></div>后发先至，为骏马之良；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283730_comment'></div>豫章手植，非老人所宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283730_comment'></div>兄为慨然：「何择于斯！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283730_comment'></div>亦既至此，安于『已而」』。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283730_comment'></div>我曰：「焉得，以身自私，人之职分，岂容或亏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283730_comment'></div>天不我与，甘之若饴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283730_comment'></div>有命不承，宁问崇卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283730_comment'></div>不登坡垄，安陟崔嵬？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283730_comment'></div>身在一日，吾将何辞」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283730_comment'></div>兄念：「孔圣，犹曰『吾衰』，不如适意，与天同归」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283730_comment'></div>「我困囚系，死生毫釐，尚欲于中，仰首伸眉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283730_comment'></div>一归之天，何以我为」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283730_comment'></div>往来应酬，各有据依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283730_comment'></div>此论未终，冀兄生疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283730_comment'></div>旬月之间，寂无一词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283730_comment'></div>棘寺逮我，方堕危机，手染报兄：「累卵之危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283730_comment'></div>兄必有策，免我庶几」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283730_comment'></div>缄题之回，望之则非：夜半负舟，疾走莫追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283730_comment'></div>弃我任我，幽明异歧！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283730_comment'></div>我亦漠然，甘与世违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283730_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283730_comment'></div>兄之文章，有源有委，兄之议论，有纲有纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283730_comment'></div>兄之行事，有张有弛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283730_comment'></div>兄之与人，有同有异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283730_comment'></div>取之不竭，有本如是，道德性命，此外何事！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283730_comment'></div>昔者难兄，既知之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283730_comment'></div>枯木死灰，去死宁几！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283730_comment'></div>人固活物，日出事起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283730_comment'></div>强恕而行，不偏不陂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283730_comment'></div>名教之中，自有乐地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283730_comment'></div>死生祸福，不阿不避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283730_comment'></div>天地之性，以人为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1283730_comment'></div>圣以此圣，礼安得伪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1283730_comment'></div>仁以此仁，义安得外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1283730_comment'></div>是中只有，离伦拔萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1283730_comment'></div>求异于人，则匪人类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1283730_comment'></div>振古如兹，始乎为士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1283730_comment'></div>异时冀兄，并驱而至，兄既长往，我存曷以！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1283730_comment'></div>天长地久，盈眶之泪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1283730_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　撰姚唐佐墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>姚唐佐墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283697")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283697'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283697'>君姓姚氏，讳汝贤，字唐佐，世居婺之永康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283697_comment'></div>曾祖坎，祖孜，父源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283697_comment'></div>君平生衣食粗足，不为后日计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283697_comment'></div>乐易好善，不求闻于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283697_comment'></div>教其子以学，而不冀其必成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283697_comment'></div>优游卒岁，盖适其真以生死者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283697_comment'></div>娶沈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283697_comment'></div>子男一人，怡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283697_comment'></div>怡为太学诸生，无所遇而死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283697_comment'></div>君哀之，越二年亦死，盖绍熙壬子八月六日，得年七十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283697_comment'></div>孙瑀甫冠，而两丧停之屋下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283697_comment'></div>怡之友林君大中、徐君木，伤其穷之至此也，于是林方入台为侍御史，不能必顾其私，命其弟大任相徐举义以葬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283697_comment'></div>而楼君城、徐君总、陈君志同与夏贡士师尹，和之尤力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283697_comment'></div>龙川陈亮尝入太学，于怡为同舍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283697_comment'></div>吴东阳竽，旧尉永康而善怡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283697_comment'></div>某施文，吴亦施字，以成诸君之盛举，使知风义不泯，薄俗尚有激也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283697_comment'></div>圣明在上，风化尚可考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283697_comment'></div>其地为承训乡马义原，其举为绍熙壬子十有二月丙午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283697_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1283697'>失其子以及其身，世固有途穷之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283697_comment'></div>死于孙之手而归骨于其子之友，法犹谓之有后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283697_comment'></div>吾将各举畚土于新阡之上，以观造物之处此壤也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1283697_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>　撰喻夏卿墓志铭。<div id='poem_1283695' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1283695' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1283695?labeling=true' target='_blank'>喻夏卿墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_1283695")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1283695_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1283695'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1283695'>淳熙庚子，义乌喻夏卿改葬其内王夫人于邑之智者乡雷公山之下，问铭于永康陈亮，盖尝叙夏卿夫妇之懿矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1283695_comment'></div>夏卿教其子孙，皆兴于学，所能自见，而多屈于春官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1283695_comment'></div>绍熙辛亥，夏卿年且九十有一，一日从容置酒语其弟侄辈曰：「群儿及今举自奋，老夫犹可待也，过是则已矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1283695_comment'></div>又曰：「我死，非陈子莫铭我也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1283695_comment'></div>怅然凝伫者久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1283695_comment'></div>未几而八月十有九日，夏卿死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1283695_comment'></div>余犹系三衢狱中，微若闻之，则为之出涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1283695_comment'></div>明年二月出狱，则往哭焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1283695_comment'></div>九月，其子义方、民献哭投余门以其先君行实，曰：「我父实求属于子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1283695_comment'></div>子知吾父者，其肯死吾父乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1283695_comment'></div>亮曰：「诺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1283695_comment'></div>昔孟子有取于「为仁不富」之论，而世俗之常言曰：「慈不主兵，义不主财」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1283695_comment'></div>其说遂以行，而闾巷之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1283695", 1283695, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>奸夫</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1283695", 1283695, "Clauses/38/Comments/1")'>猾子</span>借是以成其家，虽见鄙于清论，见绳于公法，而人乐其生得以自资，终不为之变也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1283695_comment'></div>夏卿孝友慈爱，根于天性，而著见于日用之间，如饮食之不可废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1283695_comment'></div>中年与其侄分田，不过百三十亩，卒亦几至于千亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1283695_comment'></div>然而友爱子侄，而计较秋毫之心不萌焉；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1283695_comment'></div>慈恤里闾，而豪夺力取之事不行焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1283695_comment'></div>「为仁不富」之论，盖至夏卿而废矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1283695_comment'></div>晚虽家事不如初，而亲戚故旧之急难，族人子弟之美事，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1283695", 1283695, "Clauses/59/Comments/0")'>爱莫之助</span>，每致其惓惓之意，而人人常信之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1283695_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1283695_comment'></div>为夏卿者，亦可以无憾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1283695_comment'></div>福寿康宁，子孙彬彬然皆有可观者，天于夏卿，亦何所负哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1283695_comment'></div>喻氏著籍蜀之仙井，散在浙江者惟义乌为盛，亦尝有列于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1283695_comment'></div>曾祖讳迂，祖讳宗，父讳登。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1283695_comment'></div>夏卿讳师，字夏卿，遇太上皇后庆寿，覃恩封迪功郎，及高宗再上万寿，加封脩职郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1283695_comment'></div>子男四人：义方，脩职郎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1283695_comment'></div>大方，早夭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1283695_comment'></div>知方，汝方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1283695_comment'></div>女二人，适商克忠、赵悌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1283695_comment'></div>孙男九人：侃、宪、演、湮、淡、克、充、宽、竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1283695_comment'></div>孙女八人：嫁杨一之、蒋若拙、陈某、赵某、许公升、傅某、赵某，而公升新与计偕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1283695_comment'></div>幼未行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1283695_comment'></div>曾孙男女合十六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1283695_comment'></div>汝方今名民献，与侃入太学为诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1283695_comment'></div>演尝举于乡；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1283695_comment'></div>而侃今再以姓名上礼部，即前志所谓宏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1283695_comment'></div>义方将以十一月三日壬申合葬，而亮实铭之曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1283695'>少年虑事出人意表，至于危疑之际，为人剖析无留难，而积善之报未尝泯也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1283695_comment'></div>晚岁百事不以关心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1283695_comment'></div>至于园池之间，婆娑游嬉无虚日，而释老之书未尝问也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1283695_comment'></div>乡之善士，卒为老成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1283695_comment'></div>言无枝叶，行有准绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1283695_comment'></div>空其一乡，丧此持平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1283695_comment'></div>孰昭斯铭，以淑我后生！</div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1283695_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绍兴（会稽）
-----detail

-----title
铅山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f7ec0cf5daea4425a7265bb296f5078c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f7ec0cf5daea4425a7265bb296f5078c");'><span id='f7ec0cf5daea4425a7265bb296f5078c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>，46岁</div><div id='f7ec0cf5daea4425a7265bb296f5078c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1188&endYear=1188')">1188年</a>　冬，携辛弃疾同游鹅湖，会朱熹于紫溪，仿乙未鹅湖故事。朱熹不至，有《贺新郎》词寄和稼轩。（老去凭谁说）<span class='inlineComment2'>（参见姜书阁《陈亮龙川词笺注》第45页。）</span><div id='poem_157252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺新郎 寄辛幼安和见怀韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1188年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157252")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157252'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157252'>老去凭谁说。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157252'>看几番、神奇臭腐，夏裘冬葛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157252'>父老长安今馀几，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_157252", 157252, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>后死</span>无雠可雪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157252'>犹未燥、当时生发。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157252'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_157252", 157252, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>二十五弦</span>多少恨，算世间、那有平分月。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157252'>胡妇弄，汉宫瑟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157252_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157252'>树犹如此堪重别。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157252'>只使君、从来与我，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_157252", 157252, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>话头</span>多合。<div id='poem_sentence_7_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_157252'>行矣置之无足问，谁换妍皮痴骨。<div id='poem_sentence_8_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_157252'>但莫使、伯牙弦绝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_157252'>九转丹砂牢拾取，管精金、只是寻常铁。<div id='poem_sentence_10_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_157252'>龙共虎，应声裂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_157252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_157252'><a href='javascript: -----end



-----title
南京（建康府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='deaa1c8769c141319a814f0b11ede898_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("deaa1c8769c141319a814f0b11ede898");'><span id='deaa1c8769c141319a814f0b11ede898_link' style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>初夏至金陵，晤章德茂。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>作《念奴娇》词纪金陵。（江南春色）<span class='inlineComment2'>（一说《念奴娇》（江南春色）作于淳熙十五年（1188），参见姜书阁《陈亮龙川词笺注》第36页。）</span><div id='poem_157226' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_157226' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/157226?labeling=true' target='_blank'>念奴娇 至金陵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1189年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34547, "南宋", "陈亮", "poem_title_157226")'>陈亮</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_157226_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_157226'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_157226'>江南春色，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_157226", 157226, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>算来</span>是，多少胜游清赏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_157226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_157226'>妖冶廉纤，只做得、飞鸟向人偎傍。<div id='poem_sentence_1_157226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_157226'>地辟天开，精神朗慧，到底还<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_157226", 157226, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>京样</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_157226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_157226'>人家<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_157226", 157226, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>小语</span>，一声声近清唱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_157226_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_157226'>因念旧日山城，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_157226", 157226, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>个人</span>如画，已作中州想。<div id='poem_sentence_4_157226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_157226'>邓禹笑人无限也，冷落不堪惆怅。<div id='poem_sentence_5_157226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_157226'>秋水双明，高山一弄，著我些悲壮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_157226_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_157226'>南徐好住，片帆有分来往。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_157226_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
